      <li>Unganidzirai vatsvene vangu kwandiri; Ivo vakaita sungano neni nezvibayiro.</li>
      <li>Kudenga-denga kunodudzira kururama kwake; Nokuti Mwari ndiye mutongi amene.</li>
      <li>Inzwai vanhu vangu, ndichataura; Imi Isiraeri, ndichakupupurirai, Ndini Mwari, iye Mwari wenyu.</li>
      <li>Handingakutukiyi pamusoro pezvibayiro zvenyu; Zvipiriso zvenyu zvinopiswa zviri pamberi pangu nguva dzose.</li>
      <li>Handingatori nzombe paimba yako, Kana nhongo dzembudzi pazvirugu zvako.</li>
      <li>Nokuti mhuka dzose, dziri kudondo, ndedzangu, Nemombe pamakomo ane chiuru chamazana.</li>
      <li>Ndinoziva shiri dzose dzomumakomo; Mhuka dzose, dziri musango, ndedzangu.</li>
      <li>Kana ndaiva nenzara, handizaikuudza iwe; Nokuti nyika ndeyangu, nezvaizere nazvo.</li>
      <li>Ko ndingadya nyama yehando, Kana kunwa ropa rembudzi here?</li>
      <li>Bayirai Mwari zvibayiro zvokuvonga; Uripire Wokumusorosoro mhiko dzako;</li>
      <li>Udane kwandiri pazuva rokutambudzika; Ini ndichakurwira, iwe ugondirumbidza.</li>
      <li>Asi kuneakaipa Jehovha anoti, Iwe ungadudzira seiko zvandakatema, Nokureva sungano yangu nomuromo wako?</li>
      <li>Zvaunovenga kurairwa, Nokurasha mashoko angu shure kwako.</li>
      <li>Wakati uchiona mbavha, ukafarirana nayo, Unoshamwaridzana nemhombwe.</li>
      <li>Unotendera muromo wako kureva zvakaipa, Rurimi rwako runotaura nhema.</li>
      <li>Unogara uchipomera hama yako; Unoita makuhwa pamusoro pomwanakomana wamai vako.</li>
      <li>Zvinhu izvi wakazviita, ndikaramba ndinyerere; Wakafunga kuti ini ndakafanana newe chose; Asi ndichakuraira, ndichirongedzera zvinhu izvi pameso ako.</li>
      <li>Zvino fungai chinhu ichi, imi vokukanganwa Mwari, Ndirege kukubvamburai, mukashaiwa murwiri,</li>
      <li>Munhu, anobayira chibayiro chokuvonga, unondikudza; Uye anogadzira nzira yake zvakanaka Ndichamuratidza kuponesa kwaMwari.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndinzwirei tsitsi, Mwari nokuda kwounyoro hwenyu; Dzimai kudarika kwangu nokuda kwengoni dzenyu zhinji.</li>
      <li>Ndisukei zvakaipa zvangu chose, Ndinatsei chivi changu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndinoziva kudarika kwangu; Chivi changu chinogara chiri pamberi pangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakakutadzirai imi, iyemi moga, Ndakaita chinhu chakaipa pamberi penyu; Kuti munzi makarurama pakutaura kwenyu, Muve usina mhosva pakutonga kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, ndakaberekerwa muzvakaipa; Mai vangu vakandigamuchira muzvivi.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, munoda zvokwadi pamoyo; Munoda kundidzidzisa uchenjeri mukati makavanda.</li>
      <li>Ndinatsei nehisopi, ndive akanaka, Ndishambidzei, ndichene kupfuura mazayi echando.</li>
      <li>Ndinzwisei mufaro ndive nomoyo muchena; Kuti mapfupa amakavhuna afare.</li>
      <li>Vanzirai zvivi zvangu chiso chenyu, Dzimai zvakaipa zvangu zvose.</li>
      <li>Sikai mukati mangu moyo wakachena, Mwari; Vandudzai mukati mangu mweya wakarurama.</li>
      <li>Regai kundirasha pamberi penyu; Musabvisa mweya wenyu mutsvene kwandiri.</li>
      <li>Dzoseraizve kwandiri mufaro wokuponesa kwenyu; Nditsigirei nomweya, unoda.</li>
      <li>Ipapo ndichadzidzisa vadariki nzira dzenyu; Uye vatadzi vachatendeukira kwamuri.</li>
      <li>Ndirwirei pamhosva yeropa, Mwari, imi Mwari muponesi wangu; Ipapo rurimi rwangu ruchaimbira kururama kwenyu kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Ishe, zarurai miromo yangu; Ipapo muromo wangu uchaparidza kurumbidzwa kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi hamufariri zvibayiro; ndingadai ndaikupai izvo; Hamufadzwi nechipiriso chinopiswa.</li>
      <li>Zvibayiro zvaMwari mweya wakaputsika; moyo wakaputsika nowakapwanyika, imi Mwari hamungaushori.</li>
      <li>Itirai Ziyoni zvakanaka nokuda kwenyu; Vakai masvingo eJerusaremu.</li>
      <li>Ipapo muchafarira zvibayiro zvakarurama, nechipiriso chinopiswa nechipiriso chinopiswa chose; Ipapo vachabayira nzombe paaritari yenyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Unozvirumbidzireiko nezvakashata, iwe mhare? Tsitsi dzaMwari dziripo misi yose.</li>
      <li>Rurimi rwako runofunga kutaura zvakaipa; Rwakafanana nechisvo chinopinza, ruchiita zvinonyengera.</li>
      <li>Unoda zvakaipa kupfuura zvakanaka; Nokureva nhema kupfuura kutaura zvakarurama.</li>
      <li>Unoda mashoko ose okuparadza, Iwe rurimi runonyengera.</li>
      <li>Mwari achakuparadzawo saizvozvo nokusingaperi, Achakubata akakubvisa patende rako, nokukudzura panyika yavapenyu.</li>
      <li>Vakarurama vachazviona vakatya, Vachamuseka, vachiti,</li>
      <li>Tarirai, hoyu munhu asina kuita Mwari nhare yake, Asi akavimba nokuwanda kwefuma yake, Akazvisimbisa pazvakaipa zvake.</li>
      <li>Asi kana ndirini, ndakafanana nomuorivhi munyoro muimba yaMwari; Ndinovimba netsitsi dzaMwari nokusingaperi-peri.</li>
      <li>Ndichakuvongai nokusingaperi, nokuti ndimi makazviita; Ndichamirira zita renyu pamberi pavatsvene venyu nokuti rakanaka.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Benzi rakati mumoyo maro, Mwari hakuna . Vakaora, vakaita zvakaipa zvinonyangadza; Hakuna anoita zvakanaka.</li>
      <li>Mwari, ari kudenga, wakatarira pasi kuvana vavanhu, Kuti aone kana akachenjera aripo, Anotsvaka Mwari.</li>
      <li>Mumwe nomumwe wavo akadzokera shure; vakasvibiswa pamwechete; Hakuna anoita zvakanaka, kunyange nomumwe.</li>
      <li>Ko vaiti vezvakaipa havana zivo here? Ivo vanodya vanhu vangu sechingwa, Vasingadani kuna Mwari.</li>
      <li>Vaitya kwazvo ipapo, pakanga pasina chinotyisa; Nokuti Mwari akaparadza mapfupa aiye akanga akakukomba; Iwe wakavanyadzisa, nokuti Mwari akavarasha.</li>
      <li>Dai kuponeswa kwaIsiraeri kwaibva paZiyoni! Kana Mwari achidzosa vanhu vake pakutapwa, Ipapo Jakobho achafara kwazvo naIsiraeri achafara.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndirwirei Mwari, nezita renyu, Nditongerei nesimba renyu.</li>
      <li>Inzwai munyengetero wangu, Mwari; Rerekerai nzeve yenyu munzwe mashoko omuromo wangu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vatorwa vakandimukira, Vamanikidzi vakatsvaka mweya wangu. Havana kuisa Mwari pamberi pavo.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, Mwari ndiye mubatsiri wangu. Ishe ari pakati pavanotsigira mweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Achatsiva zvakaipa kuvavengi vangu; Muvaparadze nokutendeka kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndichakubayirai nechipiriso chokungopa nokuzvidira, Ndichavonga zita renyu, Jehovha, nokuti rakanaka.</li>
      <li>Nokuti akandirwira pakutambudzika kwose; Ziso rangu rakaona kukundwa kwavavengi vangu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Rerekerai nzeve yenyu kumunyengetero wangu, Mwari; Regai kuzvivanza pakukumbira kwangu.</li>
      <li>Nditeererei, mundipindure; . Ndinoshaiwa zororo mukuchema kwangu, ndichivuvura;</li>
      <li>Nokuda kwenzwi romuvengi, Nokuda kwokumanikidza kwowakaipa; , Nokuti vanondipomera zvakaipa, Vanonditambudza nokutsamwa kwavo.</li>
      <li>moyo wangu unorwadziwa kwazvo mukati mangu; Garudzo rorufu rakandiwira,</li>
      <li>Kutya nokubvunda zvakandiwira. Kutya kukuru kwakandifukidza.</li>
      <li>Ini ndakati, Haiwa, dai ndaiva namapapiro senjiva! Ndaibhururuka, ndikandozorora.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, ndingadai ndaitizira kure, Ndaindogara kurenje.</li>
      <li>Ndaikurumidza kundovanda, Nditize mhepo inovhuvhuta nedutu guru.</li>
      <li>Paradzai, Ishe mukanganise marimi avo; Nokuti ndakaona kumanikidza nokurwa muguta.</li>
      <li>Masikati novusiku vanoripoteredza pamasvingo aro; Zvakaipawo nezvakashata zviri mukati maro.</li>
      <li>Kushata kuri pakati paro; Kumanikidza nokunyengera hazvibvi panzira dzaro.</li>
      <li>Nokuti akanga asi muvengi akandishora; Ipapo ndaigona kutsunga; Akanga asi iye aindivenga akazvikudza kwandiri; Ipapo ndaimuvanda.</li>
      <li>Asi wakanga uriwe, munhu wakaenzana neni, Shamwari yangu, nomuzikanwi wangu.</li>
      <li>Taisirangana zvakanaka, Taifamba mumba maMwari pamwechete navanhu vazhinji.</li>
      <li>Rufu ngaruvawire kamwe-kamwe, Ngavaburikire kuSheori vari vapenyu; Nokuti kushata kuri paugaro hwavo, imo mukati mavo.</li>
      <li>Kana ndirini, ndichadana kuna Mwari; Jehovha achandiponesa.</li>
      <li>Madekwana namangwanani namasikati ndichachema ndichivuvura; Iye achanzwa inzwi rangu.</li>
      <li>Wakadzikunura mweya wangu norugare, kukasava nomumwe akaswedera kwandiri; Nokuti vakanga vachirwa neni, vaiva vazhinji.</li>
      <li>Mwari achanzwa, achavapindura, Iye aripo kare nakare, Nokuti havashanduki, Havatyi Mwari.</li>
      <li>Wakatambanudzira maoko ake kuna vaiva norugare naye; Wakashora sungano yake.</li>
      <li>Mashoko omuromo wake akatedza samafuta, Asi kurwa kwakanga kuri pamoyo pake; Mashoko ake akanga ari manyoro kupfuura mafuta, Kunyange zvakadaro yaiva minondo yakavhomorwa.</li>
      <li>Kandira mutoro wako pamusoro paJehovha, iye achakusimbisa; Haangatongotenderi akarurama kuti azununguswe.</li>
      <li>Asi imi Mwari muchavaburusira kugomba rokuparadzwa; Vanhu vanokarira ropa navanonyengera havangapedzi hafu yamazuva avo; Asi ini ndichavimba nemi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndinzwirei tsitsi, Mwari; nokuti vanhu vanotsvaka kundimedza; Zuva rose vanorwa neni vachindimanikidza.</li>
      <li>Vavengi vangu vanoda kundimedza zuva rose; Nokuti vanorwa neni vachizvikudza vazhinji.</li>
      <li>Panguva yandinotya, Ndichavimba nemi.</li>
      <li>MunaMwari ndicharumbidza shoko rake; Ndakavimba naMwari, handingatyi; Nyama ingandiiteiko?</li>
      <li>Zuva rose vanoshandura mashoko angu; Mifungo yavo yose inondifungira zvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Vanoungana, vanovanda, Vanocherekedza makwara angu, Kana vachivandira mweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Vachapukunyuka nenzira yezvakaipa here? Paradzai vanhu nokutsamwa kwenyu, Mwari.</li>
      <li>Imi munoverenga madzungairiro angu; Isai misodzi yangu mumidziyo yenyu; Haizi murugwaro rwenyu here?</li>
      <li>ipapo vavengi vangu vachadzokera shure nomusi wandinodana; Ndinoziva chinhu ichi, kuti Mwari ari kurutivi rwangu.</li>
      <li>MunaMwari ndicharumbidza shoko rake; MunaJehovha ndicharumbidza shoko rake.</li>
      <li>Ndakavimba naMwari, handingatyi; Vanhu vangandiiteiko?</li>
      <li>Ndinosungwa nezvandakakupikirai Mwari; Ndichakuvigirai zvipiriso zvokuvonga nazvo.</li>
      <li>Nokuti makarwira mweya wangu parufu; Namakumbo angu pakugumburwa. Kuti ndifambe pamberi paMwari Muchiedza choupenyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>. Ndinzwirei tsitsi, Mwari, ndinzwirei tsitsi; Nokuti mweya wangu unotizira kwamuri; Zvirokwazvo, ndichatizira kumumvuri wamapapiro enyu, Kusvikira njodzi dzapfuura.</li>
      <li>Ndichadanidzira kuna Mwari Wokumusorosoro; Kuna Mwari anondiitira zvose.</li>
      <li>Achatuma mubatsiri ari kudenga, andiponese, Kana iye, anovavarira kundimedza, achindishora; Mwari achatuma tsitsi dzake nezvokwadi yake.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu uri pakati peshumba; Ndinovata pasi pakati pavanopfuta somoto, Ivo vanakomana vavanhu, vana meno anenge mapfumo nemiseve, Uye rurimi rwavo munondo unopinza.</li>
      <li>Imwi mukudzwe Mwari, pamusoro pokudenga-denga; Kurumbidzwa kwenyu ngakuve kumusoro kwapasi pose.</li>
      <li>Vakateyira tsoka dzangu mumbure; Mweya wangu wakakotamiswa; Vakachera hunza pamberi pangu; Vawira mukati mayo vamene.</li>
      <li>moyo wangu wakasimba, Mwari, moyo wangu wakasimba; Ndichaimba, zvirokwazvo, ndichaimba nziyo dzokurumbidza.</li>
      <li>Muka iwe moyo wangu, muka iwe mutengeranwa nembira; Ini ndimene ndichamuka mangwanani.</li>
      <li>Ndichakuvongai, Ishe, pakati pendudzi dzavanhu; Ndichakuimbirai nziyo dzokurumbidza pakati pavahedheni.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ngoni dzenyu ihuru kusvikira kudenga-denga, Zvokwadi yenyu inosvikira kudenga rose.</li>
      <li>Imi mukudzwe Mwari, kumusoro kwokudenga-denga; Kurumbidzwa kwenyu ngakuve kumusoro kwapasi pose.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Munototaura zvakarurama here, imi vane simba, Munotongera vanakomana vavanhu zvakarurama here?</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, mumoyo menyu munoita zvakaipa; Munoyerera vanhu pasi pose kumanikidza kwamaoko enyu.</li>
      <li>Vakaipa vakava vatorwa kubva padumbu ramai; Vanotsauka vachangozvarwa, vachireva nhema.</li>
      <li>Uturu hwavo hwakafanana nouturu hwenyoka; Vakafanana nechiva chisinganzwi, chinodzivira nzeve yacho;</li>
      <li>Chisingateereri inzwi renanga, Kunyange achiimba nouchenjeri hukuru.</li>
      <li>Mwari vhunai meno avo avo mumuromo mavo; Jehovha gurai meno makuru avana veshumba.</li>
      <li>Ngavapwe semvura inoyerera; Kana achishumba nemiseve yake, ngaive seyakagurika.</li>
      <li>Ngavafanane nehozhwa inonyakatika ichipera; Segambamwedzi romukadzi risina kuona zuva.</li>
      <li>Hari dzenyu dzisati dzanzwa moto neweminzwa, Iye achadzibvisa nechamupupuri nyama igere, nomoto pamwechete.</li>
      <li>Akarurama achafara kana achiona kutsiva; Achashambidza tsoka dzake muropa ravakaipa.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo vanhu vachati, Zvirokwazvo mubayiro wowakarurama uripo; Zvirokwazvo Mwari aripo, anotonga pasi pose.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndirwirei pavavengi vangu, Mwari wangu; Ndiisei pakakwirira kure navanondimukira.</li>
      <li>Ndirwirei pavaiti vezvakaipa, Ndiponesei pavanhu veropa.</li>
      <li>Nokuti tarirai, vanovandira mweya wangu; Vane simba vakaungana kuzorwa neni; Hakuzi nokuda kwokudarika kwangu kana kwezvivi zvangu, Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Vanomhanya nokuzvigadzira, ini ndisina mhosva hangu; Mukai mundibatsire, muone.</li>
      <li>Iyemi Jehovha, Mwari wehondo, Mwari waIsiraeri, Mukai mushanyire vahedheni vose; Musanzwira tsitsi mudariki upi noupi akaipa.</li>
      <li>Vanodzoka madekwana, vanohuhudza sembwa, Vanopota neguta.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, vanodzvova nemiromo Minondo iri pamiromo yavo; Nokuti vanoti, Ndianiko anganzwa?</li>
      <li>Asi imi Jehovha muchavaseka; Muchadadira vahedheni vose.</li>
      <li>Imi simba rangu, ndichakumirirai; Nokuti Mwari ndiye nhare yangu yakakwirira.</li>
      <li>Mwari wangu achandichingura netsitsi dzake; Mwari achandionesa kukundwa kwavavengi vangu.</li>
      <li>Musavauraya, kuti vanhu vangu varege kukanganwa; Muvaparadzire nesimba renyu, muvawisire pasi, Ishe nhovo yedu.</li>
      <li>Nokuda kwechivi chomuromo wavo, namashoko emiromo yavo, Ngavabatwe pakuzvikudza kwavo, Uye nokuda kwokutuka nenhema dzavanotaura.</li>
      <li>Vapedzei nehasha, vapedzei, varege kuzovapo; Ngavazive kuti Mwari anobata ushe pakati paJakobho, Kusvikira kumigumo yenyika.</li>
      <li>Panguva yamadekwana ngavadzoke, ngavahuhudze sembwa, Ngavapote-pote neguta.</li>
      <li>Vachadzungaira vachitsvaka zvokudya, Vachagara usiku hwose kana vasingaguti.</li>
      <li>Asi ini ndichaimba ndichireva simba renyu; Zvirokwazvo ndicharumbidza tsitsi dzenyu mangwanani; Nokuti makanga muri nhare yangu yakakwirira, Noutiziro hwangu pazuva rokutambudzika kwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichakuimbirai nziyo dzokurumbidza, imi simba rangu; Nokuti Mwari ndiye nhare yangu yakakwirira, iye Mwari anondinzwira tsitsi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mwari, makatirasha, makatiparadza; Makanga makatsamwa; Haiwa, tidzorei.</li>
      <li>Makabvundisa nyika; makaitsemura; Gadzirai mitswe yayo; nokuti inozununguka.</li>
      <li>Makaratidza vanhu venyu zvinhu zvinorema; Makatinwisa waini inobata.</li>
      <li>Makapa vanokutyai mureza, Kuti uratidzwe nokuda kwezvokwadi.</li>
      <li>Kuti vadikanwi venyu varwirwe, Tiponesei noruoko rwenyu rworudyi, mutipindure.</li>
      <li>Mwari akataura pautsvene hwake, achiti, Ndichafara kwazvo; Ndichaganhura Shekemu, ndichayera mupata weSukoti.</li>
      <li>Giriyadhi ndeyangu Manase ndeyangu; Efuremuwo inhawiro yomusoro wangu; Judha ndiyo tsvimbo yangu youshe.</li>
      <li>Moabhu ndiwo mudziyo wangu wokushambidzira; Pamusoro peEdhomu ndipo pandichakandira shangu yangu; Iwe Firisitia, pururudza nokuda kwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndianiko achandiisa muguta rakasimba? Ndianiko achandiperekedza ndiende Edhomu?</li>
      <li>Hamuna kutirasha here, Mwari? Hamubudi Mwari, nehondo dzedu.</li>
      <li>Tibatsirei pamudzivisi wedu; Nokuti kubatsira kwavanhu hakuna maturo.</li>
      <li>Muna Mwari tichaita noumhare; Nokuti ndiye achatsikira vadzivisi vedu pasi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Inzwai kuchema kwangu, Mwari, Teererai munyengetero wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichadana kwamuri ndiri pamugumo wapasi, kana moyo wangu waziya; Ndiperekedzerei kudombo randisingasvikiri.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi makanga muri utiziro hwangu, Neshongwe yangu yakasimba kwandingatiza muvengi wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichagara patende renyu nokusingaperi; Ndichavanda munyasi mamapapiro enyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi Mwari makanzwa mhiko dzangu; Makadzosa nhaka yavanotya zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Muchawedzera mazuva ohupenyu hwamambo; Makore ake achaenzana naamarudzi mazhinji.</li>
      <li>Achagara pamberi paMwari nokusingaperi; Mumugadzirire unyoro nezvokwadi, kuti zvimuchengete.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo ndichaimbira zita renyu nziyo dzokurumbidza nokusingaperi, Kuti ndiite mhiko dzangu zuva rimwe nerimwe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, mweya wangu unongorindira Mwari; Kwaari ndiko kunobva kuponeswa kwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndiye oga dombo rangu nomuponesi wangu; Ndiye shongwe yangu yakakwirira; handingazununguswi zvikuru.</li>
      <li>Muchavavarira munhu kusvikira rinhiko, Kuti mumuuraye imi mose, Sorusvingo runoda kuwa, noruzhowa runotsveyama?</li>
      <li>Vanongorangana kuti vamusundire pasi abve paukuru hwake; Vanofarira nhema; Vanoropafadza nomuromo wavo, asi vanotuka mumoyo mavo.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu, rindira Mwari zvirokwazvo Nokuti ndinomutarira iye.</li>
      <li>Ndiye oga dombo rangu noruponeso rwangu; Ndiye shongwe yangu yakakwirira; handingazununguswi.</li>
      <li>Kuna Mwari ndiko kunokuponeswa kwangu nokukudzwa kwangu; Dombo resimba rangu noutiziro hwangu zviri kuna Mwari.</li>
      <li>Vimbai naye nguva dzose, imi vanhu; Dururai moyo yenyu pamberi pake; Mwari ndiye utiziro hwedu.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo vanhu vasingakudzwi mweya chete, uye vanhu vanokudzwa inhema; Pakuyerwa havaremi; Vose pamwechete vakareruka kupfuura mweya.</li>
      <li>Regai kuvimba nokumanikidza, Regai kuzvikudza pamusoro pokupambara; Kana fuma ichiwanda, regai kuinamatira nomoyo.</li>
      <li>Mwari akataura kamwechete, Ndakazvinzwa kaviri; Kuti simba nderaMwari;</li>
      <li>Netsitsiwo ndedzenyu, Ishe; Nokuti munoitira munhu mumwe nomumwe sezvaakabata.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mwari, imi muri Mwari wangu; ndichakutsvakai mangwanani; Mweya wangu unenyota kwamuri, nyama yangu inokushuvai, Panyika yakaoma, inonzwisa nyota, isina mvura.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo ndakatarira kwamuri panzvimbo tsvene, Kuti ndione simba renyu nokubwinya kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti unyoro hwenyu hunokunda upenyu; Miromo yangu ichakurumbidzai.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo ndichakuvongai ndichiri mupenyu; Ndichasimudza maoko angu nezita renyu.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu uchaguta nezvinenge mwongo namafuta; Muromo wangu uchakurumbidzai nemiromo inofara kwazvo;</li>
      <li>Kana ndichikurangarirai panhovo yangu, Ndichikufungai panguva dzousiku.</li>
      <li>Nokuti makanga muri mubatsiri wangu, Pamumvuri wamapapiro enyu ndipo pandichafara kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu unokunamatirai nesimba rose; Ruoko rwenyu rworudyi runonditsigira.</li>
      <li>Asi avo, vanotsvaka kuparadza mweya wangu, Vachapinda munzvimbo dzapasi dzenyika.</li>
      <li>Vachaiswa pasimba romunondo; Vachava mugove wamakava.</li>
      <li>Asi mambo achafara munaMwari; Mumwe nomumwe anopika naye achafara kwazvo; Nokuti muromo wavanoreva nhema uchadzivirwa.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Inzwai inzwi rangu, Mwari, pakuchema kwangu; Chengetai upenyu hwangu ndirege kutyiswa nomuvengi.</li>
      <li>Ndivanzei pakurangana kwakavanda kwavanoita zvakaipa; Pabope ravanobata zvakaipa;</li>
      <li>Ivo vakarodza rurimi rwavo somunondo, Vakashumba miseve yavo, iwo mashoko anovava;</li>
      <li>Kuti vafure akarurama, vakavanda ivo; Kamwe-kamwe vanomufura, vasingatyi.</li>
      <li>Vanotsungirira pazano rakaipa; Vanorangana kuteya misungo pakavanda; Vanoti, Ndianiko angazviona?</li>
      <li>Vanofungisa zvakaipa; Vanoti, Tapedza kufungisa zano guru; Kufunga kwomukati kwomumwe nomumwe, nomoyo, zvakadzika.</li>
      <li>Asi Mwari achavapfura, Vachakuvadzwa kamwe-kamwe nomuseve.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo vachagumbuswa, ndimi dzavo dzichivapupurira zvakaipa; Vose vanovaona vachadzungudza musoro.</li>
      <li>Vanhu vose vachatya; Vachaparidza basa raMwari, Vachicherekedza zvakanaka zvaanoita.</li>
      <li>Vakarurama vachafara muna Jehovha, vachavimba naye; Vose vane moyo yakarurama vachafara kwazvo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Imi Mwari munofanira kurumbidzwa paZiyoni; Imi munofanira kuitirwa mhiko.</li>
      <li>Imi vokunzwa munyengetero, Vanhu vose vanofanira kuuya kwamuri.</li>
      <li>Mashoko akaipa ondikunda; Kana kuri kudarika kwedu muchakudzima imi.</li>
      <li>Akaropafadzwa munhu wamunosanangura, wamunoswededza kwamuri, Kuti agare pavazhe dzenyu; Isu tichagutiswa nounaki hweimba yenyu, Iyo nzvimbo tsvene yetemberi yenyu.</li>
      <li>Mukururama kwenyu munotipindura nezvinhu zvinotyisa, Imi Mwari muponesi wedu; Imi chivimbo chamativi ose apasi, Navari kure pagungwa;</li>
      <li>Iye, anoteya makomo nesimba rake; Iye, akasungwa chiuno nesimba;</li>
      <li>Iye, unonyaradza kutinhira kwamakungwa, iko kutinhira kwamafungo awo, Nokupopota kwavanhu.</li>
      <li>Naivo vagere kumigumo vanotya zviratidzo zvenyu; Munofadza mabudiro amangwanani naamadeko.</li>
      <li>Munoshanyira pasi, munopadiridza, Munopafumisa kwazvo; Rwizi rwaMwari ruzere nemvura; Munovagadzirira zviyo, kana magadzira pasi saizvozvo.</li>
      <li>Munozadza mihoronga yapo kwazvo; Munoenzanisa mipanje yapo; Munopanyorovesa nemvura inopfunha; Munoropafadza zvinomera zvapo.</li>
      <li>Munoshongedza mwaka nekorona younaki hwenyu; Makwara enyu anodonha mafuta.</li>
      <li>Anodonha pamafuro erenje; Zvikomo zvinozvisunga nomufaro.</li>
      <li>Mafuro akafukidzwa namapoka ezvipfuwo; Uye mipatawo yakafukidzwa nezviyo; Zvinopururudza, zvichiimbawo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pururudzai kuna Mwari, imi nyika dzose;</li>
      <li>Imbirai mukurumbira wezita rake; Rumbidzai kudzo yake.</li>
      <li>Itiyi kuna Mwari, Mabasa enyu anotyisa sei! Vavengi venyu vachazviisa pasi penyu nemhaka youkuru hwesimba renyu.</li>
      <li>Pasi pose pachanamata kwamuri, Pachakuimbirai; Vachaimbira zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Uyai, muone mabasa aMwari; Anotyisa pane zvaanoitira vana vavanhu.</li>
      <li>Akashandura gungwa rikava nyika yakaoma; Vakayambuka rwizi netsoka; Ipapo takafara maari.</li>
      <li>Anobata ushe nokusingaperi nesimba rake; Meso ake anocherekedza ndudzi; Vanomumukira ngavarege kuzvikudza.</li>
      <li>Vongai Mwari, imi vanhu, inzwi rokumurumbidza ngarinzwike;</li>
      <li>Iye anopa mweya upenyu, Asingatenderi tsoka dzedu kuti dzitedzemuke.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi Mwari makatiidza; Makatiidza sezvinoidzwa sirivha.</li>
      <li>Makatipinza pamumbure; Makatitakudza mutoro unorema pazviuno zvedu.</li>
      <li>Makafambisa vanhu pamusoro pemisoro yedu, Takapinda nomumoto nemvura; Asi makatibudisa kunzvimbo inezvakawanda.</li>
      <li>Ndichapinda mumba menyu nezvipiriso zvinopiswa, Ndichakuitirai mhiko dzangu,</li>
      <li>Dzakarehwa nemiromo yangu, Dzakataurwa nomuromo wangu pakutambudzika kwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichakubayirai zvipiriso zvinopiswa zvezvakakora, Nezvinonhuwira zvamakondohwe; Ndichabayira nzombe pamwechete nembudzi.</li>
      <li>Uyai munzwe, imi mose munotya Mwari, Ndichakududzirai zvaakaitira mweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakachema kwaari nomuromo wangu, Akarumbidzwa zvikuru norurimi rwangu.</li>
      <li>Kana ndikarangarira zvakaipa mumoyo mangu, Ishe haangandinzwi;</li>
      <li>Asi zvirokwazvo Mwari akanzwa; Akateerera inzwi rokunyengetera kwangu.</li>
      <li>Mwari ngaavongwe, Iye asina kuramba munyengetero wangu, kana kubvisa tsitsi yake kwandiri.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mwari ngaatinzwire tsitsi, atiropafadze, Ngaativhenekere nechiso chake;</li>
      <li>Kuti nzira yenyu izikanwe pasi, Nokuponesa kwenyu pakati pendudzi dzose.</li>
      <li>Vanhu ngavakuvongei, Mwari; Vanhu vose ngavakuvongei.</li>
      <li>Ndudzi ngadzifare, ngadziimbe nomufaro; Nokuti muchatonga vanhu nokururama, Muchafambisa ndudzi pasi.</li>
      <li>Vanhu ngavakuvongei Mwari; Vanhu vose ngavakuvongei.</li>
      <li>Pasi pakabereka zvibereko zvapo; Mwari, iye Mwari wedu, achatiropafadza.</li>
      <li>Mwari achatiropafadza; Nemigumo yose yapasi ichamutya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mwari ngaasimuke, vavengi vake ngavaparadzirwe; Vanomuvenga ngavatize pamberi pake.</li>
      <li>Muvadzinge, sokudzingwa kwoutsi; Sokunyauka kwenamo pamoto, Saizvozvo vakaipa ngavapere pamberi paMwari.</li>
      <li>Asi vakarurama ngavafare; ngavafare kwazvo pamberi paMwari; Ngavafare nokufara kukuru.</li>
      <li>Imbirai Mwari, imbirai zita rake nziyo dzokurumbidza; Mumugadzirire mugwagwa wakanaka, iye anofamba nengoro napamarenje; Zita rake ndiJehovha; farai kwazvo pamberi pake.</li>
      <li>Baba venherera, nomutongi wemhosva dzechirikadzi, Ndiye Mwari paugaro hwake hutsvene.</li>
      <li>Vakanga vari voga, Mwari anovagarisa pamhuri; Anobudisira vasungwa kumufaro; Asi vanomumukira vanogara panyika yakaoma.</li>
      <li>Mwari, panguva yamakatungamirira vanhu venyu, Panguva yokufamba kwenyu murenje;</li>
      <li>Pasi pakabvunda, Kudenga-denga kwakadonha pamberi paMwari; Nairo Sinai rakabvunda pamberi paMwari, iye Mwari waIsiraeri.</li>
      <li>Imi Mwari makanisa mvura zhinji, Makasimbisa nhaka yenyu panguva yokuneta kwayo.</li>
      <li>Ungano yenyu yakagaramo; Imi Mwari makagadzirira varombo zvakanaka zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ishe akataura shoko, Vakadzi vakaparidza shoko vaiva</li>
      <li>Madzimambo ehondo anotiza, Mukadzi akasara kumusha ndiye anogovera zvakapambwa.</li>
      <li>Kana imi movata pasi pakati pamatanga amakwai, Zvakafanana namapapiro enjiva akafukidzwa nesirivha, Neminhenga yakafukidzwa nendarama tsvuku.</li>
      <li>Panguva iyo waMasimbaose yaakaparadza madzimambomo, Zvakafanana nokuwa kwechando paZarimoni.</li>
      <li>Gomo reBhashani igomo raMwari; Gomo reBhashani igomo refu-refu.</li>
      <li>Imi makomo marefu, munogodorerei Iro gomo rakadikanwa naMwari kuti agare mariri? Jehovha achagara mariri nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Ngoro dzaMwari dzinosvika zviuru zvina makumi maviri, zviuru zvezviuru zvamazana; Ishe ari pakati padzo, sezvaakaita paSinai, panzvimbo tsvene.</li>
      <li>Makakwira kumusoro, mukatapa vatapwa venyu; Makagamuchira zvipo pakati pavanhu Zvirokwazvo pakati pavakakumukiraiwo, kuti Jehovha Mwari agare navo.</li>
      <li>Ishe ngaavongwe, iye anotakura mitoro yedu zuva rimwe nerimwe, Iye Mwari muponesi wedu.</li>
      <li>Mwari ndiye Mwari anotirwira; Jehovha Ishe ndiye ane nzira dzokubuda murufu.</li>
      <li>Asi Mwari achatema misoro yavavengi vake, Paganda romusoro rine vhudzi romunhu anorambira pakutadza kwake.</li>
      <li>Ishe akati, Ndichavadzosa paBhashani, Ndichavadzosazve pagungwa rakadzika;</li>
      <li>Kuti unyike rutsoka rwako muropa, Kuti ndimi dzembwa dzako dzive nomugove wadzo pavavengi vako.</li>
      <li>Vakaona mafambiro enyu, Mwari, Mafambiro aMwari wangu, Mambo wangu, achipinda panzvimbo tsvene.</li>
      <li>Vaimbi vakatungamira, varidzi vemitengeranwa vakatevera, Pakati pavasikana vakanga vachiridza makandira.</li>
      <li>Rumbidzai Mwari paungano, Iye Ishe, iyemi vetsime raIsiraeri.</li>
      <li>Bhenjamini muduku, mubati wavo, aripo, Namachinda aJudha navazhinji vavo, Namachinda aZebhuruni, namachinda aNafutari.</li>
      <li>Mwari wako akaraira simba rake; Simbisai, Mwari, izvo zvamakatiitira.</li>
      <li>Nokuda kwetemberi yenyu paJerusaremu Madzimambo achakuvigirai zvipo.</li>
      <li>Tukai chikara chetsanga, Hando zhinji, nemhuru dzendudzi dzavanhu, Vazviwisire pasi petsoka nemari yesirivha; Muparadzire vanhu vanofarira kurwa.</li>
      <li>Machinda achabuda Ijipiti; Itiopia ichakurumidza kutambanudza maoko ayo kuna Mwari.</li>
      <li>Imbirai Mwari, imi ushe hwapasi; Imbirai Ishe nziyo dzokurumbidza.</li>
      <li>Iye anotasva padenga rokudenga-denga, iro rakare nakare; Inzwai, anobudisa inzwi rake, inzwi rine simba.</li>
      <li>Ipai Mwari simba; Ukuru hwake huri pamusoro paIsiraeri, Simba rake riri mumakore.</li>
      <li>Imi Mwari munotyisa panzvimbo dzenyu tsvene; Mwari waIsiraeri ndiye anopa vanhu vake simba noushe. Mwari ngaavongwe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndiponesei, Mwari, Nokuti mvura zhinji yasvikira pamweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndinonyura munhope yakadzika, pokumira Ndakasvika pamvura zhinji yakadzika, pandinofukidzwa nenzizi.</li>
      <li>Ndaneta nokuchema kwangu; huro dzangu dzaoma; Meso angu anovava nokurindira Mwari wangu.</li>
      <li>Vanondivenga ndisina mhosva vazhinji kupfuura vhudzi romusoro wangu; Avo vanoda kundiparadza vane simba, kunyange vachindivenga ndisina mhosva; Ndakafanira kudzosera zvandinenge ndisina kutora.</li>
      <li>Mwari munoziva upenzi hwangu; Mhosva dzangu hadzina kukuvanzirwai.</li>
      <li>Ishe Mwari wehondo, vanokurindirai ngavarege kunyadziswa nokuda kwangu; Mwari waIsiraeri, vanokutsvakai ngavarege kuzvidzwa nokuda kwangu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndakatenda kushorwa nokuda kwenyu; Kunyadza kwakafukidza chiso changu.</li>
      <li>Ndakava mutorwa kuhama dzangu, Nomubvakure kuvana vamai vangu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti kushingairira imba yenyu kwakandipedza; Nokushora, kwavanokushorai kwakawira pamusoro pangu.</li>
      <li>Panguva yokuchema kwangu nokutambudza mweya wangu ndichizvinyima, Ndakashorwa nokuda kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Panguva yandakafuka masaga ndikaaita nguvo dzangu, Ndakava shumo pakati pavo.</li>
      <li>Vanogara pasuo vanondireva; Ndiri chiimbo chavakabatwa nedoro.</li>
      <li>Asi kana ndirini, munyengetero wangu uri kwamuri, Ishe, panguva yakafanira; Mwari, netsitsi dzenyu zhinji Ndipindurei nokuponesa kwenyu kwakatendeka.</li>
      <li>Ndirwirei munhope, ndirege kunyura; Ndirwirwe kuna vanondivenga, napamvura zhinji yakadzika.</li>
      <li>Boporodzi remvura rirege kundikunda, Mvura yakadzika irege kundimedza; Gomba rirege kuzarira muromo waro pamusoro pangu.</li>
      <li>Ndipindurei, Jehovha; nokuti unyoro hwenyu hwakanaka; Ringirai kwandiri nokuda kwetsitsi dzenyu zhinji.</li>
      <li>Regai kuvanzira muranda wenyu chiso chenyu; Nokuti ndiri pakutambudzika; kurumidzai kundipindura.</li>
      <li>Swederai kumweya wangu, muudzikunure; Ndidzikunurei nokuda kwavavengi vangu.</li>
      <li>Munoziva kushorwa kwangu, nokunyadzwa kwangu nokuzvidzwa kwangu Vadzivisi vangu vose vari mberi kwangu.</li>
      <li>Kushora kwakaputsa moyo wangu; ndaremerwa kwazvo; Ndakatsvaka vangandinzwira nyasha, asi kwakanga kusino munhu; Ndakatsvaka vavaraidzi, asi handina kuwana nomumwe.</li>
      <li>Vakandipa nduru zvive zvokudya zvangu; Pakunzwa nyota kwangu vakandinwisa vhiniga.</li>
      <li>Tafura yavo ngaive musungo pamberi pavo; Neriva, kana vakagarika havo.</li>
      <li>Meso avo ngaapofumadzwe, varege kuona, Zviuno zvavo ngazvirambe zvichiguda-guda.</li>
      <li>Dururai kutsamwa kwenyu pamusoro pavo, Hasha dzenyu dzinopfuta, ngadzivabate.</li>
      <li>Ugaro hwavo ngahuparadzwe; Ngakurege kuva nomunhu anogara pamatende avo.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vanotambudza uyo wamakarova; Vanotaura zvokurwadziwa kwavaya vamakakuvadza.</li>
      <li>Wedzerai zvakaipa pazvakaipa zvavo; Ngavarege kupinda pakururama kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Ngavadzimwe parugwaro rwoupenyu, Varege kunyorwa pamwechete navakarurama.</li>
      <li>Asi ini ndiri murombo, ndinorwadziwa; Kuponesa kwenyu, Mwari, ngakundiise pakakwirira.</li>
      <li>Ndicharumbidza zita raMwari norwiyo, Ndichamukudza nokuvonga.</li>
      <li>Izvo zvichafadza Jehovha kupfuura nzombe, Kana hando ine nyanga namahwanda.</li>
      <li>Vanyoro vakazviona vakafara; Imi munotsvaka Mwari, moyo yenyu ngairarame.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha anonzwa vashaiwi, Haashori vasungwa vake.</li>
      <li>Kudenga napasi ngazvimurumbidze, Makungwa, nezvose zvinopfakanyikamo.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Mwari achaponesa Ziyoni, nokuvaka maguta aJudha, Vachagaramo, ive nhaka yavo.</li>
      <li>Ichava nhaka yavana vavaranda vake; Vanoda zita rake vachagaramo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kurumidzai, Mwari, kundirwira; Kurumidzai kundibatsira, Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Ngavanyadziswe, ngavazvidzwe Ivo vanotsvaka mweya wangu; Ngavadzoserwe shure, vashovorwe Ivo vanofarira kundikuvadza.</li>
      <li>Ngavadzoserwe shure nokuda kwenyadzi dzavo Ivo vanoti, Hekani, hekani! Waro!</li>
      <li>Vose vanokutsvakai ngavafarise vave nomufaro mamuri; Vanoda kuponesa kwenyu ngavarambe vachiti, Mwari ngaakudzwe!</li>
      <li>Asi ini ndiri murombo nomushaiwi; Kurumidzai muuye kwandiri, Mwari; Imi muri mubatsiri wangu nomurwiri wangu; Regai kunonoka, Jehovha.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, ndinovimba nemi; Ngandirege kutongonyadziswa.</li>
      <li>Ndirwirei mukururama kwenyu, ndisunungurei; Rerekerai nzeve yenyu kwandiri, mundiponese.</li>
      <li>Ivai dombo rangu mandingagara, kwandingaramba ndichienda; Makaraira kuti ndiponeswe; Nokuti ndimi dombo rangu nenhare yangu.</li>
      <li>Ndisunungurei, Mwari wangu, paruoko rwowakaipa, Paruoko rwousina kururama nomunhu anomanikidza.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi, Ishe Jehovha, muri tariro yangu; Ndimi wandinovimba naye kubva pauduku hwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakatsigirwa nemi kubva pachizvaro; Ndimi makandibudisa padumbu ramai vangu; Ndichakurumbidzai.</li>
      <li>Ndiri chishamiso kuna vazhinji; Asi imi muri utiziro hwangu hwakasimba.</li>
      <li>Muromo wangu uchazadzwa nerumbidzo yenyu, Nekudzo yenyu zuva rose.</li>
      <li>Regai kundirasha panguva yokukwegura kwangu; Musandisiya kana ndapera simba.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vavengi vangu vanondireva; Vanogarira mweya wangu, vanorangana,</li>
      <li>Vachiti, Mwari amusiya; Teverai, mumubate; nokuti hakuna ungamurwira.</li>
      <li>Mwari, regai kuva kure neni; Mwari wangu, kurumidzai kundibatsira.</li>
      <li>Avo vanodzivisa mweya wangu ngavanyadziswe vapere; Vanotsvaka kundikuvadza ngavafukidzwe nokushorwa nokuzvidzwa.</li>
      <li>Asi ini ndicharamba ndichitarira, Ndicharamba ndichiwedzera kukurumbidzai.</li>
      <li>Muromo wangu uchareva kururama kwenyu, Nokuponesa kwenyu zuva rose:, Nokuti handizivi kuwanda kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Ndichauya namabasa ane simba raShe aJehovha; Ndichaparidza kururama kwenyu, iko kwenyu kwoga.</li>
      <li>Mwari, makandidzidzisa kubva paujaya hwangu; Kusvikira zvino ndadudzira mabasa enyu anoshamisa.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, kusvikira ndakwegura ndachena vhudzi, Mwari regai kundisiya; Kusvikira ndadudzira simba renyu kurudzi runouya, Nesimba renyu kunomumwe nomumwe anozouya.</li>
      <li>Kururama kwenyuwo, Mwari, kuri kumusoro-soro; Iyemi makaita zvinhu zvikuru, Mwari, ndianiko akafanana nemi?</li>
      <li>Iyemi makatiratidza madambudzo mazhinji akaipa, Ndimi muchatiraramisazve, Nokutikwidzazve tibve pakudzika kwapasi.</li>
      <li>Wedzerai hukuru hwangu, Dzokaizve mundinyaradze.</li>
      <li>Ndichakurumbidzaiwo nemitengeranwa, Naiyo zvokwadi yenyu, Mwari wangu; Ndichakuimbirai imi nziyo dzokurumbidza nembira, Iyemi Mutsvene walsiraeri.</li>
      <li>Miromo yangu ichafara kwazvo kana ndichikuimbirai nziyo dzokurumbidza; Nomweya wangu wamakadzikunura.</li>
      <li>Rurimi rwanguvo ruchataura zuva rose zvokururama kwenyu; Nokuti vanotsvaka kundikuvadza vanyadziswa, vazvidzwa.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ipai mambo zvamakatonga, Mwari, Nokururama kwenyu kumwanakomana wamambo.</li>
      <li>Achatongera vanhu venyu nokururama, Navarombo venyu achavaruramisira.</li>
      <li>Makomo nezvikomo achavigira vanhu rugare,nezvikomo nekururama.</li>
      <li>Achatongera varombo vavanhu, Achaponesa vana vavashaiwi, Nokupwanya mumanikidzi.</li>
      <li>Vachakutyai kana zuva richipo, Uye kana mwedzi uchipo, kusvikira kumarudzi namarudzi.</li>
      <li>Achaburuka iye semvura pauswa hwakagurirwa; Semvura inonaya ichidiridza pasi.</li>
      <li>Nemisi yake akarurama achakura zvakanaka; Rugare rwakawanda ruchavapo, kusvikira mwedzi waguma.</li>
      <li>Achabata ushe kubva pagungwa kusvikira pagungwa, Nokubva paRwizi kusvikira kumigumo yapasi.</li>
      <li>Vagere pamarenje vachapfugama pamberi pake; Vavengi vake vachananzva guruva.</li>
      <li>Madzimambo eTarishishi neezviwi achauya nezvipo; Madzimambo eShebha neSebha vachamuvigira zvipo;</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, madzimambo ose achawira pasi pamberi pake; Ndudzi dzose dzichamushumira.</li>
      <li>Nokuti acharwira mushaiwi kana achidanidzira; Nomurombo asina mubatsiri.</li>
      <li>Achanzwira nyasha murombo nomushaiwi, Achaponesa mweya yavashaiwi.</li>
      <li>Achadzikunura mweya yavo pakutambudzika napakumanikidzwa; Ropa ravo richava chinhu chinokosha pamberi pake;</li>
      <li>Iye achararama, achapiwa ndarama yeShebha; Vanhu vacharamba vachimunyengeterera; Vachamuvonga zuva rose.</li>
      <li>Kuchava nezviyo zvizhinji pasi pamusoro pamakomo; Zvibereko zvazvo zvichavhunga seRebhanoni; Vanogara paguta vachakura souswa pasi.</li>
      <li>Zita rake richavapo nokusingaperi; Zita rake richagara riripo panguva yose yokuvapo kwezuva; Vanhu vacharopafadzwa maari; Ndudzi dzose dzichati, Anomufaro.</li>
      <li>Jehovha Mwari, iye Mwari waIsiraeri, ngaarumbidzwe, Iye oga anoita zvinoshamisa.</li>
      <li>Zita rake rinobwinya ngarirumbidzwe nokusingaperi; Pasi pose ngapazadzwe nokubwinya kwenyu. Ameni, Ameni.</li>
      <li>Minyengetero yaDhavhidhi mwanakomana waJese yapera.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo Mwari anoitira Isiraeri zvakanaka, Ivo vane moyo yakachena.</li>
      <li>Asi kana ndirini, tsoka dzangu dzakanga dzotsauka; Makumbo angu akanga otedzemuka.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndakanga ndichigodora vana manyawi, Pakuona kwangu kufara kwavakaipa.</li>
      <li>Nokuti havatambudziki pakufa kwavo; Asi muviri wavo une simba.</li>
      <li>Havana njodzi savamwe vanhu; Havatambudzwi savamwe vanhu</li>
      <li>Saka kuzvikudza kwavo kwakafanana noruketani pamitsipa yavo; Kumanikidza kunovafukidza senguvo.</li>
      <li>Meso avo anobuda nokukora; Zvavanofunga pamoyo zvinofashamira;</li>
      <li>Vanoseka, vachireva pakuipa kwavo zvinomanikidza vamwe; Vanotaura vachizvikudza.</li>
      <li>Vakataurira kudenga nemiromo yavo, Ndimi dzavo dzinofamba-famba pasi.</li>
      <li>Saka vanhu vake vanodzokera ikoko; Vanosvinirwa mvura zhinji, mukombe uzere.</li>
      <li>Zvino vanoti, Mwari angaziva seiko? Wokumusorosoro angava nokuziva here?</li>
      <li>Tarirai, ndizvo zvakaita vakaipa; Vanowedzera fuma yavo vachingogara vasingatamburi.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo ndakanatsa moyo wangu pasina, Nokushambidza maoko angu ndisina mhosva;</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndakatambudzwa zuva rose, Ndakarangwa mangwanani ose.</li>
      <li>Kana ndaiti, ndichataura kudai; Tarirai, ndainyengera rudzi rwavana venyu.</li>
      <li>Zvino ndakaramba ndichifunga kuti ndizvinzwisise, Asi zvakandiremera kwazvo;</li>
      <li>Kusvikira ndapinda panzvimbo tsvene yaMwari, Ndikatarira kuguma kwavo.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo munovaisa panotedza; Munovawisira pasi kuti vaparadzwe.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, vanoparadzwa kamwe-kamwe! Vanopedzwa chose nezvinotyisa.</li>
      <li>Sezvakarotwa, kana munhu apepuka; Saizvozvo, Ishe, muchashora mufananidzo wavo, kana muchimuka.</li>
      <li>Nokuti moyo wangu wakachema, Ndakabayiwa patsvo dzangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakanga ndiri benzi, ndisingazivi chinhu; Ndakanga ndakafanana nemhuka pamberi penyu.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro ndinoramba ndinemi; Makabata ruoko rwangu rworudyi.</li>
      <li>Muchandiperekedza nezano renyu, Ndokuzondigamuchira pakubwinya.</li>
      <li>Ndianiko kudenga, kana musimi? Napasi hapana wandinoda kunze kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Nyama yangu nomoyo wangu zvinopera; Asi Mwari ndiye dombo romoyo wangu nomugove wangu nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Nokuti tarirai, vari kure nemi vachapera; Makaparadza vose vakakusiyai noupombwe hwavo.</li>
      <li>Kana ndirini, kuswedera pedo naye ndizvo zvinondifadza; Ishe Mwari ndakamuita nhare yangu, Kuti ndiparidze mabasa enyu ose.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haiwa Mwari, makatirashireiko nokusingaperi? Hasha dzenyu dzinopfungairira makwai amafuro enyu nemhaka yeiko?</li>
      <li>Rangarirai ungano yenyu yamakatenga kare, Yamakadzikunura kuti ruve rudzi rwenhaka yenyu; Gomo reZiyoni pamakanga mugere.</li>
      <li>Simudzai makumbo enyu muone zvakaparadzwa zvisingaperi, Izvo zvakaipa zvose zvakaitwa navavengi panzvimbo tsvene.</li>
      <li>Vadzivisi venyu vakanduruma pakati peungano yenyu; Vakamisa mireza yavo zvive zviratidzo.</li>
      <li>Vakafanana navanhu vakasimudza Masanhu mudondo remiti.</li>
      <li>Zvino zvose zvakavezwa zvayo Vanozviputsa nedimuro nenyundo.</li>
      <li>Vakapisa nzvimbo yenyu tsvene nomoto; Vakashatisa ugaro hwezita renyu vachihuputsira pasi.</li>
      <li>Vakati mumoyo mavo, Ngativaparadze pamwechete; Vakapisa nzvimbo dzose pavanounganira Mwari munyika.</li>
      <li>Hatichaoni zviratidzo zvedu; Hapachina muporofita; Pakati pedu hapana munhu anoziva kuti zvichasvikira rinhi.</li>
      <li>Haiwa Mwari, mudzivisi, achashora kusvikira rinhiko? Muvengi acharamba achizvidza zita renyu nokusingaperi here?</li>
      <li>Munodzosereiko ruoko rwenyu, irwo ruoko rwenyu rworudyi? Rutambanudzei pachipfuva chenyu, muvapedze.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro Mwari ndiye Mambo wangu kubva kare, Iye anobata mabasa okuponesa pakati penyika,</li>
      <li>Makapamura gungwa nesimba renyu; Makaputsa misoro yezvikara zvegungwa mumvura.</li>
      <li>Makaputsanya misoro yengwena, Makaipa vanhu vagere murenje kuti ive nyama yavo.</li>
      <li>Makapamura tsime neboporodzi; Makapwisa nzizi huru.</li>
      <li>Masikati ndeenyu, nousiku ndohwenyuwo; Ndimi makagadzira chiedza nezuva.</li>
      <li>Ndimi makatara miganho yose yapasi; Ndimi makaita zhizha nechando.</li>
      <li>Rangarirai chinhu ichi, kuti muvengi akakuzvidzai, Jehovha, Uye kuti rudzi rwamapenzi rwakamhura zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Regai henyu kuisa kuchikara mweya wenjiva yenyu; Musakanganwa upenyu hwavarombo venyu.</li>
      <li>Rangarirai sungano; Nokuti nzvimbo dzine rima dzapasi dzizere nougaro hwavamanikidzi.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, vanomanikidzwa ngavarege kudzoka vachinyara; Varombo navashaiwi ngavarumbidze zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Simukai Mwari, muzvireverere mhaka yenyu, Rangarirai kuzvidzwa kwenyu nebenzi zuva rose.</li>
      <li>Regai kukanganwa inzwi ravadzivisi venyu; Bope ravanokumukira rinogara richikwira.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Tinokuvongai, Mwari; Tinovonga, nokuti zita renyu riri pedo; Vanhu vanoparidza mabasa enyu anoshamisa.</li>
      <li>Kana ndichiwana nguva yakafanira, Ndichatonga zvakarurama.</li>
      <li>Pasi pose panyauka navose vagerepo; Ndini ndakamisa mbiru dzayo.</li>
      <li>Ndakati.kuna vanamanyawi , Regai kuita namanyawi; Nokuna vakaipa, Regai kusimudza runyanga.</li>
      <li>Regai kusimudza runyanga rwenyu kudenga; Regai kutaura nomutsipa mukukutu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti kunyange kumabudazuva, kana kumavirira, Kana kurenje, hakuzi ikoko kunobva kukudzwa.</li>
      <li>Asi Mwari ndiye mutongi; Anoninipisa mumwe achikudza mumwe.</li>
      <li>Nokuti muruoko rwaJehovha munomukombe, newaini inopupuma; Uzere nezvakavhenganiswa, zvino anodurura mauri; Zvirokwazvo, vakaipa vose venyika vachasvina masese awo, nokuanwa.</li>
      <li>Asi ini ndichaparidza nokusingaperi, Ndichaimbira Mwari waJakobho nziyo dzokurumbidza.</li>
      <li>Nyanga dzose dzavakaipa ndichadzigura; Asi nyanga dzavakarurama dzichasimudzwa.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mwari anozikanwa pakati paJudha; Zita rake iguru pakati palsiraeri.</li>
      <li>PaSaremiwo ndipo pane tabhenakeri yake, NapaZiyoni ugaro hwake.</li>
      <li>Ndipo paakavhuna miseve youta; Nenhovo, nomunondo, nokurwa.</li>
      <li>Imi munokubwinya, makanaka kwazvo, Kupfuura makomo ezvakapambwa.</li>
      <li>Vakatsunga pamoyo, vakapambwa, vakavata hope dzavo; Pakati pavarume vane simba hakuna akawana maoko ake.</li>
      <li>Pakutuka kwenyu, Mwari waJakobho, Ngoro nebhiza zvose zvinobatwa nehope dzorufu.</li>
      <li>Imi, iyemi, munofanira kutyiwa; Ndianiko angamira pamberi penyu kana matsamwa?</li>
      <li>Makanzwisa vanhu kutonga kwenyu kuchibva kudenga; Pasi pakatya, pakanyarara,</li>
      <li>Panguva yokumuka kwaMwari kuzotonga, Kuti aponese vanyoro vose vapasi.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, kutsamwa kwavanhu kuchakurumbidzai; Munozvisunga chiuno nokutsamwa kwakasara.</li>
      <li>Pikai, muripire Jehovha Mwari wenyu; Vose vakamupoteredza ngavauye nezvipo kuna iye anofanira kutyiwa;</li>
      <li>Iye achagura mweya yamachinda; Anotyisa kwazvo madzimambo apasi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndichadana kuna Mwari nenzwi rangu; kuna iye Mwari nenzwi rangu, acharerekera nzeve yake kwandiri.</li>
      <li>Pazuva rokutambudzika kwangu ndakatsvaka Ishe; Ruoko rwangu rwakanga rwakatambanudzwa usiku, ndisingaregi; Mweya wangu wakaramba kunyaradzwa.</li>
      <li>Ndinorangarira Mwari, ndokushaiwa mufaro; Ndinofungisisa, mweya wangu ndokuziya.</li>
      <li>Hamutenderi meso angu kutsinzina; Ndinotambudzika, handigoni kutaura.</li>
      <li>Ndakarangarira mazuva ekare, Makore enguva dzakare-kare.</li>
      <li>Ndinozviyeudzira kuimba kwangu pakati pousiku; Ndinotaurirana nomoyo wangu; Mweya wangu wakanzvera kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Ko Ishe angarasha nokusingaperi? Haachazonzwiri ngoni here?</li>
      <li>Ko tsitsi dzake dzaenda chose nokusingaperi? Chipikirwa chake chakakona nokusingaperi here?</li>
      <li>Ko Mwari akanganwa kuva nenyasha? Apfigira tsitsi dzake nyoro pakutsamwa kwake here?</li>
      <li>Ipapo ndakati, Ndihwo utera hwangu, Asi ndicharangarira makore oruoko rworudyi rwoWokumusorosoro.</li>
      <li>Ndichareva zvakaitwa naJehovha; Nokuti ndicharangarira zvishamiso zvenyu zvakare.</li>
      <li>Ndichafungisawo basa renyu rose, Nokurangarira zvamakaita.</li>
      <li>Nzira yenyu, Mwari, iri panzvimbo tsvene; Ndianiko mwari mukuru, akafanana naiye Mwari?</li>
      <li>Ndimi Mwari anoita zvishamiso; Makaratidza simba renyu pakati pavanhu.</li>
      <li>Makadzikunura vanhu venyu noruoko rwenyu, Ivo vanakomana vaJakobho naJosefa.</li>
      <li>Mvura zhinji yakakuonai, Mwari; Mvura zhinji yakakuonai, ikatya; Pakadzika pakabvunda.</li>
      <li>Makore akadurura mvura; Denga rose rakabudisa inzwi; Miseve yenyu yakafambafamba kwose.</li>
      <li>inzwi rokutinhira kwenyu rakanga riri muchamupupuri; Mheni dzakavhenekera nyika; Pasi pakabvunda nokuzununguka.</li>
      <li>Kufamba kwenyu kwakanga kuri mugungwa, Nenzira dzenyu mumvura zhinji-zhinji, Makwara enyu akanga asingazikanwi.</li>
      <li>Makafambisa vanhu venyu seboka ramakwai, Noruoko rwaMozisi norwaAroni.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Teererai murayiro wangu, imi vanhu vangu; Rerekerai nzeve dzenyu munzwe mashoko omuromo wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichashamisa muromo wangu nditaure nomufananidzo; Ndichaparidza mashoko akavanzika ekare,</li>
      <li>Zvatakanzwa nezvatakaziva, Nezvatakaudzwa namadzibaba edu.</li>
      <li>Hatingazvivanziri vana vavo, Asi tichaudza rudzi runotevera mabasa angarumbidzwa aJehovha , Nesimba rake, namabasa ake, anoshamisa, aakaita.</li>
      <li>Nokuti akamutsa chipupuriro pakati. paJakobho, Akatema murayiro pakati paIsiraeri, Akazviraira madzibaba edu, Kuti vazvizivise vana vavo;</li>
      <li>Kuti rudzi runotevera ruzvizive, ivo vana vachazoberekwa; Ivo vasimuke vazviudze vana vavo;</li>
      <li>Kuti tariro yavo ive kuna Mwari, Varege kukanganwa mabasa aMwari, Asi vachengete mirairo yake;</li>
      <li>Varege kufanana namadzibaba avo, Rwakanga ruri rudzi rusingateereri, rwakamukira Mwari. Rudzi rwakaramba kururamisa moyo yavo, Uye mweya yavo yakanga isina kutendeka kuna Mwari.</li>
      <li>Vana vaEfuraimu, kunyange vakanga vakashonga nhumbi dzokurwa nouta, Vakadzokera shure pazuva rokurwa.</li>
      <li>Havana kuchengeta sungano yaMwari, Vakaramba kufamba nomurayiro wake;</li>
      <li>Vakakanganwa zvaakaita, Namabasa ake akashamisa, aakavaratidza.</li>
      <li>Wakaita zvinhu zvinoshamisa pamberi pamadzibaba avo, Panyika yeIjipiti, pasango reZoani.</li>
      <li>Wakapamura gungwa, akavayambusa; Akamisa mvura ikafanana nomurwi.</li>
      <li>Masikatiwo wakavafambisa negore, Nousiku hwose nechiedza chomoto.</li>
      <li>Wakapamura matombo murenje, Akavanwisa zvakanaka kwazvo sapamvura inobva pakadzika.</li>
      <li>Akabudisawo hova dzemvura padombo, Akayererisa mvura zhinji yakaita senzizi.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro vakaramba vachimutadzira, Nokumukira Wokumusorosoro murenje.</li>
      <li>Vakaidza Mwari mumoyo mavo Vachikumbira zvokudya zvavakanga vachidawo.</li>
      <li>vakapopotera Mozisi Vakati, Mwari angatigadzirira chokudya murenje here?</li>
      <li>Tarirai, akarova dombo, mvura zhinji ikadzutuka, Hova dzakayerera; Ko angapa chingwawo here? Ungavigira vanhu vake nyama here?</li>
      <li>Saka Jehovha akanzwa, akatsamwa; Moto ukaveserwa Jakobho, Kutsamwa kukamukira Isiraeri;</li>
      <li>Nokuti havana kutenda Mwari, Havana kuvimba nokuponeswa kwake.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro wakaraira denga rose kumusoro, Akazarura mikova yokudenga;</li>
      <li>Akanisa mana pamusoro pavo kuti vadye, Akavapa zviyo zvokudenga.</li>
      <li>Vanhu vakadya chingwa chavatumwa; Akavatumira zvokudya kusvikira vaguta.</li>
      <li>Akabudisa mhepo yakabva mabvazuva, ikarira kudenga; Akafambisa mhepo yakabva nyasi nesimba rake.</li>
      <li>Akanisawo nyama pamusoro pavo ikaita seguruva, Neshiri, dzina mapapiro, dzikaita sejecha regungwa;</li>
      <li>Akazviwisira pakati pemisasa yavo, Pose-pose pavakanga vagere.</li>
      <li>Ipapo vakadya, vakaguta kwazvo; Akavapa zvavakanga vachikarira.</li>
      <li>Vakanga vasati vanyaradza kukara kwavo, Zvokudya zvavo zvakanga zvichiri mumiromo yavo,</li>
      <li>Kutsamwa kwaMwari kukavamukira, Akauraya vakakoresa pakati pavo, Akaparadza majaya aIsiraeri.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro vakaramba vachitadza, Vakasatenda mabasa ake aishamisa.</li>
      <li>Saka akapedza mazuva avo panezvisina maturo, Namakore avo panezvinotyisa.</li>
      <li>Zvino akati achivauraya, ipapo vakamubvunza , vakashingaira kutsvaka Mwari.</li>
      <li>Vakarangarira kuti Mwari ndiye dombo ravo, NaMwari Wokumusorosoro mudzikunuri wavo.</li>
      <li>Asi vakamubata kumeso nemiromo yavo, Vakamurevera nhema nendimi dzavo.</li>
      <li>Nokuti moyo yavo yakanga isina kururama kwaari, Uye vakanga vasina kutendeka pasungano yake.</li>
      <li>Asi iye, zvaakanga ane nyasha huru, akavakanganwira kuipa kwavo, akasavaparadza; Zvirokwazvo, kazhinji akadzora kutsamwa kwake, Akasamutsa hasha dzake dzose.</li>
      <li>Akarangarira kuti vakanga vari nyama bedzi; Nemhepo, inopfuura, isingadzokizve.</li>
      <li>Vakamumukira murenje kazhinji sei, Nokumunzwisa shungu mugwenga!</li>
      <li>Vakapamhidzazve, vakaidza Mwari, Vakadzivisa Mutsvene waIsiraeri.</li>
      <li>Havana kurangarira ruoko rwake, Kana zuva raakavadzikunura pamudzivisi.</li>
      <li>Panguva yaakavaratidza zviratidzo zvake Nezvishamiso zvake pasango reZoani;</li>
      <li>Akashandura nzizi dzavo dzikava ropa, Nehova dzavo, vakakoniwa kunwa mvura yadzo.</li>
      <li>Akatuma pakati pavo mapupira enhunzi, dzakavaruma; Namatafi, akavaparadza.</li>
      <li>Zvibereko zvavo wakazvipa mhunduru, Zvavakabatira akazvipa mhashu.</li>
      <li>Akaparadza mizambiringa yavo nechimvuramabwe, Nemionde yavo nechando.</li>
      <li>Mombe dzavo akadziisawo pachimvuramabwe, Zvipfuwo zvavo akazviisa pamheni.</li>
      <li>Akatuma pakati pavo kutsamwa kwake kukuru, Nehasha neshungu nokutambudza, Rikaita boka ravatumwa vezvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Akagadzirira kutsamwa kwake nzira; Haana kubvisa mweya wavo parufu, Asi akaisa upenyu hwavo kuhosha;</li>
      <li>Akarova matangwe ose paIjipiti, Ivo vokutanga vesimba ravo pamatende aHami;</li>
      <li>Asi akabudisa vanhu vake samakwai, Akavaperekedza murenje seboka rezvipfuwo.</li>
      <li>Akavafambisa vakafara, vakasatya; Asi gungwa rakafukidza vavengi vavo.</li>
      <li>Akavasvitsa panyika yake tsvene, Pagomo iri, raakatenga noruoko rwake rworudyi.</li>
      <li>Akadzingawo ndudzi pamberi pavo, Akavaganhurira ivo vave nhaka yavo, Akagarisa vaIsiraeri pamatende avo.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro vakaidza Mwari Wokumusorosoro, vakamumukira, Vakasachengeta zvipupuriro zvake;</li>
      <li>Asi vadzoka, vakaita zvinonyengera. Vakatsauka souta hunonyengera.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vakamutsa kutsamwa kwake namatunhu avo akakwirira, Vakamutsa godo rake nezvifananidzo zvavo zvakaveziwa.</li>
      <li>Zvino Mwari akati achizvinzwa, akatsamwa kwazvo, Akasema Isiraeri kwazvo-kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Akabva patabhenakeri yeShiro, Tende raakanga akaisa pakati pavanhu;</li>
      <li>Akaisa simba rake mukutapwa, Nokubwinya kwake muruoko rwomudzivisi.</li>
      <li>Vanhu vake wakavaisawo kumunondo; Akatsamwira nhaka yake kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Moto wakapedza majaya avo; Vasikana vavo havana kuimbirwa pakuwanikwa kwavo.</li>
      <li>Vapirisiti vavo vakaurawa nomunondo; Chirikadzi dzavo hadzina kuchema.</li>
      <li>Ipapo Ishe akapepuka somunhu akanga avete, Semhare inoridza mhere nokuda kwewaini.</li>
      <li>Akarova vadzivisi vake, vakadzokera sure. Akavanyadzisa zvisingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akarambawo tende raJosefa, Akasanangura rudzi rwaEfuremu.</li>
      <li>Asi akasanangura rudzi rwaJudha, Negomo reZiyoni raakanga achida.</li>
      <li>Akavaka nzvimbo yake tsvene senhare dzakakwirira, Sapasi paakateya nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akasanangurawo Dhavhidhi muranda wake, Akamubvisa pamatanga amakwai;</li>
      <li>Akandomutora paaifudza matunzvi aimwisa, Kuti ave mufudzi wavanhu vake Jakobho, naIsiraeri nhaka yake.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo akavafudza nokururama kwomoyo wake; Akavaperekedza nouchenjeri hwamaoko ake.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haiwa Mwari, vahedheni vakapinda panhaka yenyu; Vakasvibisa temberi yenyu tsvene; Jerusaremu vakariita dongo.</li>
      <li>Zvitunha zvavaranda venyu vakazvipa shiri dzokudenga zvive zvokudya zvadzo. Uye nyama yavatsvene venyu vakaipa zvikara zvapasi.</li>
      <li>Vakateura ropa ravo pose-pose paJerusaremu semvura; Vakashaiwa anovaviga.</li>
      <li>Tava chinhu chinoshorwa navatigere navo, Chinhu chinozvidzwa nechinosekwa navakatipoteredza.</li>
      <li>Haiwa Jehovha, mucharamba makatsamwa nokusingaperi kusvikira rinhiko? Godo renyu richapfuta somoto here?</li>
      <li>Dururai hasha dzenyu pamusoro pavahedheni vasingakuziviyi, Napamusoro poushe huzhinji, husingadi zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vakapedza Jakobho, Vakaparadza ugaro hwake.</li>
      <li>Musarangarira kutirova pamusoro pezvakaipa zvamadzibaba edu; Ngoni dzenyu nyoro ngadzikurumidze kusangana nesu; nokuti taneta kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Tibatsirei, Mwari muponesi wedu, nokuda kwomukurumbira wezita renyu;</li>
      <li>Vahedheni vacharevereiko, vachiti, Mwari wavo aripiko? Kutsihwa kweropa ravaranda venyu, rakateurwa, Ngakuzikanwe pakati pavahedheni pamberi pedu.</li>
      <li>Kugomera kwomusungwa ngakusvike kwamuri; Noukuru hwesimba renyu chengetai vana vorufu;</li>
      <li>Mutsivire vagere nesu kanomwe pachipfuva chavo. Kushora kwavakakushorai nako, imi Ishe.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo isu vanhu venyu, namakwai amafuro enyu, Tichakuvongai nokusingaperi; Ticharatidza kurumbidzwa kwenyu kumarudzi namarudzi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>teererai nenzeve, Mufudzi waIsiraeri, Iyemi munotungamirira Josefa seboka rezvipfuwo; Imi mugere pakati pamakerubhi, penyai!</li>
      <li>Mutsai simba renyu pamberi paEfuremu naBhenjamini naManase, Muuye kuzotirwira.</li>
      <li>Tidzosereizve, Mwari; Penyesai chiso chenyu, isu tiponeswe.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, Mwari wehondo, Muchatsamwira munyengetero wavanhu venyu kusvikira rinhiko?</li>
      <li>Makavadyisa zvokudya zvemisodzi, Nokuvanwisa misodzi yakawanda kwazvo.</li>

      <li>Makaputsireiko mhanda dzawo, Kuti vose vanopfuura nenzira vautanhe?</li>

      <li>Dodzokai henyu, Mwari wehondo, Tarirai muri kudenga, muone, muve nehanya nomuzambiringa uyu.</li>
      <li>Muchengete chakasimwa noruoko rwenyu rworudyi, Nomwanakomana, wamakazvirerera.</li>
      <li>Wapiswa nomoto, watemwa; Vanopera nokutuka kwechiso chenyu.</li>
      <li>Ruoko rwenyu ngaruve pamusoro pomunhu woruoko rwenyu rworudyi, Pamusoro poMwanakomana womunhu, wamakazvirerera.</li>
      <li>Ipapo hatingazobvi kwamuri; Tiraramisei isu, tigodana zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Tidzosereizve, Jehovha Mwari wehondo; Penyesai chiso chenyu, isu tiponeswe.</li>
    </ol>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Imbirai Mwari kwazvo, iye simba redu; Pururudzai kuna Mwari waJakobho.</li>
      <li>Vambai rwiyo, muridze ngoma, Nembira dzinonakidza nomutengeranwa.</li>
      <li>Ridzai hwamanda pakugara kwomwedzi, Napakuchena kwomwedzi, pamutambo wedu wakatarwa.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndizvo zvakatemerwa Zvakarairwa naMwari waJakobho.</li>
      <li>Wakazvitema muna Josefa kuti chive chipupuriro, Panguva yaakandorwa nenyika yeIj ipiti; Pandakanzwa rurimi rwandakanga ndisingazivi.</li>
      <li>Ndakabvisa mutoro pafudzi rake; Maoko ake akaregedza dengu.</li>
      <li>Iwe wakadana pakutambudzika, ndikakurwira; Ndakakupindura ndiri panovanda kutinhira; Ndakakuidza pamvura zhinji yeMeribha.</li>
      <li>Inzwai vanhu vangu, ndikupupurirei; Haiwa Isiraeri, dai waida hako kunditeerera!</li>
      <li>Ngakurege kuvapo pakati penyu mwari wokumwe; Musanamata kunomumwe mwari wavatorwa.</li>
      <li>Ndini Jehovha Mwari wako, Akakubudisa panyika yeIjipiti; Shamisa muromo wako kwazvo, ndigouzadza.</li>
      <li>Asi vanhu vangu havana kuteerera inzwi rangu; Isiraeri wakandiramba chose.</li>
      <li>Saka ndakavaregera paukukutu hwemoyo yavo, Kuti vafambe namano avo.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, dai vanhu vangu vainditeerera havo, Dai Isiraeri aifamba nenzira dzangu!</li>
      <li>Ndingadai ndakakurumidza kukunda vavengi vavo, Nokurova vadzivisi vavo noruoko rwangu.</li>
      <li>Vanovenga Jehovha vaizviisa pasi pake; Asi nguva yavo yaivapo nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Angadai aivadyisawo zviyo zvakaisvonaka; Ndaikugutsa nohuchi hunobva padombo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mwari anomira paungano yaMwari; Anotonga pakati pavamwari.</li>
      <li>Muchatonga zvisina kururama kusvikira rinhiko, Muchisanangura vanhu vakaipa?</li>
      <li>Tongerai mhaka dzavarombo nenherera; Ruramisirai vanotambudzika navanoshaiwa chose.</li>
      <li>Sunungurai varombo navashaiwi Varwirei paruoko rwowakaipa.</li>
      <li>Havazivi, havanzwisisi; Vanofamba-famba murima; Nheyo dzose dzapasi dzinozununguka.</li>
      <li>Ndakati, Muri vamwari, Mose muri vanakomana voWokumusorosoro.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro muchafa savanhu, Muchafa somumwe wamachinda.</li>
      <li>Simukai Mwari, mutongere pasi; Nokuti ndudzi dzose dzichava nhaka yenyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haiwa Jehovha, regai kuramba munyerere; Regai kuramba musingatauri, musanyarara Mwari.</li>
      <li>Nokuti tarirai, vavengi venyu vanoita bope; Vanokuvengai vakasimudza misoro yavo.</li>
      <li>Vanofunga mano kuti vanyengere vanhu venyu, Vanorangana pamusoro pavakavanzwa nemi.</li>
      <li>Vakati, Uyai, tivaparadze, varege kuzova rudzi; Kuti zita raIsiraeri rirege kuzorangarirwa.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vakarangana nomoyo mumwe; Vanoita sungano kuzorwa nemi.</li>
      <li>Matende aEdhomu navaIshimaeri, Moabhu navaHagari;</li>
      <li>Gebhari, naAmoni, naAmareki; Firisitia pamwechete navagere Tire;</li>
      <li>Asiriawo wakasangana navo; Vakabatsira vana vaRoti.</li>
      <li>Muvaitire sezvamakaitira Midhiani; NaSisera, naJabhini, paRwizi Kishoni;</li>
      <li>Ivo vakaparadzwa paEndori; Vakava mupfudze wapasi.</li>
      <li>Itai vakuru vavo saOrebhi naZeebhi; Zvirokwazvo machinda avo ose saZebha naZarimuna;</li>
      <li>Ivo vakati, Ngatizvitorere Ugaro hwaMwari huve hwedu.</li>
      <li>Mwari wangu, muvaite seguruva rinondeyeswa nemhepo; Samakoto anodzingwa nemhepo.</li>
      <li>Somoto unopisa dondo, Somurazvo womoto unopisa makomo;</li>
      <li>Muvateverere saizvozvo nedutu renyu remhepo, Muvavhunduse nechamupupuri chenyu.</li>
      <li>Fukidzai zviso zvavo nokunyadziswa; Kuti vatsvake zita renyu, Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Ngavanyadziswe, vavhunduswe nokusingaperi; Zvirokwazvo, ngavanyadziswe vafe;</li>
      <li>Vazive kuti imi moga, imi munezita rinonzi Jehovha, Ndimi Wokumusorosoro kumusoro kwapasi pose.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ugaro hwenyu hunodikanwa sei, Imi Jehovha wehondo!</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu unoshuva, zvirokwazvo unopanga vazhe dzaJehovha; moyo wangu nenyama yangu zvinodana kuna Mwari mupenyu.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, shiri yakazviwanira imba, Nyenganyenga yakazviwanira dendere, painoisa vana vayo, Ipo paaritari dzenyu, Jehovha wehondo, Mambo wangu, naMwari wangu.</li>
      <li>Vakaropafadzwa vanogara mumba menyu; Vachagara vachikurumbidzai.</li>
      <li>Akaropafadzwa munhu ane simba rake mamuri; Anemigwagwa inoenda Ziyoni mumoyo make.</li>
      <li>Kana vachipfuura nomumupata wakaoma, vanouita nzvimbo inamatsime; Zvirokwazvo, mvura yomunhuruka inoufukidza nemikomborero.</li>
      <li>Vanowedzera simba pasimba ravo, Mumwe nomumwe wavo anosvika pamberi paMwari paZiyoni.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, Jehovha wehondo, inzwa munyengetero wangu; teererai nenzeve, Mwari waJakobho.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, Mwari, nhovo yedu, Muone chiso chomuzodzwa wenyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti zuva rimwe pavazhe dzenyu rinokunda mamwe ane chiuru pakunaka. Ndinoti zviri nani kuti ndive murindi womukova mumba maMwari wangu, Pakuti ndigare pamatende avane zvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha Mwari izuva nenhovo; Jehovha achapa nyasha nokukudzwa; Hapana chinhu chakanaka chaanganyima vanofamba nokururama.</li>
      <li>Jehovha wehondo, Akaropafadzwa munhu anovimba nemi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, makafarira nyika yenyu; Makadzosa Jakobho pakutapwa.</li>
      <li>Makakanganwira kutadza kwavanhu venyu, Makafukidza zvivi zvavo zvose.</li>
      <li>Makabvisa kutsamwa kwenyu kwose; Makazvidzora pahasha dzenyu dzakanyanya.</li>
      <li>Tidzosei, Mwari muponesi wedu, Gumisai hasha dzenyu kwatiri.</li>
      <li>Ko mucharamba makatitsamwira nokusingaperi? Muchasvitsa kutsamwa kwenyu kumarudzi namarudzi here?</li>
      <li>Imi hamungatiraramisizve here, Kuti vanhu venyu vafare nemi?</li>
      <li>Tiratidzei ngoni dzenyu, Jehovha, Mutipe ruponeso rwenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndichanzwa zvichataura Mwari Jehovha; Nokuti achataura rugare kuvanhu vake nokuvatsvene vake; Asi ngavarege kudzokerazve kuupenzi.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo kuponesa kwake kuri pedo navanomutya; Kuti kubwinya kugare munyika yedu.</li>
      <li>Ngoni nezvokwadi zvakasangana; Kururama norugare zvakatsvodana.</li>
      <li>Zvokwadi zvinomera pasi; Kururama kwakatarira pasi kuri kudenga.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, Jehovha uchapa zvinhu zvakanaka; Nyika yedu ichabereka zvibereko zvayo.</li>
      <li>Kururama kuchamutungamirira; Kuchagadzirira tsoka dzake nzira.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Rerekai nzeve dzenyu, Jehovha, ndipindurei; Nokuti ndiri murombo nomushaiwi.</li>
      <li>Chengetai mweya wangu; nokuti ndiri mudikanwi wenyu; Haiwa Mwari wangu, ponesai muranda wenyu anovimba nemi.</li>
      <li>Ndinzwirei ngoni, Ishe; Nokuti ndinodana kwamuri zuva rose.</li>
      <li>Fadzai mweya womuranda wenyu; Nokuti ndinosimudzira mweya wangu kwamuri Ishe wangu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi, Ishe makanaka, munofarira kukanganwira, Mune ngoni zhinji kuna vose vanodana kwamuri.</li>
      <li>Rerekerai nzeve yenyu, Jehovha kumunyengetero wangu; Teererai inzwi rokukumbira kwangu.</li>
      <li>Pazuva rokutambudzika kwangu ndichadana kwamuri, Nokuti muchandipindura.</li>
      <li>Hapana akafanana nemi pakati pavamwari, Ishe, Uye hapana mabasa akafanana namabasa enyu.</li>
      <li>Ndudzi dzose dzamakaita dzichauya kuzonamata pamberi penyu, Ishe, Dzicharumbidza zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi muri mukuru, munoita Ndimi Mwari woga.</li>
      <li>Ndidzidzisei nzira yenyu, Jehovha, ndichafamba muzvokwadi yenyu, Batanidzai moyo wangu kuti nditye zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndichakurumbidzai, Ishe Mwari wangu, nomoyo wangu wose, Ndicharumbidza zita renyu nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ngoni dzenyu ihuru kwandiri; Makarwira mweya wangu pagomba rakadzika-dzika.</li>
      <li>Mwari, vanozvikudza vakandimukira, Ungano yavanhu, vanomanikidza, vakatsvaka mweya wangu, Havana kukuisai pamberi pavo.</li>
      <li>Asi imi, Ishe muri Mwari une tsitsi nenyasha, Hamukurumidzi kutsamwa, mune ngoni zhinji nezvokwadi.</li>
      <li>Ringirai kwandiri, mundinzwire ngoni; Ipai muranda wenyu simba renyu, Muponese mwanakomana womurandakadzi wenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndiratidzei chiratidzo mundiitire zvakanaka; Kuti vanondivenga vazvione, vanyadziswe; Nokuti imi Jehovha, makandibatsira nokundinyaradza.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Nheyo dzake dziri pamakomo matsvene.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anoda masuo eZiyoni Kupfuura pose panogara Jakobho.</li>
      <li>Zvinhu zvakanakisa zvinotaurwa pamusoro pako, Iwe guta raMwari.</li>
      <li>Rahabhi neBhabhironi ndichati vari pakati pavanondiziva; Tarirai, Firisitia, neTire, neItiopia; Munhu uyu akazvarirwako.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, pamusoro peZiyoni vachati, Uyu nouyo vakazvarirwamo; Naiye Wokumusorosoro amene acharisimbisa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha achaverenga, pakunyora kwake ndudzi, achiti, Munhu uyu akazvarirwako.</li>
      <li>Vanoimba navanotamba, vachati, Matsime angu ose ari mauri.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, Mwari muponesi wangu, Ndakachema masikati nousiku pamberi penyu;</li>
      <li>Munyengetero wangu ngaupinde pamberi penyu; Rerekerai nzeve yenyu munzwe kuchema kwangu;</li>
      <li>Nokuti mweya wangu uzere namatambudziko, Upenyu hwangu hwoswedera kuSheori.</li>
      <li>Ndinoverengwa pamwechete navanoburukira kugomba; Ndakafanana nomunhu anoshaiwa mubatsiri;</li>
      <li>Ndakarashirwa pakati pavakafa, Savakaurawa vavete mubwiro, Vamusati mucharangarira; Vakagurwa paruoko rwenyu.</li>
      <li>Makandiisa mugomba rakadzika-dzika, Panzvimbo dzine rima, makadzika kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Hasha dzenyu dzinorema kwazvo pamusoro pangu, Makanditambudza namafungu enyu ose.</li>
      <li>Makaisa vazikani vangu kure neni; Makandiita chinhu chinonyangadza kwavari; Ndakapfigirwa, handigoni kubuda.</li>
      <li>Ziso rangu ropera nemhaka yokutambudzika; Ndakadana kwamuri, Jehovha, zuva rimwe nerimwe, Ndakatambanudzira maoko angu kwamuri.</li>
      <li>Mungaitira vakafa zvinoshamisa here? Ko vakaparara vangamuka vakakurumbidzai here?</li>
      <li>Hunyoro hwenyu hungaparidzwa mubwiro here? Kana kutendeka kwenyu mukuparadza here?</li>
      <li>Zvishamiso zvenyu zvingazikanwa murima here? Nokururama kwenyu panyika yokukanganwa here?</li>
      <li>Asi ndakachema kwamuri, Jehovha, Munyengetero wangu uchasvika pamberi penyu mangwanani.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, munorashireiko mweya wangu? Munovanzireiko chiso chenyu kwandiri?</li>
      <li>Kubva pauduku hwangu ndakanga ndichitambudzwa ndichirwiso-fa; Kana ndichityiswa nemi ndinoshaiwa mano.</li>
      <li>Kutsamwa kwenyu kukuru kwakapfuura napamusoro pangu; Kutyisa kwenyu kwakandiparadza.</li>
      <li>Zvakandikomberedza zuva rose semvura; Zvakandipoteredza pamwechete.</li>
      <li>Iye, anondida, neshamwari yangu, makavaisa kure neni, Nomuzikani wangu ari murima.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndichaimba ndichireva ngoni dzaJehovha nokusingaperi; Ndichaparidza nomuromo wangu kutendeka kwenyu kumarudzi namarudzi.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndakati, Ngoni dzichavakwa nokusingaperi, Muchasimbisa kutendeka kwenyu mukudenga-denga mumene.</li>
      <li>Ndakaita sungano nomusanangurwa wangu, Ndakapika kumuranda wangu Dhavhidhi, ndichiti,</li>
      <li>Ndichamisa vana vako nokusingaperi, Nokuvaka chigaro chako choushe kusvikira kumarudzi namarudzi.</li>
      <li>Kudenga-denga kucharumbidza zvishamiso zvenyu, Jehovha; Nokutendeka kwenyuwo paungano yavatsvene.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndianiko mudenga rose angaenzaniswa naJehovha? Ndianiko pakati pavanakomana vaMwari akafanana naJehovha?</li>

      <li>Ndimi munobata kuzvikudza kwegungwa; Kana mafungu aro achisimuka, ndimi munoanyaradza.</li>
      <li>Makaputsanya Rahabhi, somunhu akaurawa; Makaparadzira vavengi venyu noruoko rwenyu rune simba.</li>
      <li>Kudenga-denga ndokwenyu, napasi ndopenyuwo; Nyika nezvose zvayo, ndimi makazviteya.</li>
      <li>Kumusoro nenyasi, ndimi makazvisika; Tabhori neHerimoni anofara nezita renyu.</li>
      <li>Munoruoko rune simba; Chanza chenyu chine simba, ruoko rwenyu rworudyi rwakasimudzwa.</li>
      <li>Kururama nokururamisa ndidzo nheyo dzechigaro chenyu choushe; Ngoni nezvokwadi zvinokutungamirirai.</li>
      <li>Vakaropafadzwa vanhu vanoziva inzwi romufaro; Vanofamba, Jehovha, muchiedza chechiso chenyu.</li>
      <li>Vanofara muzita renyu zuva rose; Vanosimudzwa nokururama kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi muri kubwinya kwesimba ravo; Runyanga rwedu ruchasimudzwa netsitsi dzenyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti nhovo yedu ndeyaJehovha; Namambo wedu ndowoMutsvene waIsiraeri.</li>
      <li>Panguva iyo makataura navatsvene venyu pakuzviratidza kwenyu, Mukati, Ndakabatsira mhare; Ndakasimudza mumwe wakasanangurwa pakati pavanhu.</li>
      <li>Ndakawana Dhavhidhi muranda wangu; Ndakamuzodza namafuta angu matsvene;</li>
      <li>Chanza changu chichasimbiswa naye; Ruoko rwanguvo ruchamusimbisa.</li>
      <li>Muvengi haangamumanikidzi; Mwanakomana wezvakaipa haangamutambudzi.</li>
      <li>Ndichaparadza vadzivisi vake pamberi pake, Ndicharova vanomuvenga.</li>
      <li>Asi kutendeka kwangu nengoni dzangu zvichava naye; Runyanga rwake ruchasimudzwa nezita rangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichaisawo ruoko rwake pamusoro pegungwa, Noruoko rwake rworudyi pamusoro penzizi.</li>
      <li>Iye achadana kwandiri, achiti, Ndimi baba vangu, Mwari wangu, nedombo rokuponeswa kwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichamuitawo dangwe rangu, Mukuru wamadzimambo apasi.</li>
      <li>Ndichamuchengetera ngoni dzangu nokusingaperi, Sungano yangu icharamba yakasimba kwaari.</li>
      <li>Vana vake ndichavagarisawo nokusingaperi, Chigaro chake choushe chichafanana namazuva okudenga.</li>
      <li>Kana vana vake vakasiya murayiro wangu, Vakasafamba nezvandakatonga;</li>
      <li>Kana vakazvidza zvandakatema, Vakasachengeta mirau yangu;</li>
      <li>Ipapo ndichavaranga neshamhu pamusoro pokudarika kwavo, Uye nokurova pamusoro pokuipa kwavo.</li>
      <li>Asi handingamutoreri unyoro hwangu chose, Kana kutendera kutendeka kwangu kuitiswa nhema.</li>
      <li>Sungano yangu handingaizvidzi, Kana kushandura chinhu chakabuda pamuromo wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakapika kamwe chete neutsvene hwangu; Handingarevi nhema kuna Dhavhidhi;</li>
      <li>Vana vake vachavapo nokusingaperi, Chigaro chake choushe chichafanana nezuva pamberi pangu.</li>
      <li>Chichasimbiswa nokusingaperi somwedzi, Sechapupu chakatendeka chiri kudenga.</li>
      <li>Asi imi makarasha nokuramba, Makatsamwira muzodzwa wenyu.</li>
      <li>Makasema sungano yomuranda wenyu; Makazvidza korona yake mukaikandira pasi.</li>
      <li>Makaputsa madziro ake ose; Makaita nhare dzake matongo.</li>
      <li>Vose vanopfuura nenzira vanopamba nhumbi dzake; Wava chinhu chinosekwa navaanogara navo.</li>
      <li>Makasimudza ruoko rworudyi rwavadzivisi vake; Makafadza vavengi vake vose.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, munodzosa munondo wake unopinza, Hamuna kumusimbisa pakurwa.</li>
      <li>Makagumisa kubwinya kwake, Makawisira pasi chigaro chake choushe.</li>
      <li>Makatapudza mazuva ohujaya hwake; Makamufukidza nokunyara.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, muchazvivanza nokusingaperi kusvikira rinhiko? Kutsamwa kwenyu kuchapisa somoto kusvikira rinhiko?</li>
      <li>Haiwa, rangarirai kuti nguva yangu ipfupi kwazvo; Kuti makasikira vana vavanhu vose zvinhu zvisina maturo kwazvo!</li>
      <li>Ndoupiko munhu angararama akasaona kufa, Angarwira mweya wake pasimba reSheori here?</li>
      <li>Ishe, unyoro hwenyu hwakare huripiko, Hwamakapika kuna Dhavhidhi nokutendeka kwenyu here?</li>
      <li>Rangarirai, Ishe, kushorwa kwavaranda venyu; Kuti ndinotakura muchipfuva changu kushora kwavanhu vazhinji;</li>
      <li>Uko kwakashora vavengi venyu nako, Jehovha, Kwavakashora nako makwara omuzodzwa wenyu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ngaavongwe nokusingaperi. Ameni, zvirokwazvo, Ameni.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ishe, makanga muri ugaro hwedu Pamarudzi namarudzi.</li>
      <li>Makomo asati azvarwa, Musati matongosika nyika nevhu, Kubva pakusingaperi kusvikira pakusingaperi imi muri Mwari.</li>
      <li>Munodzosera munhu kuguruva; Muchiti, Dzokai vana vavanhu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti kwamuri makore ane chiuru Akangofanana nezuva razuro kana rapfuura, Senguva yokurinda yousiku.</li>
      <li>Munovakukura semvura zhinji; vava sehope; Mangwanani vakaita souswa hunomera.</li>
      <li>Mangwanani hunotumbuka, hunomera; Madekwana hunodzurwa, ndokusvava.</li>
      <li>Nokuti tinopedzwa nokutsamwa kwenyu, Tinotambudzika nehasha dzenyu.</li>
      <li>Makaisa zvakaipa zvedu pamberi penyu, Zvivi zvedu zvakavanzika pachiedza chechiso chenyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti mazuva edu ose anopfuura makatsamwa; Makore edu anopera sorungano.</li>
      <li>Mazuva amakore edu anosvika makore makumi manomwe, Kana tine simba makore makumi masere; Asi kunyange achikudzwa ndiko kutambudzika nenhamo bedzi. Nokuti gare-gare aenda, nesu tabhururuka taenda.</li>
      <li>Ndianiko anoziva simba rokutsamwa kwenyu, Nehasha dzenyu, kuti mutyiwe zvakafanira here?</li>
      <li>Tidzidzisei kunatsoverenga mazuva edu, Kuti tizviwanire moyo wakachenjera.</li>
      <li>Dzokai Jehovha; kusvikira rinhiko? Muzvidembe pamusoro pavaranda venyu.</li>
      <li>Tigutsei mangwanani nengoni dzenyu; Kuti tifarise, tive nomufaro mazuva edu ose.</li>
      <li>Tifadzei zvinoenzana namazuva amakatitambudza, Namakore atakaona zvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Zvamakaita ngazvionekwe navaranda venyu, Nokubwinya kwenyu pamusoro pavana vavo.</li>
      <li>Kunaka kwaJehovha Mwari wedu ngakuve pamusoro pedu; Mutisimbisire basa ramaoko edu; Zvirokwazvo, basa ramaoko edu murisimbise.</li>
    </ol>

      <li>Uyo agere panzvimbo yokuvanda yoWokumusorosoro Acharambira pamumvuri wowaMasimbaose.</li>

      <li>Kana hosha inofamba murima, Kana kuparadza kunouraya masikati.</li>

      <li>Zvaakandida, ndichamurwira; Ndichamuisa pakakwirira, nokuti wakaziva zita rangu.</li>

      <li>Zvakanaka kuvonga Jehovha, Nokuimbira zita renyu nziyo dzokurumbidza, imi Wokumusorosoro;</li>

      <li>Jehovha anobata ushe; akafuka umambo; Jehovha akafuka simba, akazvisunga chiuno naro; Nyikawo yakateyiwa, haingazununguswi.</li>
      <li>Chigaro chenyu choushe chakasimbiswa kubva kare; Imi muripo kubva pakusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, Nzizi dzakanzwisa manzwi adzo; Nzizi dzinonzwisa kutinhira kwadzo.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, Mwari mutsivi, Imi Mwari mutsivi, penyai.</li>
      <li>Zvisimudzei, imi Mutongi wenyika; Ipai vanozvikudza sezvavakafanira.</li>

      <li>Vanouraya chirikadzi nomweni, Nenherera vanodziuraya.</li>

      <li>Iye,anoranga vahedheni, haangarairi here? Iye, anodzidzisa vanhu zivo?</li>
      <li>Jehovha anoziva kufunga kwavanhu,) Kuti hazvina maturo.</li>
      <li>Akaropafadzwa munhu, anorangwa nemi, Jehovha, lye wamunodzidzisa pamurayiro wenyu;</li>
      <li>Kuti mumuzorodzei pamazuva okutambudzika, Kusvikira vakaipa vachererwa gomba.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha haangarashi vanhu vake, Uye haangasiyi nhaka yake.</li>
      <li>Nokuti kutonga kuchadzokera kukururama; Vose vane moyo yakarurama vachakutevera.</li>
      <li>Ndianiko achandirwira pavaiti vezvakaipa? Ndianiko achandibatsira panavanoita zvakaipa?</li>
      <li>Dai Jehovha aisava mubatsiri wangu, Mweya wangu ungadai wakakurumidza kugara pakati mwii.</li>
      <li>Panguva yandakati, Rutsoka rwangu rwotedzemuka, Ngoni dzenyu,Jehovha, dzakanditsigira.</li>
      <li>Mundangariro dzangu zhinji mukati mangu Kunyaradza kwenyu kunofadza mweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Chigaro chezvakaipa chingashamwaridzana nemi here, Icho chinofunga kuita zvakashata nemitemo yacho?</li>
      <li>Vanounganira upenyu hwowakarurama, Vachipa mhosva ropa risina mhosva.</li>
      <li>Asi Jehovha ndiye nhare yangu yakasimba; Mwari wangu idombo routiziro hwangu.</li>
      <li>Achadzosera pamusoro pavo kutadza kwavo, Achavaparadza pakati pokuita kwavo; Jehovha Mwari wedu achavaparadza.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Uyai, tiimbire Jehovha; Ngatipururudzei dombo rokuponeswa kwedu.</li>
      <li>Ngatisvike pamberi pake tichivonga, Ngatimupururudzirei namapisarema,</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha ndiMwari mukuru, ,Mambo mukuru anokunda vamwari vose.</li>
      <li>Nzvimbo dzakadzika dzapasi dziri muruoko rwake; Misoro yamakomo ndeyakewo.</li>
      <li>Gungwa nderake, ndiye akariita; Maoko ake akaumba nyika yakaoma.</li>
      <li>Uyai, tinamate tikotamire pasi; Ngatipfugame pamberi paJehovha Muiti wedu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndiye Mwari wedu, Isu tiri vanhu vanofudzwa naye, namakwai oruoko rwake. Nhasi dai muchinzwa henyu inzwi rake!</li>
      <li>Regai kuomesa moyo yenyu sapaMeribha, Sapazuva reMasa murenje;</li>
      <li>Panguva yandakaidzwa namadzibaba enyu, Vakandiidza, vakaona zvandakaita.</li>
      <li>Ndakanza ndine shungu pamusoro porudzi urwo makore makumi mana, Ndikati, Ndivanhu vakarashika pamoyo yavo, Havana kuziva nzira dzangu;</li>
      <li>Saka ndakapika pakutsamwa kwangu, ndikati, Havangazopindi pazororo rangu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Imbirai Jehovha rwiyo rutsva; Imbirai Jehovha, pasi pose.</li>
      <li>Imbirai Jehovha, rumbidzai zita rake; Paridzai kuponesa kwake zuva rimwe nerimwe.</li>
      <li>Dudzirai kubwinya kwake pakati pavahedheni, Mabasa ake, anoshamisa pakati pendudzi dzose.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha mukuru, anofanira kurumbidzwa kwazvo; Anofanira kutyiwa kupfuura vamwari vose.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vamwari vose vendudzi zvifananidzo hazvo; Asi Jehovha akaita kudenga-denga.</li>
      <li>Kukudzwa noumambo zviri pamberi pake; Simba nokunaka zviri panzvimbo yake tsvene.</li>
      <li>Ipai Jehovha, imi mhuri dzavanhu, Ipai Jehovha kukudzwa nesimba.</li>
      <li>Ipai Jehovha kukudzwa kunofanira zita rake; Uyai nechipiriso, mupinde muvazhe dzake.</li>
      <li>Namatai kuna Jehovha nenguva tsvene; Pasi pose panobvunda pamberi pake.</li>
      <li>Itiyi pakati pavahedheni, Jehovha ndiye anobata ushe; Nyikawo yakasimbiswa, kuti irege kuzununguswa; Iye achatonga vanhu zvakarurama.</li>
      <li>Kudenga-denga ngakufare, kwazvo; Gungwa ngaritinhire, nezvose zviri mukati maro;</li>
      <li>Sango ngarive nomufaro, nezvose zviri mukati maro; Ipapo miti yose yedondo ichaimba nomufaro;</li>
      <li>Pamberi paJehovha, nokuti anouya; Nokuti anouya kuzotonga pasi; uchatonga nyika zvakarurama, Nendudzi nokutendeka kwake.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha anobata ushe; nyika ngaifare kwazvo; Zviwi zvizhinji ngazvifare.</li>
      <li>Makore nerima zvinomukomberedza; Kururama nokururamisa ndidzo nheyo dzechigaro chake choushe.</li>
      <li>Moto unotungamira pamberi pake, Uchipisa vadzivisi vake pamativi ose.</li>
      <li>Mheni dzake dzakavheneka nyika yose; Pasi pakaona, ndokubvunda.</li>
