      <li>Makomo akanyauka senamo pamberi paJehovha, Pamberi paShe wapasi pose.</li>
      <li>Kudenga-denga kunoparidza kururama kwake, Ndudzi dzose dzakaona kubwinya kwake.</li>
      <li>Vose, vanoshumira mifananidzo yakaveziwa, vanonyadziswa, Ivo vanozvirumbidza pamusoro pezvifananidzo; Namatai kwaari, imi vamwari vose</li>
      <li>Ziyoni rakanzwa ndokufara, Navakunda vaJudha vakafara kwazvo; Nokuda kwezvamakatonga, imi Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi Jehovha, muri kumusoro-soro kwapasi pose; Makakwirira kupfuura vamwari vose.</li>
      <li>Vengai zvakaipa, imi munoda Jehovha; Iye anochengeta mweya yavatsvene vake; Unovarwira paruoko rwawakaipa.</li>
      <li>Chiedza chinodzvarirwa wakarurama, Nomufaro vane moyo yakarurama.</li>
      <li>Farai munaJehovha, imi vakarurama; Vongai pakurangarira utsvene hwake.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Imbirai Jehovha rwiyo rutsva; Nokuti akaita zvinhu zvinoshamisa; Chanza chake chorudyi, noruoko rwake rutsvene, zvakamukundisa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha akazivisa kuponesa kwake; Akaratidza pachena kururama kwake pamberi pavahedheni.</li>
      <li>Akarangarira ngoni dzake nokutendeka kwake kuimba yaIsiraeri; Migumo yose yapasi yakaona kuponesa kwaMwari wedu.</li>
      <li>Pururudzirai Jehovha, pasi pose; Danidzirai, muimbe nomufaro, imbai nziyo dzokurumbidza.</li>
      <li>Imbirai Jehovha nziyo dzokurumbidza nembira; Nembira, uye nenzwi rokuimba.</li>
      <li>Nehwamanda, nenzwi romumanzi Pururudzai pamberi paMambo, Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Gungwa ngaritinhire nezvose zviri mukati maro; Nenyika, navanogaramo.</li>
      <li>Nzizi ngadziuchire; Namakomo ngaaimbe pamwechete nomufaro;</li>
      <li>Pamberi paJehovha, nokuti anouya kuzotonga pasi, Achatonga nyika zvakarurama, Navanhu nokururama.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha anobata ushe; vanhu ngavabvunde; Iye agere pakati pamakerubhi; nyika ngaizununguswe.</li>
      <li>Jehovha mukuru paZiyoni; Ari kumusoro-soro kwavanhu vose.</li>
      <li>Ngavarumbidze zita renyu guru rinotyisa; Ndiye Mutsvene.</li>
      <li>Simba ramambo rinodawo kururamisa; Imi munosimbisa kururama, Munotonga muchiruramisa pakati paJakobho.</li>
      <li>Kudzai Jehovha Mwari wedu, Munamate pachitsiko chetsoka dzake; Ndiye Mutsvene.</li>
      <li>Mozisi naAroni pakati pavapirisiti vake, NaSamueri pakati pavanodana zita rake; Vakadana kuna Jehovha, iye akavapindura.</li>
      <li>Akataura navo ari mushongwe yegore; Vakachengeta zvipupuriro zvake nomutemo waakavapa.</li>
      <li>Makavapindura, Jehovha Mwari wedu; Maiva Mwari aivakanganwira, Kunyange makatsiva zvavaiita.</li>
      <li>Kudzai Jehovha Mwari wedu, Namatai pagomo rake dzvene; Nokuti Jehovha Mwari wedu ndiye Mutsvene.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pururudzai Jehovha, imi nyika dzose.</li>
      <li>Shumirai Jehovha nomufaro; Uyai pamberi pake muchiimba.</li>
      <li>Zivai kuti Jehovha ndiye Mwari; Ndiye wakatiita, tiri vanhu vake; Tiri vanhu vake, namakwai anofudzwa naye.</li>
      <li>Pindai pamasuo ake muchivonga, Napavazhe dzake muchirumbidza; Chimuvongai, murumbidze zita rake.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha akanaka; ngoni dzake dziripo nokusingaperi; Nokutendeka kwake kumarudzi namarudzi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndichaimba ndichireva ngoni nokururama; Ndimi Jehovha wandichaimbira nziyo dzokurumbidza.</li>
      <li>Ndichaita zvose nokugwara panzira yakarurama; Haiwa, muchauya kwandiri rinhiko? Ndichafamba mumba mangu nomoyo wakarurama.</li>
      <li>Handingavavariri chinhu chakaipa; Ndinovenga zvinoitwa navanotsauka; Hazvingandinamatiri.</li>
      <li>moyo wakatsauka ngaubve kwandiri; Handidi kuziva zvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Anoitira vokwake makuhwa, ndichamuparadza; Anotarira namanyawi, nounomoyo unozvikudza, handingavi nehanya naye.</li>
      <li>meso angu achatarira vakatendeka panyika, kuti vagare neni; Munhu anofamba nenzira yakarurama, ndiye angava mushumiri wangu.</li>
      <li>Anonyengera haangagari mumba mangu; Anoreva nhema haangarambiri pamberi pangu.</li>
      <li>Mangwanani ose ndichaparadza vakaipa vose venyika; Kuti ndipedze vose vanoita zvakaipa paguta raJehovha.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Inzwai munyengetero wangu, Jehovha, Kuchema kwangu ngakusvikire kwamuri.</li>
      <li>Regai kundivanzira chiso chenyu pazuva rokutambudzika kwangu; Rerekerai nzeve yenyu kwandiri; Pazuva rokudana kwangu kurumidzai kundipindura.</li>
      <li>Nokuti mazuva angu anopera soutsi, Mapfupa angu anotsva sechitsa.</li>
      <li>moyo wangu warohwa souswa, waoma; Nokuti ndinokanganwa kudya zvokudya zvangu.</li>
      <li>Nokuda kwenzwi rokugomera kwangu Mapfupa angu anonamatira nyama yangu.</li>
      <li>Ndafanana nehukurwizi yomurenje; Ndava sezizi romumatongo.</li>
      <li>Handivati, ndafanana Neshiri iri yoga pamusoro pedenga reimba.</li>
      <li>Vavengi vangu vanondituka zuva rose; Avo vanondipengera vanonditukisa kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndakadya madota sezvokudya, Ndikavhenganisa zvokunwa zvangu nemisodzi.</li>
      <li>Nokuda kwehasha dzenyu nokutsamwa kwenyu; Nokuti makandisimudza mukandirasha.</li>
      <li>Mazuva angu akafanana nomumvuri wareba; Ndaoma souswa.</li>
      <li>Asi imi Jehovha, muchavapo nokusingaperi; Marudzi namarudzi achakurangarirai.</li>
      <li>Imi muchasimuka, mukanzwira Ziyoni ngoni; Nokuti nguva yavapo yokurinzwira tsitsi, zvirokwazvo, nguva, yakatarwa, yasvika.</li>
      <li>Nokuti varanda venyu vanofarira mabwe aro, Vanonzwira tsitsi guruva raro.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo vahedheni vachatya zita raJehovha, Namadzimambo ose apasi kubwinya kwenyu;</li>
      <li>Jehovha zvaakavaka Ziyoni, Akaonekwa nokubwinya kwake;</li>
      <li>Akava nehanya nomunyengetero wavakakamurwa, Akasazvidza munyengetero wavo.</li>
      <li>Izvi zvichanyorerwa rudzi runozouya; Vanhu, vachazosikwa, vacharumbidza Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Nokuti wakatarira pasi ari panzvimbo yake tsvene yakakwirira; Jehovha akacherekedza nyika ari kudenga;</li>
      <li>Kuti anzwe kugomera kwomusungwa; Kuti asunungure vana vorufu;</li>
      <li>Kuti vanhu vaparidze zita raJehovha paZiyoni, Nokurumbidzwa kwake paJerusaremu;</li>
      <li>Kana marudzi avanhu aungana, Noushe huzhinji, kuti vashumire Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Wakatapudza simba rangu panzira; Wakafupisa mazuva angu.</li>
      <li>Ndakati, Mwari wangu, regai kundibvisa mazuva angu achigere kusvika; Makore enyu anosvika kumarudzi namarudzi.</li>
      <li>Makateya nyika kare-kare; Nedenga rose ibasa ramaoko enyu.</li>
      <li>Zvichaparara izvo, asi imi muchagara muripo; Zvirokwazvo, izvozvo zvose zvichasakara senguvo; Muchazvishandura sechisimiro, zvikashanduka;</li>
      <li>Asi imi hamushanduki, Makore enyu haangavi nomugumo.</li>
      <li>Vana vavaranda venyu vachagara varipo, Navana vavo vachasimbiswa pamberi penyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Rumbidzai Jehovha, mweya wangu; Zvose zviri mukati mangu ngazvirumbidze zita rake dzvene.</li>
      <li>Rumbidza Jehovha, mweya wangu, Urege kukanganwa mikomborero yake;</li>
      <li>Iye, anokanganwira zvakaipa zvako zvose; Anoporesa kurwara kwako kwose;</li>
      <li>Anodzikunura hupenyu hwako pakuparadzwa; Anokuisa korona younyoro nengoni;</li>
      <li>Anogutisa moyo wako nezvakanaka; Kuti utsva hwako huvandudzwe segondo.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anoita zvinhu zvakarurama, Nokururamisira vose vanomanikidzwa.</li>
      <li>Akazivisa Mozisi nzira dzake, Navana vaIsiraeri zvaakaita.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anetsitsi nenyasha, Haachimbidziki kutsamwa, ane ngoni zhinji.</li>
      <li>Haangarambi achirwa; Uye haangarambi akatsamwa nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Haana kutiitira sezvakafanira zvivi zvedu, Kana kutipa mubayiro sezvakafanira zvakaipa zvedu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti sokukwirira kwokudenga kumusoro, Ndizvo zvakaita kukura kwengoni dzake kuna vanomutya.</li>
      <li>Sokuva kure kwamabvazuva namavirira, Saizvozvo akabvisa kudarika kwedu kwose kure nesu.</li>
      <li>Sokunzwira tsitsi kwababa vana vake, Saizvozvo Jehovha anonzwira tsitsi vanomutya.</li>
      <li>Nokuti iye anoziva chatakaitwa nacho, Anorangarira kuti tiri guruva.</li>
      <li>Kana ari munhu, mazuva ake akaita souswa; Seruva resango, iye anokura saizvozvo.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imhepo inopfuura pamusoro paro, onei raenda; Nenzvimbo yaro haicharizivi.</li>
      <li>Asi ngoni dzaJehovha dziripo nokusingaperi-peri kuna vanomutya, Nokururama kwake kuvana vavana vavo;</li>
      <li>kuna ivo vanochengeta sungano yake, Nokuna vanorangarira zvaakaraira, kuti vazviite.</li>
      <li>Jehovha akasimbisa chigaro chake choushe kudenga-denga; Ushe hwake hunobata zvinhu zvose.</li>
      <li>Rumbidzai Jehovha, imi vatumwa vake; Imi mhare dzine simba, munoita zvaakataura, Muchiteerera inzwi reshoko rake.</li>
      <li>Rumbidzai Jehovha, imi hondo dzake dzose; Imi vashumiri vake, vanoita zvinomufadza.</li>
      <li>Rumbidzai Jehovha, imi mabasa ake ose, Panzvimbo dzose dzoumambo hwake; Rumbidza Jehovha, mweya wangu!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Rumbidza Jehovha, mweya wangu! Jehovha Mwari wangu, muri mukuru kwazvo; Makafukidzwa nokukudzwa noumambo.</li>
      <li>Imi munozvifukidza nechiedza sechisimiro; Munotatamura kudenga-denga somucheka wetende;</li>
      <li>Ndiye anoteya matanda edzimba dzake mumvura; Anoita makore ngoro yake; Anofamba pamusoro pamapapiro emhepo</li>
      <li>Anoita mhepo nhume dzake; Nomoto, unopfuta, vashumiri vake;</li>
      <li>Akateya nheyo dzapasi; Kuti parege kuzununguswa nokusingaperi,</li>
      <li>Makapafukidza nemvura yakadzika sechisimiro; Mvura zhinji yakamira pamusoro pamakomo,</li>
      <li>Makati muchituka ikatiza; inzwi rokutinhira kwenyu rakati richinzwika, ikachimbidzika kuenda.</li>
      <li>Makomo akakwira, mipata yakaderera; Ikaenda kunzvimbo yamakaigadzirira,</li>
      <li>Makaitarira muganho, kuti irege kudarika; Kuti irege kudzoka kuzofukidza pasizve.</li>
      <li>Anotuma matsime mumipata; Mvura inoyerera napakati pamakomo;</li>
      <li>Anonwisa mhuka dzose dzesango; Mbizi dzinopedza nyota yadzo.</li>
      <li>Shiri dzokudenga dzinogara paari, Dzinorira pakati pamatavi.</li>
      <li>Anodiridza makomo ari padzimba dzake; Pasi panogutiswa nechibereko chamabasa enyu.</li>
      <li>Anomeresa uswa hwezvipfuwo, Nemiriwo, inobatsira vanhu; Kuti abudise zvokudya pasi;</li>
      <li>Newaini inofadza moyo womunhu, Namafuta anobwinyisa chiso chake, Nechingwa chinosimbisa moyo womunhu.</li>
      <li>Miti yaJehovha inoguta; Iyo misidhari yeRebhanoni yaakasima;</li>
      <li>Apo panovaka shiri matendere adzo, Kana riri zimudo, miti yemisipiresi ndiyo imba yaro.</li>
      <li>Makomo marefu ndeetsoma; Matombo ndihwo utiziro hwembira.</li>
      <li>Akatara mwedzi kuti uratidze nguva; Zuva rinoziva nguva yokuvira kwaro.</li>
      <li>Munoita rima, usiku ndokuvapo; Panguva iyo mhuka dzose dzedondo dzinobuda.</li>
      <li>Vana veshumba vanoomba vachitsvaka zvavangauraya, Vanotsvaka zvokudya zvavo kuna Mwari.</li>
      <li>Kana zuva richibuda, dzinoenda hadzo, Dzichindovata mumapako adzo.</li>
      <li>Zvino munhu obudira kubasa rake. Nokumurimo wake kusvikira madekwana.</li>
      <li>Haiwa Jehovha, mabasa enyu mazhinji sei! Makaaita ose nenjere; Pasi pazere nefuma yenyu.</li>
      <li>Hero gungwa, rakakura ibamhi, Mukati maro mune zvinhu zvinokambaira zvisingagoni kuverengwa, Zvipenyu zviduku nezvikuru.</li>
      <li>Hezvo zvikepe, zvinofamba; Heyo ngwena yamakaumba, kuti itambe mariri.</li>
      <li>Izvi zvose zvinokumirirai, Kuti muzvipe zvokudya zvazvo nenguva yakafanira.</li>
      <li>Zvamunozvipa imi, ndizvo zvazvinounganidza; Munotadzanura ruoko rwenyu, izvo ndokuguta nezvakanaka.</li>
      <li>Munovanza chiso chenyu, izvo ndokuvhunduswa; Munozvitorera mweya wazvo, izvo ndokufa, Zvichidzokera kuguruva razvo.</li>
      <li>Munotuma mweya wenyu, izvo ndokusikwa; Munovandudza chiso chevhu.</li>
      <li>Kubwinya kwaJehovha ngakugare nokusingaperi; Jehovha ngaafarire mabasa ake;</li>
      <li>Iye anotarira pasi, ipo ndokubvunda; Unonyangata makomo, iwo ndokubudisa utsi.</li>
      <li>Ndichaimbira Jehovha panguva yose youpenyu hwangu; Ndichaimbira Mwari wangu nziyo dzokurumbidza ndichiripo.</li>
      <li>Kurangarira kwangu ngakumufadze; Ndichafara kwazvo muna Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Vatadzi ngavaparadzwe pasi, Navakaipa ngavarege kuzovapo. Rumbidzai Jehovha, mweya wangu. Hareruya</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vongai Jehovha, mudane zita rake; Zivisai zvaakaita pakati pendudzi dzavanhu.</li>
      <li>Muimbirei, mumuimbire nziyo dzokukudza; Rondedzerai mabasa ake ose anoshamisa.</li>
      <li>Zvirumbidzei muzita rake dzvene; moyo yavanotsvaka Jehovha ngaifare kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Tsvakai Jehovha nesimba rake; Tsvakai chiso chake nguva dzose.</li>
      <li>Rangarirai mabasa ake anoshamisa, aakaita; Zvishamiso zvake, nezvaakatonga nomuromo wake;</li>
      <li>Imi vana vaAbhurahamu, muranda wake, Imi vanakomana vaJakobho, vasanangurwa vake.</li>
      <li>Ndiye Jehovha Mwari wedu; Zvaakatonga zviri pasi pose.</li>
      <li>Wakarangarira sungano yake nokusingaperi, Iro shoko raakaraira kumarudzi ane chiuru;</li>
      <li>Iyo sungano yaakaita naAbhurahamu, Nemhiko yake kuna Isaka.</li>
      <li>Akazvisimbisira Jakobho, kuti uve mutemo, Kuna Isiraeri kuti ive sungano isingaperi;</li>
      <li>Achiti, Ndichakupa iwe nyika yeKanani, Uve mugove wenhaka yenyu;</li>
      <li>Panguva yavakanga vachiri varume vashoma pakuverengwa, Zvirokwazvo, vashoma kwazvo, navatorwa mairi;</li>
      <li>Vakafamba-famba vachibva kuno rumwe rudzi vachienda kuno rumwe, Nokubva kunoumwe ushe vachienda kuna vamwe vanhu.</li>
      <li>Haana kutendera munhu kuvaitira zvakaipa; Zvirokwazvo, wakatuka madzimambo nokuda kwavo;</li>
      <li>Achiti, Musagunzva vazodzwa vangu, Navaporofita vangu musavaitira chakaipa.</li>
      <li>Akadana nzara kuti iuye panyika; Akavhuna mudonzvo wose wechingwa.</li>
      <li>Akatuma murume pamberi pavo; Josefa akatengeswa akava muranda;</li>
      <li>Vakakuvadza tsoka dzake nezvisungo zvesimbi, Akasungwa namaketani amatare;</li>
      <li>Kusvikira panguva yakaitika shoko rake; Shoko raJehovha rakamuidza.</li>
      <li>Mambo akatuma nhume akamusunungura; Mubati wendudzi dzavanhu, akamuregedza.</li>
      <li>Akamuita ishe weimba yake, Nomubati wefuma yake yose;</li>
      <li>Kuti araire machinda ake nokuda kwake, Nokudzidzisa vakuru vake huchenjeri.</li>
      <li>Isiraeri akasvikawo Ijipiti, NaJakobho wakagara ari mutorwa panyika yaHamu.</li>
      <li>Akawanza vanhu vake kwazvo, Akavapa simba rakapfuura ravadzivisi vavo.</li>
      <li>Wakashandura moyo yavo kuti vavenge vanhu vake, Kuti vanyengere varanda vake.</li>
      <li>Akatuma Mozisi muranda wake, NaAroni waakanga asanangura.</li>
      <li>Ivo vakaratidza zviratidzo zvake pakati pavo, Nezvishamiso panyika yaHamu.</li>
      <li>Akatuma rima, akaisvibisa; Vakasamukira mashoko ake.</li>
      <li>Akashandura mvura yavo yose, ikaita ropa, Akauraya hove dzavo.</li>
      <li>Nyika yavo yakazara namatatya, Mudzimba dzamadzimambo avo.</li>
      <li>Akataura, mapupira enhunzi akasvika, Nenda panyika yavo yose.</li>
      <li>Akavapa chimvuramabwe panzvimbo yemvura, Uye moto wakapfuta munyika yavo.</li>
      <li>Wakarovawo mizambiringa yavo nemionde yavo; Akavhuna-vhunawo miti yenyika yavo</li>
      <li>Akataura, mhashu dzikasvika, Namagwatakwata asingagoni kuverengwa.</li>
      <li>Zvikapedza miriwo yose munyika yavo, Nokupedza zvibereko zvevhu ravo.</li>
      <li>Akarovawo matangwe ose munyika yavo, Ivo vokutanga vesimba ravo rose.</li>
      <li>Akavabudisa vane sirivha nendarama; Kwakanga kusina nomumwe pakati pamarudzi avo wakashaiwa simba.</li>
      <li>Nyika yeIjipiti yakafara pakubva kwavo, Nokuti vakanga vabatwa nokutya nokuda kwavo.</li>
      <li>Wakatatamura gore rikava chifukidzo; Nomoto kuzovhenekera usiku.</li>
      <li>Vakakumbira, akauyisa zvihuta, Akavagutisa nechingwa chakabva kudenga.</li>
      <li>Akazarura dombo, mvura zhinji ikadzutuka; Ikayerera pakanga pakaoma sorwizi.</li>
      <li>Nokuti akarangarira shoko rake dzvene, NaAbhurahamu muranda wake.</li>
      <li>Akabudisa vanhu vake nomufaro, Navasanangurwa vake vachiimba.</li>
      <li>Akavapa nyika dzavahedheni; Vakazvitorera zvakanga zvabatwa nendudzi dzavanhu;</li>
      <li>Kuti vachengete zvaakatema, Nokuteerera mirairo yake. Hareruya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya. Vongai Jehovha, nokuti akanaka; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Ndianiko angareva zvinhu zvine simba zvakaitwa naJehovha, Kana kududzira kurumbidza kwake kwose?</li>
      <li>Vakaropafadzwa vanochengeta kururama, Naiye anoita zvakarurama nguva dzose.</li>
      <li>Ndirangarirei Jehovha, nounyoro hwamunahwo kuvanhu venyu; Ndishanyirei noruponeso rwenyu.</li>
      <li>Kuti ndione kukomborerwa kwavasanangurwa venyu, Kuti ndifare kwazvo nomufaro wavanhu venyu, Kuti ndirumbidze pamwechete nenhaka yenyu.</li>
      <li>Takatadza pamwechete namadzibaba edu, Takaita pamwechete namadzibaba edu, Takaita zvisina kururama, takaita zvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Madzibaba edu haana kunzwisisa zvishamiso zvenyu paIjipiti; Haana kurangarira ngoni dzenyu zhinji; Asi vakakumukirai pagungwa, ipo paGungwa Dzvuku.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro akavaponesa nokuda kwezita rake, Kuti azivise simba rake guru.</li>
      <li>Akarairawo Gungwa Dzvuku, rikapwa, Akavafambisa pakadzika sapanenge pabani.</li>
      <li>Akavaponesa paruoko rwowaivavenga. Akavadzikunura paruoko rwomuvengi.</li>
      <li>Mvura zhinji yakafukidza vadzivisi vavo; Kwakanga kusina nomumwe wavo akasara.</li>
      <li>Ipapo vakatenda mashoko ake; Vakaimba vachimurumbidza.</li>
      <li>Vakachimbidzika kukanganwa mabasa ake; Havana kurindira zano rake.</li>
      <li>Asi vakachiva kwazvo-kwazvo murenje, Vakaidza Mwari mugwenga.</li>
      <li>Akavapa chavakakumbira; Asi akatuma kuonda mumweya yavo.</li>
      <li>Vakagodora Mozisi pamisasa, NaAroni, mutsvene waJehovha.</li>
      <li>Pasi pakashama pakamedza Dhatani, Pakafukidza boka raAbhirami.</li>
      <li>Moto ukapfuta pakati peboka ravo; Murazvo ukapisa vakaipa.</li>
      <li>Vakaita mhuru paHorebhi, Vakanamata mufananidzo wakaumbwa.</li>
      <li>Vakatsinhana saizvozvo kubwinya kwavo Nomufananidzo wemombe, inochera bundo.</li>
      <li>Vakakanganwa Mwari muponesi wavo, Wakaita zvinhu zvikuru paIjipiti;</li>
      <li>Mabasa anoshamisa munyika yaHamu, Nezvinhu zvinotyisa paGungwa Dzvuku.</li>
      <li>Saka akati, Ndinoda kuvaparadza; Dai Mozisi musanangurwa wake asina kumira pamberi pake ipo pakaputsika, Kuti adzore kutsamwa kwake, arege kuvaparadza.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, vakazvidza nyika inofadza, Havana kutenda shoko rake;</li>
      <li>Asi vakanyunyuta mumatende avo, Vakasateerera inzwi raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Saka wakavasimudzira ruoko rwake. Kuti avaparadze murenje;</li>
      <li>Uye kuti aparadze vana vavo pakati pavahedheni. Avaparadzire panyika dzose.</li>
      <li>Vakazvibatanidzawo naBhaaripeori, Vakadya zvakabayirwa vakafa.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo vakamutsamwisa nezvavakaita; Denda ndokupinda pakati pavo.</li>
      <li>Ipapo Pinehasi akasimuka, akaita zvakarurama; Denda ndokuguma.</li>
      <li>Izvozvo zvikanzi kwaari kururama, Kusvikira kumarudzi namarudzi nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Vakamutsamwisawo pamvura zhinji yeMeribha, Naizvozvo Mozisi akaoneswa nhamo nokuda kwavo;</li>
      <li>Nokuti vakamukira mweya wake, Iye akataura nehasha nemiromo yake.</li>
      <li>Havana kuparadza ndudzi dzavanhu, Sezvavakanga varairwa naJehovha,</li>
      <li>Asi vakavengana navahedheni, Vakadzidza mabasa avo;</li>
      <li>Vakashumira zvifananidzo zvavo; Izvo zvikava musungo kwavari.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, vakabayira mweya yakaipa vanakomana vavo navanasikana vavo,</li>
      <li>Vakateura ropa risina mhosva, iro ravanakomana vavo navanasikana vavo, Vakavabayira zvifananidzo zveKanani; Nyika ikasvibiswa neropa.</li>
      <li>Vakasvibiswa saizvozvo namabasa avo, Vakapata pane zvavakaita.</li>
      <li>Saka kutsamwa kwaJehovha kwakamukira vanhu vake, Akasema nhaka yake.</li>
      <li>Akavaisa muruoko rwavahedheni; Vakavavenga ndivo vaivabata.</li>
      <li>Vavengi vavo vakavamanikidzawo, Vakaiswa pasi poruoko rwavo.</li>
      <li>Akavarwira kazhinji, Asi vakamumukira pakurangana kwavo, Vakanyudzwa muzvakaipa zvavo.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro akatarira kutambudzika kwavo, Panguva yaakanzwa kuchema kwavo;</li>
      <li>Akarangarira sungano yake nokuda kwavo, Akazvidemba nokuda kwokuwanda kwengoni dzake.</li>
      <li>Akavanzwisawo tsitsi Navose vakanga vavatapa.</li>
      <li>Tiponesei, Jehovha Mwari wedu, Tiunganidzei, tibve pakati pavahedheni, Kuti tivonge zita renyu dzvene, Tifarisise pakukurumbidzai.</li>
      <li>Jehovha Mwari waIsiraeri ngaakudzwe, Kubva pakusingaperi kusvikira pakusingaperi. Vanhu vose ngavati, Ameni. Hareruya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vongai Jehovha, nokuti iye wakanaka; nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaoeri</li>
      <li>Vakadzikunurwa naJehovha ngavadaro, Ivo vakadzikunurwa muruvoko rwomudzivisi;</li>
      <li>Akavavunganidza panyika dzose kumabvazuva nekumavirira, kumusoro nezasi.</li>
      <li>vakafamba-famba murenje munzira yomugwenga;Havana kuwana muguta mavangagara</li>
      <li>vakafa nenzara nenyota,Mweya yavo ikaziya mukati mavo.</li>
      <li>Ipapo vakachema kuna Jehovha pakutambudzika kwavo, Iye akavarwira panjodzi dzavo.</li>
      <li>Wakavafambisawo nenzira yakarurama, Kuti vasvike kuguta rokugara.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, dai vanhu vachirumbidza Jehovha nokuda kwokunaka kwake, Uye nokuda kwamabasa ake, anoshamisa, aakaitira vanakomana vavanhu!</li>
      <li>Nokuti anogutisa mweya, une nyota, Uye mweya, une nzara, anouzadza nezvakanaka.</li>
      <li>Ndivo, vakanga vagere murima nomumvuri worufu, Vakanga vakasungwa mukutambudzika namatare,</li>
      <li>Nokuti vakamukira mashoko aMwari, Vakashora zano roWokumusorosoro;</li>
      <li>Saka wakaninipisa moyo yavo nokutambura; Vakawira pasi, kukasava nomunhu anobatsira.</li>
      <li>Ipapo vakachema kuna Jehovha panhamo yavo, Akavaponesa pamatambudziko avo.</li>
      <li>Akavabudisa parima nomumvuri worufu, Akadamburanya zvisungo zvavo.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, dai vanhu vachirumbidza Jehovha nokuda kwokunaka kwake, Uye nokuda kwamabasa ake, anoshamisa, aakaitira vanakomana vavanhu!</li>
      <li>Nokuti wakavhuna masuo endarira, Nokuguranya mazariro amatare.</li>
      <li>Mapenzi anotambudzika nokuda kwokudarika kwavo, Uye nokuda kwazvakaipa zvavo.</li>
      <li>Mweya wavo unosema zvokudya zvose; Vanoswedera pedo namasuo orufu.</li>
      <li>Zvino vochema kuna Jehovha panhamo yavo, Iye anovaponesa pamatambudziko avo.</li>
      <li>Anotuma shoko rake, ndokuvaporesa, Nokuvarwira pakuparadzwa kwavo.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, dai vanhu vachirumbidza Jehovha nokuda kwokunaka kwake, Uye nokuda kwamabasa ake anoshamisa, aakaitira vanakomana vavanhu!</li>
      <li>Ngavabayire zvibayiro zvokuvonga, Nokududzira mabasa ake nokuimba.</li>
      <li>Avo, vanoburukira kugungwa muzvikepe, Vanoshambadzira kumvura zhinji;</li>
      <li>Ndivo vanoona mabasa aJehovha, Nezvishamiso zvake pakadzika.</li>
      <li>Nokuti anoraira, ndokumutsa dutu guru, Rinomutsa mafungu aro.</li>
      <li>Vanosimudzirwa kudenga; ndokuburukirazve pakadzika; Mweya wavo unonyauka nokuda kwenhamo.</li>
      <li>Vanondeya-ndeya nokudzengedzeka somunhu akabatwa. Vapera mano.</li>
      <li>Zvino vochema kuna Jehovha panhamo yavo, Iye ndokuvabudisa pamatambudziko avo.</li>
      <li>Anonyaradza dutu remhepo, Mafungu aro ndokunyarara.</li>
      <li>Ipapo vanofara nokuti anyarara; Zvino iye ndokuvasvitsa pakadzikama pavaida kuvapo.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, dai vanhu vachirumbidza Jehovha nokuda kwokunaka kwake Uye nokuda kwamabasa ake anoshamisa aakaitira vanakomana vavanhu!.</li>
      <li>Ngavamukudzisewo paungano yavanhu, Vamurumbidze pamakurukota avakuru.</li>
      <li>Anoshandura nzizi dzikaita renje, Namatsime emvura aite nyika yakaoma;</li>
      <li>Nyika, inobereka zvakanaka, ive sango rebare, Nokuda kwezvakaipa zvavanogara mairi.</li>
      <li>Anoshandura renje riite dziva remvura, Nenyika yakaoma iite matsime emvura.</li>
      <li>Ndipapo paanogarisa vane nzara, Kuti vamutse guta rokugaramo;</li>
      <li>Vadzvare minda, vasime minda yemizambiringa, Vawane zvibereko zvizhinji.</li>
      <li>Akavaropafadzawo, vakawanda kwazvo; Akasatendera zvipfuwo zvavo kutapudzwa.</li>
      <li>Zvino vakatapudzika nokuva vashoma. Nemhaka yokumanikidzwa, nenhamo, nokuzvidya moyo.</li>
      <li>Anodurura kuzvidza pamusoro pamachinda, Achivadzungaidza murenje musina nzira.</li>
      <li>Kunyange zvakadaro, anogadza mushaiwi kumusoro kusina dambudziko, Achimumutsira mhuri samapoka amakwai.</li>
      <li>Akarurama achazviona, akafara; Uye zvakaipa zvose zvichadzivirwa muromo wazvo.</li>
      <li>Ani naani akachenjera achacherekedza zvinhu izvozvi, Vachafunga unyoro hwaJehovha. Mwari Mubatsiri wedu</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>moyo wangu wakasimba, Mwari; Ndichaimba, zvirokwazvo, ndichaimba nziyo dzokurumbidza, nomweya wangu wose.</li>
      <li>Muka iwe mutengeranwa nembira; Ini ndimene ndichamuka mangwanani.</li>
      <li>Ndichakuvongai Jehovha, pakati pendudzi dzavanhu; Ndichakuimbirai nziyo dzokurumbidza pakati pavahedheni.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ngoni dzenyu ihuru kumusoro kwokudenga-denga, Uye zvokwadi yenyu inosvikira kudenga rose.</li>
      <li>Imi mukudzwe Mwari, kumusoro kwokudenga-denga; Kurumbidzwa kwenyu ngakuve kumusoro kwapasi pose.</li>
      <li>Kuti vadikanwi venyu varwirwe, Tiponesei noruoko rwenyu rworudyi, mutipindure.</li>
      <li>Mwari akataura pautsvene hwake, achiti, Ndichafara kwazvo; Ndichaganhura Shekemu, ndichayera mupata weSukoti.</li>
      <li>Giriyadhi ndeyangu naManase ndeyangu; Efuremuwo inhaviro yomusoro wangu; Judha ndiyo tsvimbo yangu youshe.</li>
      <li>Moabhu ndiwo mudziyo wangu wokushambidzira; Pamusoro peEdhomu ndipo pandichakandira shangu yangu; Ndichapururudza nokuda kwaFirisitia.</li>
      <li>Ndianiko achandiisa muguta rakakombwa namasvingo? Ndianiko achandiperekedza ndiende Edhomu?</li>
      <li>Hamuna kutirasha here, Mwari? Hamubudi Mwari, nehondo dzedu.</li>
      <li>Tibatsirei pamudzivisi wedu; Nokuti kubatsira kwavanhu hakuna maturo.</li>
      <li>MunaMwari tichaita noumhare; Nokuti ndiye achatsika vadzivisi vedu pasi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Regai kunyarara, Mwari wokurumbidza kwangu;</li>
      <li>Nokuti vakandishamisira muromo wowakaipa, uye muromo unonyengedzera; Vakandireva norurimi rune nhema.</li>
      <li>Vakandikombawo namashoko embengo, Vakarwa neni pasina mhosva.</li>
      <li>Pakuvada kwangu vava vadzivisi vangu; Asi ini ndinonyengetera hangu.</li>
      <li>Vakanditsivira zvakaipa pane zvakanaka, zvandakavaitira, Nembengo pakuvada kwangu.</li>
      <li>Isai munhu akaipa ave ishe wake; Mudzivisi ngaamire paruoko rwake rworudyi.</li>
      <li>Kana achitongwa, ngaapiwe mhosva; Munyengetero wake ngaushandurwe zvivi.</li>
      <li>Mazuva ake ngaave mashoma; Mumwe ngaatore basa rake.</li>
      <li>Vana vake ngavave nherera, Uye mukadzi wake ngaave chirikadzi.</li>
      <li>Vana vake ngavave vadzungairi, navapemhi; Ngavatsvake zvokudya kure namatongo avo.</li>
      <li>Waakadyira chikwerete ngaatore zvose zvaanazvo; Vatorwa ngavapambe zvose zvaakabatira.</li>
      <li>Ngakushaikwe munhu anomunzwira ngoni; Ngakushaikwe munhu anetsitsi nenherera dzake.</li>
      <li>Vana vake ngavarove; Zita ravo ngaridzimwe parudzi runotevera.</li>
      <li>Zvakaipa zvamadzibaba ake ngazvirangarirwe naJehovha; Zvivi zvamai vake ngazvirege kudzimwa.</li>
      <li>Ngazvirambe zviri pamberi paJehovha nguva dzose, Kuti aparadze kurangarirwa kwavo pasi.</li>
      <li>Nemhaka yokuti haana kurangarira kunzwira ngoni, Asi wakatambudza murombo nomushaiwi, Neanomoyo wakaputsika, kuti avauraye.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, kutuka ndizvo zvaakada, zvikauyawo kwaari; Kukomborera haana kukufarira kukagara kure naye.</li>
      <li>Akazvifukidzawo nokutuka, zvikaita senguvo yake, Zvikapinda mukati make semvura, Samafuta mumapfupa ake.</li>
      <li>Ngazvive kwaari sechisimiro chaanofukidza nacho, Segwarada raakazvisunga naro nguva dzose.</li>
      <li>Uyu ndiwo mubayiro wavadzivisi vangu, unobva kuna Jehovha, Nowavanotaurira mweya wangu zvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Asi imi Jehovha Ishe, ndiitirei zvakanaka nokuda kwezita renyu; Ngoni dzenyu zvadzakanaka, ndirwirei.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndiri murombo nomushaiwi, Nomoyo wangu wakakuvadzwa mukati mangu.</li>
      <li>Ndaenda somumvuri wareba; Ndapepereswa semhashu.</li>
      <li>Mabvi angu haachine simba nokuzvinyima zvokudya; Nyama yangu yaonda nokushaiwa mafuta.</li>
      <li>Ndavawo chinhu chinozvidzwa navo; Kana vachindiona vanodzungudza misoro yavo.</li>
      <li>Ndibatsirei, Jehovha, Mwari wangu; Ndiponesei nengoni dzenyu.</li>
      <li>Kuti vazive kuti ndirwo ruoko rwenyu; Kuti imwi Jehovha, ndimwi makazviita.</li>
      <li>Ngavatuke havo, asi imi ropafadzai; Kana vachisimuka, vachanyadziswa, asi muranda wenyu achafara kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Vadzivisi vangu ngavafukidzwe nokunyadziswa, Ngavazvifukidze nokunyara kwavo sejasi.</li>
      <li>Ndichavonga Jehovha kwazvo nomuromo wangu; Zvirokwazvo, ndichamurumbidza pakati pavazhinji.</li>
      <li>Nokuti iye achamira kuruoko rworudyi rwomushaiwi, Kuti amuponese panavanotonga mweya wake.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha akati kuna She wangu, Gara kurudyi rwangu, Kusvikira ndaita vavengi vako chitsiko chetsoka dzako.</li>
      <li>Jehovha achatambanudza tsvimbo yesimba rako ribude paZiyoni, achiti, Bata ushe pakati pavavengi vako.</li>
      <li>Vanhu vako vachazviisa nomoyo wose pazuva rauchaunganidza hondo yako, Nenguva tsvene, pachizvaro chamangwanani, Ndipo pane dova rohujaya hwako.</li>
      <li>Jehovha akapika, haangazvidembi, achiti, Iwe uri mupirisiti nokusingaperi. Unorudzi naMerikizedheki.</li>
      <li>Ishe parudyi rwako Achaparadza madzimambo pazuva rokutsamwa kwake.</li>
      <li>Iye achatonga pakati pavahedheni, Achazadza nyika nezvitunha; Achaparadza misoro panyika zhinji.</li>
      <li>Achanwa parukova panzira; Saka achasimudza musoro wake.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Ndichavonga Jehovha nomoyo wangu wose, Parangano yavakarurama, napaungano.</li>
      <li>Mabasa aJehovha makuru, Anocherechedzwa navose vanoafarira.</li>
      <li>Basa rake rinoratidza kukudzwa noumambo; Kururama kwake kunogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Mabasa ake, anoshamisa, wakaaita chiyeudziro; Jehovha anenyasha netsitsi.</li>
      <li>Akapa zvokudya vanomutya; Acharangarira sungano yake nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akaratidza vanhu vake simba ramabasa ake, Zvaakavapa nhaka yavahedheni.</li>
      <li>Mabasa amaoko ake izvokwadi nokururamisira; Mirairo yake yose yakasimba.</li>
      <li>Yakasimbiswa nokusingaperi-peri, Yakaitwa nezvokwadi nokururama.</li>
      <li>Akatumira vanhu vake rudzikunuro; Akaraira sungano yake nokusingaperi; Zita rake idzvene rinotyisa.</li>
      <li>Kutya Jehovha ndiko kutanga kwouchenjeri; Vose vanozviita vanomurangariro wakanaka; Kurumbidzwa kwake kunogara nokusingaperi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Akaropafadzwa munhu anotya Jehovha, Anofarira zvikuru mirairo yake.</li>
      <li>Vana vake vachava nesimba pasi; Rudzi rwowakarurama rucharopafadzwa.</li>
      <li>fuma nezvakawanda zviri mumba make; Kururama kwake kunogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akarurama anobudirwa nechiedza parima; Iye anenyasha, netsitsi nokururama.</li>
      <li>Ane mufaro munhu uyo anoita nenyasha, anopa chikwerete, Acharuramisirwa mhaka yake pakutonga.</li>
      <li>Nokuti haangatongozununguswi; Akarurama acharamba achirangarirwa nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Haangatyi mashoko ezvinhu zvakaipa; moyo wake wakasimba, uchavimba naJehovha.</li>
      <li>moyo wake wakasimbiswa, haangatyi, Kusvikira aona kukundwa kwavadzivisi vake.</li>
      <li>Akaparadzira, akapa vashaiwi; Kururama kwake kunogara nokusingaperi; Runyanga rwake ruchakwiridzwa nokukudzwa.</li>
      <li>Akaipa achazviona, ndokufa neshungu; Achageda-geda meno ake, ndokunyauka; Kuda kwowakaipa kuchaparara.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Rumbidzai, imi varanda vaJehovha, Rumbidzai zita raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Zita raJehovha ngarikudzwe Kubva panguva ino kusvikira pakusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Kubva pakubuda kwezuva kusvikira pakuvira kwaro Zita raJehovha rinofanira kurumbidzwa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha uri kumusoro kwavahedheni vose, Nokubwinya kwake kumusoro kwokudenga-denga.</li>
      <li>Ndianiko akafanana naJehovha Mwari wedu, Iye anogara kumusoro,</li>
      <li>Iye anozvidukupisa kuti aone Zviri kudenga napasi?</li>
      <li>Anosimudza murombo abve muguruva, anomumutsa abve padurunhuru;</li>
      <li>Kuti amugarise pamwechete namachinda, Iwo machinda avanhu vake.</li>
      <li>Anogarisa mukadzi asingabereki mumba,ave mai vanofara navana. Hareruya</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pakubuda kwaIsiraeri Imba yaJakobho ichibuda pakati pavanhu vakanga vanorumwe rurimi;</li>
      <li>Judha akaitwa imba yake tsvene, Nalsiraeri ushe hwake.</li>
      <li>Gungwa rakazviona, rikatiza; Jorodhani rwakadzokera shure.</li>
      <li>Makomo akapembera samakondobwe, Nezvikomo samakwayana.</li>
      <li>Unonzweiko iwe gungwa, zvaunotiza iwe? Newe Jorodhani, zvaunodzokera shure?</li>
      <li>Nemi makomo, zvamunopembera samakondobwe; Nemi zvikomo, samakwayana?</li>
      <li>Bvunda iwe pasi, pamberi paShe, Pamberi paMwari waJakobho;</li>
      <li>Iye akashandura dombo, rikava dziva remvura,</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Isu kwete, Jehovha, isu kwete, Asi zita renyu ngarikudzwe, Nokuda kwengoni dzenyu, uye nokuda kwokutendeka kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Vahedheni vachareverei, vachiti, Ko Mwari wavo zvino uripi?</li>
      <li>Asi Mwari wedu ari kudenga-denga; Akaita zvose zvaakada.</li>
      <li>Zvifananidzo zvavo sirivha nendarama, Basa ramaoko avanhu.</li>
      <li>Zvinemiromo, asi hazvitauri; nameso zvinawo, asi hazvioni;</li>
      <li>Zvinenzeve, asi hazvinzwi; Nemhino zvinadzo, asi hazvinhuwidzi;</li>
      <li>zvina maoko, asi hazvibati; Namakumbo zvinawo, asi hazvifambi; Hazvitauri napahuro pazvo.</li>
      <li>Ivo vanozviita vachafanana nazvo; Zvirokwazvo, navose vanovimba nazvo.</li>
      <li>lwe Isiraeri, vimba naJehovha; Ndiye mubatsiri wavo nenhovo yavo.</li>
      <li>Iwe imba yaAroni, vimba naJehovha; Ndiye mubatsiri wavo nenhovo yavo.</li>
      <li>Imi munotya Jehovha, vimbai naJehovha; Ndiye mubatsiri wavo nenhovo yavo.</li>
      <li>Jehovha akatirangarira; iye achatiropafadza; Acharopafadza imba yaIsiraeri, Acharopafadza imba yaAroni.</li>
      <li>Acharopafadza vanotya Jehovha, Vaduku navakuru vose.</li>
      <li>Jehovha acharamba achikuwanzai, Imi navana venyu.</li>
      <li>Imi makaropafadzwa naJehovha, Iye akaita kudenga napasi.</li>
      <li>Kudenga-denga ndiko kudenga-denga kwaJehovha; Asi pasi akapa vanakomana vavanhu.</li>
      <li>Vakafa havarumbidzi Jehovha, Kunyange ani naani anoburukira kwakanyarara;</li>
      <li>Asi isu hedu tichakudza Jehovha Kubva panguva ino kusvika pakusingaperi. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndinoda Jehovha, nokuti anonzwa inzwi rangu nokukumbira kwangu.</li>
      <li>Zvaakarereka nzeve yake kwandiri, Ndichadana kwaari mazuva angu ose.</li>
      <li>Misungo yorufu yakandikomba, Kurwadziwa kweSheori kwakandibata; Ndakawana kutambudzika nokuchema.</li>
      <li>Ipapo ndakadana zita raJehovha; Haiwa Jehovha, ndinonyengetera kuti murwire mweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anenyasha, akarurama; Zvirokwazvo, Mwari wedu ane tsitsi.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anochengeta vasina mano; Ndakanga ndashaiwa simba, iye akandiponesa.</li>
      <li>Dzokera kuzororo rako, mweya wangu; Nokuti Jehovha akakuitira zvakanaka.</li>
      <li>Nokuti makarwira mweya wangu parufu; Nameso angu pamisodzi, Netsoka dzangu pakugumburwa.</li>
      <li>Ndichafamba pamberi paJehovha Panyika yavapenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakatenda pakutaura kwangu, ndichiti, Ndakamanikidzwa kwazvo,</li>
      <li>Ndakati pakuvhunduka kwangu, Vanhu vose vanoreva nhema.</li>
      <li>Ndichavigireiko Jehovha Pamusoro pemikomborero yake yose kwandiri?</li>
      <li>Ndichasimudza mukombe wokuponeswa, Ndichidana zita raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Ndicharipira Jehovha mhiko dzangu, Ndichazviita pamberi pavanhu vake vose.</li>
      <li>Chinhu chinokosha pamberi paJehovha, Ndirwo rufu rwavatsvene vake.</li>
      <li>Haiwa Jehovha, zvirokwazvo ndiri muranda wenyu; Ndiri muranda wenyu, mwanakomana womurandakadzi wenyu; Makasunungura misungo yangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichakubayirai zvibayiro zvokuvonga, Ndichidana zita raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Ndicharipira Jehovha mhiko dzangu, Ndichazviita pamberi pavanhu vake vose;</li>
      <li>Pavazhe dzeimba yaJehovha, Mukati mako, iwe Jerusaremu. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Rumbidzai Jehovha, imi ndudzi dzose dzavanhu, Mukudzei, imi vanhu vose.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ngoni dzake kwatiri ihuru; Kutendeka kwaJehovha kunogara nokusingaperi. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vongai Jehovha; nokuti wakanaka; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Isiraeri zvino ngavati, Ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Imba yaAroni zvino ngaiti, Ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Avo vanotya Jehovha zvino ngavati, Ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Ndakadanidzira kuna Jehovha pakutambudzika kwangu, Jehovha paakandipindura, akandiisa pakafarikana.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ari kurutivi rwangu; handingatyi; Munhu angandiiteiko?</li>
      <li>Jehovha ari kurutivi rwangu pakati pavanondibatsira; Saka ndichaona kukundwa kwavanondivenga.</li>
      <li>Zviri nani kutizira kuna Jehovha Pakuvimba nomunhu.</li>
      <li>Zviri nani kutizira kuna Jehovha Pakuvimba namachinda.</li>
      <li>Vahedheni vose vakandikomba; Ndichavaparadza nezita raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Vakandikomba, zvirokwazvo, vakandikomba, Ndichavaparadza nezita raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Vakandikomba senyuchi; vakadzimwa somoto weminzwa; Ndichavaparadza nezita raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Kundisundidzira wakandisundidzira iwe kuti ndiwe; Asi Jehovha akandibatsira.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ndiye simba rangu norwiyo rwangu; Iye akava muponesi wangu.</li>
      <li>inzwi rokufara nerokuponeswa riri mumatende avakarurama; Ruoko rworudyi rwaJehovha runokunda.</li>
      <li>Ruoko rworudyi rwaJehovha rwakasimudzwa, Ruoko rworudyi rwaJehovha runokunda.</li>
      <li>Handingafi, asi ndichararama, Ndichadudzira mabasa aJehovha.</li>
      <li>Kundiranga Jehovha akandiranga; Asi haana kundiisa pakufa.</li>
      <li>Ndizarurirei masuo okururama; Ndichapinda nawo, ndivonge Jehovha.</li>
      <li>iri ndiro suo raJehovha; Vakarurama vachipinda naro.</li>
      <li>Ndichakuvongai, nokuti makandipindura, Mukava muponesi wangu.</li>
      <li>Ibwe rakaraswa navavaki Ndiro rakazova musoro wekona.</li>
      <li>Ichi chinhu chakabva kuna Jehovha; Zvinoshamisa kana tichizviona.</li>
      <li>Rino izuva rakaitwa naJehovha; Ngatifare kwazvo tirifarire.</li>
      <li>Tiponesei zvino, Jehovha ndizvo zvatinonyengetera; Jehovha, tipei mufaro ndizvo zvatinonyengetera.</li>
      <li>Akaropafadzwa iye anouya nezita raJehovha; Takaropafadzwa tiri mumba maJehovha.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ndiye Mwari, ndiye akativhenekera; Sungirai chibayiro namabote ipo panyanga dzearitari pamene.</li>
      <li>Imi muri Mwari wangu, ndichakuvongai; Muri Mwari wangu, ndichakukudzai.</li>
      <li>Vongai Jehovha; nokuti akanaka; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vakaropafadzwa avo vane nzira yakarurama, Vanofamba mumurau waJehovha.</li>
      <li>Vakaropafadzwa vanochengeta zvipupuriro zvake, Vanomutsvaka nomoyo wose.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, havaiti chinhu chisina kururama, Vanofamba munzira dzake.</li>
      <li>Makatiraira zvirevo zvenyu, Kuti tizvichengete zvakanaka.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, dai nzira dzangu dzakagadzirirwa Kuchengeta mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ipapo handinganyadziswi, Kana ndichirangarira mirairo yenyu yose.</li>
      <li>Ndichakuvongai nomoyo wakarurama, Kana ndichidzidza zvamakatonga zvakarurama.</li>
      <li>Ndichachengeta mitemo yenyu; Haiwa, regai kundirasha chose.</li>
      <li>Jaya ringaramba richinatsa nzira yaro neiko? Kana richichenjerera sezvinoraira shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakakutsvakai nomoyo wangu wose; Musanditendera kutsauka pamirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Shoko renyu ndakariviga mumoyo wangu, Kuti ndirege kukutadzirai.</li>
      <li>Imi munofanira kukudzwa, Jehovha; Ndidzidzisei mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakadudzira nemiromo yangu Zvose zvamakatonga nomuromo wenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakafara kwazvo munzira yezvipupuriro zvenyu, Sezvandinofarira fuma yose.</li>
      <li>Ndichafungisisa zvirevo zvenyu, Nokurangarira nzira dzenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndichazvifadza nemitemo yenyu; Handingakanganwi shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Itirai muranda wenyu zvakanaka, kuti ndirarame; Ipapo ndichachengeta shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndisvinudzei meso angu, kuti ndione Zvinhu zvinoshamisa zviri pamurau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndiri mutorwa panyika; Regai kundivanzira%mirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu wapera nokushuva Panguva dzose zvamakatonga.</li>
      <li>Makaraira vanozvikudza, Ngavatukwe vanotsauka pamirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Bvisai kwandiri kushorwa nokuzvidzwa; Nokuti ndakachengeta zvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Machindawo akagara akandireva; Asi muranda wenyu akafungisisa mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Zvipupuriro zvenyuwo zvinondifadza kwazvo, Ndizvo zvinondipa mano.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu unonamatira guruva; Ndiponesei neshoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakadudzira nzira dzangu, imi makandipindura; Ndidzidzisei mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndidzidzisei ndinzwisise nzira yezvirevo zvenyu; Ipapo ndichafungisisa mabasa enyu anoshamisa.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu unonyunguruka nokuremerwa; Ndisimbisei sezvinorehwa neshoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Bvisai kwandiri nzira yenhema; Nenyasha dzenyu mundipe murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakasanangura nzira yakatendeka; Ndakaisa zvamakatonga pamberi pangu.</li>
      <li>Ndinonamatira zvipupuriro zvenyu; Jehovha, regai kundinyadzisa.</li>
      <li>Ndichamhanya nenzira yemirairo yenyu, Kana munenge makurisa moyo wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndidzidzisei, Jehovha, nzira yemitemo yenyu; Ndigoichengeta kusvikira pakuguma.</li>
      <li>Ndipei njere, ndichengete murau wenyu; Zvirokwazvo, ndichauchengeta nomoyo wangu wose.</li>
      <li>Ndifambisei munzira yemirairo yenyu; Nokuti ndinoifarira kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Kweverai moyo wangu kuzvipupuriro zvenyu, Urege kukweverwa mukuchiva.</li>
      <li>Dzorai meso angu ndirege kuona zvisina maturo, Mundiponese panzira dzenyu.</li>
      <li>Simbisai Shoko renyu kumuranda wenyu, Rakakwanira vanokutyai.</li>
      <li>Bvisai kushoorwa kwangu kwandinotya, Nokuti zvamakatonga zvakanaka.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, ndakashuva zvirevo zvenyu; Ndiponesei mukururama kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Ngoni dzenyu ngadziuyewo kwandiri, Jehovha, Iko kuponesa kwenyu, sezvinoreva shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo ndichagona kupindura anondishora; Nokuti ndinovimba neshoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Regai kubvisa shoko rezvokwadi chose pamuromo wangu; Nokuti ndakatarira zvamakatonga.</li>
      <li>Naizvozvo ndichasichengeta murau wenyu Nokusingaperi-peri.</li>
      <li>Ndichasifamba ndakasununguka, Nokuti ndakatsvaka zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndichataurawo zvipupuriro zvenyu pamberi pamadzimambo, Ndisinganyadziswi.</li>
      <li>Ndichazvifadza kwazvo nemirairo yenyu, Yandinoda.</li>
      <li>Ndichasimudzirawo maoko angu kumirairo yenyu, yandinoda; Ndichafungisisa mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Rangarirai shoko renyu kumuranda wenyu, Nokuti makandimutsira tariro.</li>
      <li>Ndizvo zvinondinyaradza pakutambudzika kwangu; Nokuti shoko renyu rakandiponesa.</li>
      <li>Vanozvikudza vakandiseka kwazvo; Kunyange zvakadaro handina kutsauka pamurau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakarangarira zvamakatonga kare-kare, Jehovha, Ndikazvinyaradza.</li>
      <li>Kutsamwa kukuru kwakandibata, Nokuda kwavakaipa vanorasha murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Mitemo yenyu yaiva nziyo dzangu Mumba muutorwa hwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakarangarira zita renyu, Jehovha, usiku, Ndikachengeta murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndizvo zvandakanga ndinazvo, Nokuti ndakachengeta zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ndiye mugove wangu; Ndakati, ndichachengeta mashoko enyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakakumbira chiso chenyu nomoyo wangu wose; Ndinzwirei nyasha, sezvinoreva shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakafunga nzira dzangu, Ndikadzorera tsoka dzangu kuzvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakakurumidza, handina kunonoka Kuchengeta mirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Mabote avakaipa akandimonera; Asi handina kukanganwa murau Venyu.</li>
      <li>Ndichamuka pakati pousiku kuti ndikuvongei Pamusoro pezvamakatonga zvakarurama.</li>
      <li>Ndiri shamwari yavose vanokutyai, Neyavanochengeta zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, pasi pazere nengoni dzenyu; Ndidzidzisei mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Makaitira muranda wenyu zvakanaka, Jehovha, sezvinoreva shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndidzidzisei ungwaru hwakanaka nenjere; Nokuti ndakatenda mirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakati ndichigere kutambudzika ndikarashika; Asi zvino ndinochengeta shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Imi makanaka, uye munoita zvakanaka; Ndidzidzisei mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Vanozvikudza vakandipomera nhema; Ndichachengeta zvirevo zvenyu nomoyo wangu wose.</li>
      <li>moyo wavo wakakora samafuta; Asi ini ndinofarira murau wenyu kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Zvakanga zvakanaka kuti nditambudzike; Kuti ndidzidze mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Murau womuromo wenyu wakanaka kwandiri Kukunda zviuru zvamazana zvendarama nesirivha.</li>
      <li>Maoko enyu akandiita nokundisimbisa; Ndipei kunzwisisa, kuti ndidzidze mirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Vanokutyai vachandiona ndokufara; Nokuti ndakatarira shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndinoziva, Jehovha, kuti zvamakatonga zvakarurama, Uye kuti makanditambudza nokutendeka.</li>
      <li>Ndinokumbira kuti tsitsi dzenyu dzindinyaradze, Sezvamakareva kumuranda wenyu.</li>
      <li>Unyoro hwenyu ngabwuuye kwandiri, kuti ndirarame; Nokuti murau wenyu ndiwo mufaro wangu mukuru.</li>
      <li>Vanozvikudza ngavanyadziswe; nokuti vakandiitira zvakaipa ndisina mhosva; Asi ndichafungisisa zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Vanokutyai ngavadzokere kwandiri, Vagoziva zvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>moyo wangu ngaururame pamitemo yenyu; Kuti ndirege kunyadziswa.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu unopanga kuponesa kwenyu; Asi ndinotarira shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Meso angu anopera nokutsvaka shoko renyu, Ndichiti, Muchandinyaradza rinhiko?</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndava sehombodo iri muutsi; Kunyange zvakadaro handikanganwi mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Mazuva omuranda wenyu manganiko? Muchatonga rinhiko vanonditambudza?</li>
      <li>Vanozvikudza vakandicherera hunza, Ivo vasingateereri murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Mirairo yenyu yose yakatendeka; Vanonditambudza ndisina mhosva; ndibatsirei imi.</li>
      <li>Vakanga voda kundiparadza pasi; Asi handina kusiya zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndiponesei nokuda kwounyoro hwenyu; Naizvozvo ndichachengeta chipupuriro chomuromo wenyu.</li>
      <li>Shoko renyu rakasimba kudenga Nokusingaperi, Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Kutendeka kwenyu kunosvika kumarudzi namarudzi; Imi makasimbisa pasi, panoramba pagere.</li>
      <li>Zvinoramba zvigere nanhasi sezvamakatema; Nokuti zvinhu zvose varanda venyu.</li>
      <li>Dai murau wenyu usina kuva mufaro wangu mukuru, Ndingadai ndakaparara nedambudziko rangu.</li>
      <li>Handingatongokanganwi zvirevo zvenyu; Nokuti makandiponesa nazvo.</li>
      <li>Ndiri wenyu, ndiponesei; Nokuti ndakatsvaka zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Vakaipa vakandigarira kuti vandiparadze; Asi ndichafunga zvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakaona kuguma kwezvose zvakakwana, Asi murayiro wenyu mupamhi kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Haiwa, ndinoda murau wenyu seiko! Ndicho chandinofungisisa zuva rose.</li>
      <li>Mirairo yenyu inondiita akachenjera kupfuura vavengi vangu; Nokuti inogara neni nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Ndine njere kupfuura vadzidzisi vangu vose; Nokuti zvipupuriro zvenyu ndizvo zvandinofungisisa.</li>
      <li>Ndinonzwisisa kupfuura vakakwegura, Nokuti ndakachengeta zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakadzora tsoka dzangu panzira dzose dzakaipa; Kuti ndichengete shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Handina kutsauka pane zvamatonga; Nokuti makandidzidzisa.</li>
      <li>Mashoko enyu anonaka seiko mumukanwa mangu! Zvirokwazvo, anokunda uchi mumuromo mangu!</li>
      <li>Pazvirevo zvenyu ndinowana njere; Saka ndinovenga nzira dzose dzenhema.</li>
      <li>Shoko renyu ndiwo mwenje wetsoka dzangu, Nechiedza panzira yangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakapika, ndikazvisimbisa, Kuti ndichachengeta zvamakatonga zvakarurama.</li>
      <li>Ndinotambudzika kwazvo; Ndiponesei, Jehovha, neshoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Gamuchirai henyu Jehovha ndizvo zvandinokumbira zvipo zvomuromo wangu zvandinopa nomoyo wangu, Mundidzidzise zvamakatonga.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu unongosiva muruoko rwangu; Kunyange zvakadaro handikanganwi murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Vakaipa vakanditeyera musungo; Kunyange zvakadaro handina kutsauka pazvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Zvipupuriro zvenyu ndakazviita nhaka yangu nokusingaperi; Nokuti ndizvo zvinofadza moyo wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakarerekera moyo wangu kuti uite mitemo yenyu, Nokusingaperi, kusvikira pakuguma.</li>
      <li>Ndinovenga vane moyo miviri; Asi ndinoda murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Imi muri chivando changu nenhovo yangu; Ndinotarira shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ibvai kwandiri, imi munoita zvakaipa; Kuti ndichengete mirairo yaMwari wangu.</li>
      <li>Nditsigirei sezvinoreva shoko renyu, kuti ndirarame; Kuti ndirege kunyadziswa pakutarira kwangu.</li>
      <li>Nditsigirei, ndichengetwe, Ndigoramba ndichirangarira mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Makazvidza vose vanotsauka pamitemo yenyu; Nokuti kunyengera kwavo inhema.</li>
      <li>Vakaipa vose vapasi munovagumisa sefuro; Saka ndinoda zvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Nyama yangu inobvunda nokukutyai; Ndinotya zvamakatonga.</li>
      <li>Ndakaita zvakatongwa nezvakarurama; Musandiisa kuvamanikidzi vangu.</li>
      <li>Ivai rubatso rwomuranda wenyu kuti ndiitirwe zvakanaka, Vanozvikudza ngavarege kundimanikidza.</li>
      <li>Meso angu apera nokutsvaka kuponesa kwenyu, Neshoko renyu rakarurama.</li>
      <li>Itirai muranda wenyu nounyoro hwenyu, Mundidzidzise mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndiri muranda wenyu, ndipei njere; Kuti ndizive zvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Inguva yaJehovha yokubata nayo; Nokuti vakaputsa murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Saka ndinoda mirairo yenyu Kupfuura ndarama, zvirokwazvo, kupfuura ndarama yakaisvonaka.</li>
      <li>Saka ndinoti, zvirevo zvenyu zvose pamusoro pezvose zvakarurama; Ndinovenga nzira dzose dzenhema.</li>
      <li>Zvipupuriro zvenyu zvinoshamisa; Saka mweya wangu unozvichengeta.</li>
      <li>Kuzarurwa kwamashoko enyu kunopa chiedza; Kunopa njere vasina mano.</li>
      <li>Ndakashamisa muromo wangu kwazvo, ndikatakwaira; Nokuti ndakashuva mirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ringirirai kwandiri, mundinzwire nyasha, Sezvamunoitira vanoda zita renyu.</li>
      <li>Simbisirai kutsika kwangu mushoko renyu; Zvakaipa ngazvirege kutongova nesimba pamusoro pangu.</li>
      <li>Ndidzikunurei pakumanikidza kwomunhu; Naizvozvo ndichachengeta zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Chiso chenyu ngachivhenekere muranda wenyu; Mundidzidzise mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Nzizi dzemvura dzinoyerera pameso angu, Nokuti havachengeti murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Imi makarurama, Jehovha, Nezvamakatonga zvakaruramawo.</li>
      <li>Makaraira zvipupuriro zvenyu nokururama Uye nokutendeka kukuru.</li>
      <li>Kushingaira kwangu kwakandipedza, Nokuti vadzivisi vangu vakakangwanwa mashoko enyu.</li>
      <li>Shoko renyu rakaisvonatswa; Saka muranda wenyu anorida.</li>
      <li>Ndiri muduku, ndakazvidzwa; Asi handikanganwi zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Kururama kwenyu ndiko kururama kusingaperi, Nomurau wenyu izvokwadi.</li>
      <li>Nhamo nokumanikidzwa zvakandibata; Asi mirairo yenyu ndiwo mufaro wangu mukuru.</li>
      <li>Zvipupuriro zvenyu zvakarurama nokusingaperi; Ndipei njere, ndigorarama.</li>
      <li>Ndakadana nomoyo wangu wose; ndipindurei, Jehovha; Ndichachengeta mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakadana kwamuri; ndiponesei, Ndigochengeta zvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakatangira mambakwedza ndikadana; Ndakatarira mashoko enyu.</li>
      <li>Meso angu akatangira nguva dzousiku, Kuti ndifungisise shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Inzwai inzwi rangu nokuda kwounyoro hwenyu; Ndiponesei Jehovha, sezvinoreva zvamakatonga.</li>
      <li>Vanotevera zvakaipa voswedera pedo; Vari kure nomurau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Imi muri pedo, Jehovha; Mirairo yenyu izvokwadi.</li>
      <li>Kubva kare ndakaziva nezvipupuriro zvenyu Kuti makazviteya nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Tarirai dambudziko rangu, mundirwire; Nokuti handikanganwi murau wenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndireverei mhosva yangu, mundidzikunure; Ndiponesei sezvinoreva shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Kuponeswa kuri kure navakaipa; Nokuti havatsvaki mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Ngoni dzenyu izhinji, Jehovha; Ndiponesei sezvinoreva zvamakatonga.</li>
      <li>Vatambudzi vangu navadzivisi vangu vazhinji; Kunyange zvakadaro handina kutsauka pazvipupuriro zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakaona vanyengedzeri, ndikavasema; Nokuti havana kuchengeta shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Fungai kuti ndinoda zvirevo zvenyu; Ndiponesei, Jehovha, nokuda kwounyoro hwenyu.</li>
      <li>Unganidzo yeshoko renyu izvokwadi; Zvose zvamakatonga, zvakarurama, zvinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Machinda akanditambudza ndisina mhosva; Asi moyo wangu unotya shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Ndinofarira shoko renyu kwazvo, Somunhu awana zvizhinji zvakapambwa.</li>
      <li>Nhema ndinodzivenga nokudzisema; Asi murau wenyu ndinouda.</li>
      <li>Ndinokurumbidzai kanomwe pazuva, Nokuda kwezvakarurama zvamakatonga.</li>
      <li>Vanoda murau wenyu vane rugare rukuru; Hapana chinovagumbusa.</li>
      <li>Ndakatarira kuponesa kwenyu, Jehovha, Ndikaita mirairo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu wakachengeta zvipupuriro zvenyu; Ndinozvida kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Ndakachengeta zvirevo zvenyu nezvipupuriro zvenyu; Nokuti nzira dzangu dzose dziri pamberi penyu.</li>
      <li>Kudana kwangu ngakusvike pamberi penyu, Jehovha; Ndipei njere sezvinoreva shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Kukumbira kwangu ngakusvike pamberi penyu; Ndirwirei sezvinoreva shoko renyu.</li>
      <li>Miromo yangu ngairumbidze; Nokuti munondidzidzisa mitemo yenyu.</li>
      <li>Rurimi rwangu ngaruimbe shoko renyu; Nokuti mirairo yenyu yose yakarurama.</li>
      <li>Ruoko rwenyu ngarundibatsire; Nokuti ndakasanangura zvirevo zvenyu.</li>
      <li>Ndakashuva kuponesa kwenyu, Jehovha; Murau wenyu ndiwo mufaro wangu mukuru.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu ngaurarame, ugokurumbidzai; Nezvamakatonga ngazvindibatsire.</li>
      <li>Ndakadzungaira segwai rakarashika; tsvakai muranda wenyu; Nokuti handikanganwi mirairo yenyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pakutambudzika kwangu ndakadana kuna Jehovha, Iye akandipindura.</li>
      <li>Rwirai mweya wangu, Jehovha, pamiromo inoreva nhema, Naparurimi runonyengedzera.</li>
      <li>Iwe uchapiweiko, chinyi chichawedzerwa kwauri, Iwe rurimi runonyengedzera?</li>
      <li>Miseve inopinza yeanesimba, Namazimbe anopfuta omurara.</li>
      <li>Ndine ropa rakaipa zvandiri mutorwa paMesheki, Zvandigere pamatende eKedhari!</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu wakagara nguva refu Neanovenga rugare.</li>
      <li>Ini ndinoda rugare; Asi kana ndichitaura, ivo vanotsvaka kurwa.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndichasimudzira meso angu kumakomo; Kubatsirwa kwangu kuchabvepiko?</li>
      <li>Kubatsirwa kwangu kunobva kuna Jehovha, Wakaita kudenga napasi.</li>
      <li>Haangatenderi rutsoka rwako kuti rutedzemuke; Muchengeti wako haangakotsiri.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, muchengeti waIsiraeri Haangakotsiri kana kuvata.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ndiye muchengeti wako; Jehovha ndiye mumvuri wako paruoko rwako rworudyi.</li>
      <li>Zuva haringakubayi masikati, Nomwedzi usiku.</li>
      <li>Jehovha achakuchengeta pazvakaipa zvose; Achachengeta mweya wako.</li>
      <li>Jehovha achakuchengeta pakubuda kwako napakupinda kwako, Kubva panguva ino kusvikira pakusingaperi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndakafara panguva yavakati kwandiri, Hendei kumba kwaJehovha.</li>
      <li>Tsoka dzedu dzimire Pakati pamasuo ako, Jerusaremu;</li>
      <li>Jerusaremu, iwe wakavakwa seguta rakasanganiswa zvakanaka;</li>
      <li>Ndiko kunokwira ndudzi, ndudzi dzaJehovha, Sezvakarairwa Isiraeri, Kuti vavonge zita raJehovha.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndiko kwakagadzwa zvigaro zvokutonga, Zvigaro zvoushe zveimba yaDhavhidhi.</li>
      <li>kumbirirai Jerusaremu rugare; Vanokudai, vachakomborerwa.</li>
      <li>Rugare ngaruve mukati mamasvingo ako, Nokufarikana mukati medzimba dzako dzoushe.</li>
      <li>Nokuda kwehama dzangu neshamwari dzangu, Ndichati zvino, Rugare ngaruve mukati mako.</li>
      <li>Nokuda kweimba yaJehovha Mwari wedu Ndichakutsvakira zvakanaka.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndinosimudzira meso angu kwamuri, Iyemi, munogara kudenga.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, meso avaranda sezvaanotarira ruoko rwatenzi wavo, Uye meso omurandakadzi sezvaanotarira ruoko rwatenzikadzi wake; Saizvozvo meso edu anotarira kuna Jehovha Mwari wedu, Kusvikira atinzwira nyasha.</li>
      <li>Tinzwirei nyasha, Jehovha, tinzwirei nyasha; Nokuti tapera kwazvo nokuzvidzwa.</li>
      <li>Mweya wedu wapera chose Nokushora kwavanogara havo zvakanaka, Uye noruzvidzo rwavanozvikudza.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Dai Jehovha asaiva nesu, Isiraeri ngavadaro;</li>
      <li>Dai Jehovha asaiva nesu, Panguva yatakamukirwa navanhu;</li>
      <li>Vangadai vakatimedza tiri vapenyu, Panguva yatakamukirwa nehasha dzavo;</li>
      <li>Mvura zhinji ingadai yakatifukidza, Rwizi rungadai rwakapfuura napamusoro pomweya wedu.</li>
      <li>Mvura zhinji, inozvikudza, ingadai yakapfuura napamusoro pomweya wedu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ngaarumbidzwe, Iye asina kutiisa kuti tiparadzwe nameno avo.</li>
      <li>Mweya wedu wapukunyuka seshiri parugombe rwomuteyi weshiri; Rugombe rwadambuka, isu tapukunyuka.</li>
      <li>Kubatsirwa kwedu kuri muzita raJehovha, Akaita kudenga napasi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vanovimba naJehovha Vakafanana negomo reZiyoni, risingazununguswi, asi rimire nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Sokupoteredzwa kweJerusaremu namakomo, Saizvozvo Jehovha unopoteredza vanhu vake, Kubva panguva ino kusvikira pakusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Nokuti tsvimbo youshe yezvakaipa haingagari panhaka yavakarurama; Kuti vakarurama varege kutambanudzira maoko avo kune zvakaipa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, itirai vakanaka zvakanaka, Navane moyo yakarurama.</li>
      <li>Asi kana vari vanhu vanotsaukira kunzira dzavo dzakaminama, Jehovha achavaparadza pamwechete navaiti vezvakaipa. Isiraeri ngaave norugare!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha panguva yaakadzosa vatapwa veZiyoni, Isu takanga takafanana navanorota hope.</li>
      <li>Panguva iyo muromo wedu wakanga uzere nokuseka, Norurimi rwedu nokuimba; Ipapo pakati pavahedheni vakati, Jehovha akavaitira zvinhu zvikuru;</li>
      <li>Jehovha wakatiitira zvinhu zvikuru; Isu tinofara.</li>
      <li>Dzosai vatapwa vedu, Jehovha, sehove panyika yeNyasi.</li>
      <li>Vanodzvara nemisodzi vachakohwa nomufaro.</li>
      <li>Anofamba-famba, achichema, akatakura tsama yembeu, achadzoka nomufaro akatakura zvisote zvake.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kana Jehovha asingavaki imba, Vavaki vayo vanobata pasina; Kana Jehovha asingachengeti guta, Murindi anorindira pasina.</li>
      <li>Hazvina maturo kuti mumuke mangwanani nokunonoka kundovata, Nokudya zvokudya zvamakatamburira; Nokuti anopa vadikanwi vake izvozvo vavete.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, vana inhaka inobva kuna Jehovha; Chibereko chechizvaro ndiwo mubayiro waanopa.</li>
      <li>Semiseve muruoko rwemhare, Ndizvo zvakaita vana voujaya.</li>
      <li>Unomufaro iye murume anegoba rizere navo; Havanganyadziswi, Kana vachitaurirana navavengi vavo pasuo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vakaropafadzwa vose vanotya Jehovha, Vanofamba munzira dzake.</li>
      <li>Nokuti iwe uchadya zvawakabatira namaoko ako; Uchava nomufaro, uye zvichava zvakanaka newe.</li>
      <li>Mukadzi wako uchava somuzambiringa, unobereka zvakanaka, mukati meimba yako; Vana vako vachava semiti yemiorivhi, vakakomberedza tafura yako.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, murume anotya Jehovha Acharopafadzwa saizvozvo.</li>
      <li>Jehovha achakuropafadza ari paZiyoni; Uchaona kukomborerwa kweJerusaremu mazuva ose oupenyu hwako.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, uchaona vana vavana vako. Isiraeri ngaave norugare.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vakanditambudza kazhinji kubva pauduku hwangu, Isiraeri ngaadaro zvino;</li>
      <li>Vakanditambudza kazhinji kubva pauduku hwangu; Kunyange zvakadaro havana kundikunda.</li>
      <li>Varimi vakarima pamusana wangu; Vakaita mihoronga yavo mirefu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha akarurama; Akaguranya mabote avakaipa.</li>
      <li>Ngavanyadziswe, vadzoserwe shure, Ivo vose vanovenga Ziyoni.</li>
      <li>Ngavave souswa pamatenga eimba, Hunooma husati hwakura;</li>
      <li>Mucheki haazadzi ruoko rwake nahwo, Uye anosunga zvisote, fungatwa rake.</li>
      <li>Navanopfuura havangati, Jehovha ngaakuropafadzei; Tinokuropafadzai nezita raJehovha.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndakadanidzira kwamuri, Jehovha, ndiri makadzika.</li>
      <li>Ishe inzwai inzwi rangu; Nzeve dzenyu ngadziteerere inzwi rokukumbira kwangu.</li>
      <li>Dai imi Jehovha, mairangarira zvisakarurama, Ndianiko airamba amire, Ishe?</li>
      <li>Asi kukanganwirwa kuriko kwamuri, Kuti vanhu vakutyei.</li>
      <li>Ndinorindira Jehovha, mweya wangu unorindira; Ndinotarira shoko rake.</li>
      <li>Mweya wangu unorindira Ishe, Kupfuura varindi vanorindira rungwanani; Zvirokwazvo, kupfuura varindi vanorindira rungwanani.</li>
      <li>Imi Isiraeri, tarirai kuna Jehovha; .Sokuti kuna Jehovha kune ngoni, Uye kwaari kunokudzikunurwa kukuru.</li>
      <li>Iye achadzikunura Isiraeri Panezvisakarurama zvake zvose.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, moyo wangu hauzvikudzi, meso angu haana manyawi; Handine hanya nezvinhu zvikuru-kuru, Kana nezvinhu zvinondikurira.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo ndakavaraidza mweya wangu nokuunyaradza; Somwana wakarumurwa ari pana mai vake, Mweya wangu wakaita kwandiri somwana akarumurwa.</li>
      <li>Imi Isiraeri, tarirai kuna Jehovha Kubva panguva ino kusvikira pakusingaperi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, rangarirai Dhavhidhi Nedambudziko rake rose;</li>
      <li>Namapikiro ake kuna Jehovha, Nokupika kuna Wamasimba waJakobho, achiti,</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo handingapindi mutende reimba yangu, Kana kukwira pamubhedha wandakawadzirwa;</li>
      <li>Handingatenderi meso angu kuvata, Kana mafungiro angu kukotsira;</li>
      <li>Kusvikira ndawanira Jehovha nzvimbo, Netabhenakeri dzaWamasimba waJakobho.</li>
      <li>Tarirai, takazvinzwa muEfurata; Takazviwana pasango reJaari.</li>
      <li>Tichapinda mutabhenakeri dzake; Tichanamata pachitsiko chetsoka dzake.</li>
      <li>Simukai Jehovha, mupinde pamungazorora; Imi, neareka yesimba renyu.</li>
      <li>Vapiristi venyu ngavafukidzwe nokururama; Uye vatsvene venyu ngavapururudze nomufaro .</li>
      <li>Nokuda kwaDhavhidhi muranda wenyu Regai kuramba chiso chomuzodziwa wenyu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha akapika kuna Dhavhidhi; Haangashanduki pazviri, achiti, Zvibereko zvomuviri wako ndizvo zvandichaisa pachigaro chako choushe.</li>
      <li>Kana vana vako vachichengeta sungano yangu Nezvipupuriro zvangu zvandichavadzidzisa, Navana vavowo vachagara pachigaro chako choushe nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha wakasanangura Ziyoni; Akarida kuti huve ugaro hwake.</li>
      <li>Pano ndipo pandinozorora nokusingaperi; Ndichagara pano; nokuti ndakapada.</li>
      <li>Ndicharopafadza zvokudya zvaro kwazvo; Ndichagutisa varombo varo nezvokudya.</li>
      <li>Vapirisiti varo ndichavafukidzawo noruponeso; Vatsvene varo vachapururudza nomufaro.</li>
      <li>Ipapo ndichameresera Dhavhidhi runyanga; Ndakagadzirira muzodzwa wangu mwenje.</li>
      <li>Vavengi vake ndichavafukidza nokunyadziswa; Asi korona yake ichapenya pamusoro pake.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Tarirai, kunaka kwazvo nokufadza kwazvo Kana hama dzichigara pamwechete norugare.</li>
      <li>Zvakafanana namafuta anokosha ari pamusoro, Anoyerera pandebvu, Idzo ndebvu dzaAroni; Anoburukira kusvikira pamipendero yenguvo dzake;</li>
      <li>Zvakafanana nedova reHerimoni, Rinoburukira pamakomo eZiyoni; Nokuti ndipo Jehovha paakaraira kuropafadza kwake, Ndihwo upenyu husingaperi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Tarirai, rumbidzai Jehovha, imi varanda vose vaJehovha, Imi munomira usiku mumba maJehovha.</li>
      <li>Simudzirai maoko enyu kunzvimbo tsvene, Murumbidze Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ngaakuropafadze ari paZiyoni; Iye akasika kudenga napasi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Rumbidzai zita raJehovha; Murumbidzei, imi varanda vaJehovha;</li>
      <li>Imi mumire mumba maJehovha, Muvazhe dzeimba yaMwari wedu.</li>
      <li>Rumbidzai Jehovha; nokuti Jehovha akanaka; Imbirai zita rake nziyo dzokurumbidza; nokuti ndizvo zvinofadza.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha akazvisanangurira Jakobho, NaIsiraeri kuti ave fuma yake chaiyo.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ndinoziva kuti Jehovha . mukuru, Uye kuti Ishe wedu ari kumusoro kwavamwari vose.</li>
      <li>Zvose zvaakada kuita Jehovha akazviita, Kudenga napasi, nomumakungwa napakadzika pose.</li>
      <li>Anokwidza makore pamigumo yapasi; Anoita mheni kuuyisa mvura; Anobudisa mhepo panovigwa fuma yake.</li>
      <li>Ndiye akaparadza matangwe Avanhu neezvipfuwo.</li>
      <li>Akatuma zviratidzo nezvishamiso mukati mako, iwe Ijipiti, Pamusoro paFarao napamusoro pavaranda vake vose.</li>
      <li>Ndiye akaparadza ndudzi zhinji, Nokuuraya madzimambo anesimba.</li>
      <li>Sihoni mambo wavaAmori, NaOgi mambo weBhashani, Noushe hwose hweKanani;</li>
      <li>Akapa nyika yavo ive nhaka, Ive nhaka yaIsiraeri vanhu vake.</li>
      <li>Zita renyu, Jehovha, riripo nokusingaperi; Munorangarirwa Jehovha, kusvikira kumarudzi namarudzi.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha achatonga vanhu vake, Nokuzvidemba pamusoro pavaranda vake.</li>
      <li>Zvifananidzo zvavahedheni isirivha nendarama, Mubato wamaoko avanhu.</li>
      <li>Zvinemiromo, asi hazvitauri; Nameso zvinawo, asi hazvioni;</li>
      <li>Zvinenzeve, asi hazvinzwi; Hakuna kufema pamiromo yazvo.</li>
      <li>Vanozviita vachafanana nazvo; Zvirokwazvo, navose vanovimba nazvo.</li>
      <li>Imi veimba yalsiraeri, rumbidzai Jehovha; Imi veimba yaAroni, rumbidzai Jehovha;</li>
      <li>Imi veimba yaRevhi, rumbidzai Jehovha; Imi vanotya Jehovha, rumbidzai Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ngaarumbidzwe paZiyoni, Iye agere Jerusaremu. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vongai Jehovha, nokuti akanaka; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Vongai Mwari wavamwari; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Vongai Ishe wamadzishe; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye oga, anoita zvishamiso zvikuru; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye, akaita kudenga-denga nenjere dzake; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye akatatamura pasi pamusoro pemvura zhinji; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye akaita zviedza zvikuru; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Zuva, kuti ribate ushe masikati; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Mwedzi nenyeredzi, kuti zvibate ushe usiku; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye, akarova veIjipiti pamatangwe avo; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akabudisa Isiraeri pakati pavo; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Nechanza chine simba, uye noruoko rwakatambanudzwa; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye akaparadzanisa Gungwa Dzvuku napakati; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akayambusa Isiraeri nomukati maro; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akawisira Farao nehondo yake muGungwa Dzvuku; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye, akaperekedza vanhu vake murenje; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye, akaparadza madzimambo makuru; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akauraya madzimambo akakurumbira; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Sihoni mambo wavaAmori; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>NaOgi mambo weBhashani; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Akapa nyika yavo ive nhaka; ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Ive nhaka yaIsiraeri muranda wake; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Iye, akatirangarira paurombo hwedu; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi;</li>
      <li>Akatirwira pavadzivisi vedu; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Ndiye anopa zvinhu zvose zvokudya zvazvo; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Vongai Mwari wokudenga; Nokuti ngoni dzake dzinogara nokusingaperi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Panzizi dzeBhabhironi, Ndipo patakagara pasi, zvirokwazvo tikachema, Pakurangarira kwedu Ziyoni.</li>
      <li>Pamikonachando mukati madzo Takaturika mbira dzedu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti ipapo avo vakatitapa vakakumbira kwatiri mashoko orwiyo, Vakatiparadza vakakumbira mufaro, vachiti, Tiimbireiwo rwiyo rweZiyoni.</li>
      <li>Tingaimba seiko rwiyo rwaJehovha Munyika yavatorwa?</li>
      <li>Kana ndikakukanganwa, iwe Jerusaremu, Ruoko rwangu rworudyi ngarukanganwe umhizha hwarwo.</li>
      <li>Rurimi rwangu ngarunamatire kumatadzo angu, Kana ndikarega kukurangarira; Kana ndisingati Jerusaremu Ndiwo mufaro wangu mukuru unopfuura zvose.</li>
      <li>Rangarirai Jehovha, murove vana vaEdhomu Pamusoro pezuva reJerusaremu; Ivo, vakati, Paradzai, paradzai, Kusvikira panheyo dzaro.</li>
      <li>Iwe mukunda weBhabhironi, iwe unobva woparadzwa; Munhu uyo achava nomufaro, achakutsivira Sezvawakatiitira iwe.</li>
      <li>Munhu uyo achava nomufaro, achatora pwere dzako Nokudzirovera padombo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndichakuvongai nomoyo wangu wose; Ndichakuimbirai nziyo dzokurumbidza pamberi pavamwari.</li>
      <li>Ndichanamata ndakatarira kutemberi yenyu tsvene, Nokuvonga zita renyu nokuda kwounyoro hwenyu nokutendeka kwenyu; Nokuti makakurisa shoko renyu kupfuura zita renyu rose.</li>
      <li>Pazuva randakadana makandipindura, Makandisimbisa nesimba pamweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Madzimambo ose enyika achakuvongai, Jehovha, Nokuti vakanzwa mashoko omuromo wenyu.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, vachaimba vachireva nzira dzaJehovha; Nokuti kubwinya kwaJehovha kukuru.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha ari kumusoro, kunyange zvakadaro ane hanya neanozvininipisa; Asi anamanyawi Jehovha anomuziva ari kure.</li>
      <li>Kana ndichifamba pakati penhamo, imi muchandiponesa; Muchatambanudza ruoko rwenyu kudzivisa kutsamwa kwavavengi vangu, Ruoko rwenyu rworudyi ruchandiponesa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha achandikwanisira zvinhu zvangu; Ngoni dzenyu, Jehovha, dzinogara nokusingaperi; Musarega mabasa amaoko enyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, imi makandinzvera, nokundiziva.</li>
      <li>Munoziva kugara kwangu pasi nokusimuka kwangu, Munonzwisisa kufunga kwangu muri kure.</li>
      <li>Munocherekedza kufamba kwangu nokuvata kwangu pasi, Munoziva nzira dzangu dzose.</li>
      <li>Nokuti shoko risati ravapo parurimi rwangu, Tarirai, imi Jehovha, matoriziva rose.</li>
      <li>Makandikomberedza shure kwangu nemberi, Nokuisa ruoko rwenyu pamusoro pangu.</li>
      <li>Kuziva kwakadai kunondishamisa kwazvo; Zviri kumusoro, handigoni kusvikira kwazviri.</li>
      <li>Ndingaendepiko ndibve pamweya wenyu? Kana ndingatizirepiko ndibve pamberi penyu?</li>
      <li>Kana ndingakwira kudenga muripo; Kana ndikazviwarira nhovo paSheori, tarirai muripowo.</li>
      <li>Kana ndikabhururuka namapapiro amangwanani, Ndikandogara pamigumo yegungwa;</li>
      <li>Naipapowo ruoko rwenyu ruchandifambisa, Ruoko rwenyu rworudyi ruchandifambisa,</li>
      <li>Kana ndikati, Zvirokwazvo, rima richandifukidza, Chiedza chinondikomberedza chichava sousiku;</li>
      <li>Kunyange rima haringandivanzi kwamuri, Asi usiku hunopenya samasikati; Rima nechiedza zvakafanana.</li>
      <li>Nokuti imi makaumba itsvo dzangu; Makandiruka mudumbu ramai vangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichakuvongai; nokuti ndakaitwa nomutoo unotyisa unoshamisa; Mabasa enyu anoshamisa; Mweya wangu unozviziva kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Mapfupa angu akanga asina kuvanzwa kwamuri, Panguva yandakaitwa pakavanda, Pakuumbwa kwangu nenjere panzvimbo dzezasi dzapasi.</li>
      <li>Meso enyu akaona muviri wangu uchigere kukwaniswa,Zvose zvakanga zvakanyorwa murugwaro rwenyu,zuva rimwe nerimwe rokuumbwa kwazvo, Kusati kwava nechimwe chazvo.</li>
      <li>Mirangariro yenyu, Mwari, inodikanwa sei neni! Yakakura sei pakuverengwa kwayo!</li>
      <li>Kana ndikaiverenga, ingapfuura jecha pakuwanda; Kana ndichipepuka, ndichinemi.</li>
      <li>Dai muchiuraya henyu vakaipa, Mwari; Naizvozvo ibvai kwandiri, imi vanhu veropa.</li>
      <li>Nokuti vanokutaurirai zvakaipa, Vavengi venyu vanoreva zita renyu pasina.</li>
      <li>Ko ini handivengi avo vanokuvengai here, Jehovha? Handine shungu here navanokumukirai?</li>
      <li>Ndinovavenga nembengo huru; Vava vavengi vangu.</li>
      <li>Ndinzverei, Mwari, muzive moyo wangu; Ndiidzei, muzive ndangariro dzangu;</li>
      <li>Mutarire kana panenzira yakaipa mandiri, Mundifambise munzira isingaperi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndirwirei Jehovha pamunhu wakaipa, Ndichengetei pamunhu anehasha;</li>
      <li>Ivo, vanofunga zvakaipa mumoyo yavo; Vanogara vachimutsa kurwa.</li>
      <li>Vakarodza rurimi rwavo senyoka; Uturu hwechiva huri pasi pemiromo yavo.</li>
      <li>Ndichengetei, Jehovha, pamaoko owakaipa; Ndichengetei pamunhu anomanikidza; Vanofunga mano okugumburisa tsoka dzangu.</li>
      <li>Vanozvikudza vakandivanzira musungo namabote; Vakadzika mumbure parutivi rwenzira, Vakanditeyera rugombe.</li>
      <li>Ndakati kuna Jehovha, Mwari wangu; Teererai, Jehovha, munzwe inzwi rokukumbira kwangu.</li>
      <li>Mwari Ishe, ndimi simba rokuponeswa kwangu, Makafukidza musoro wangu pazuva rokurwa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, regai kupa wakaipa zvaanotsvaka; Musapfuudza zano rake rakaipa; kuti varege kuzvikudza.</li>
      <li>Kana uri musoro wavanondikomba, Zvakashata zvemiromo yavo imene ngazvivafukidze.</li>
      <li>Mazimbe omoto, anopfuta, ngaawire pamusoro pavo; Ngavakandirwe mumoto; Nomumakomba akadzika, kuti varege kumukazve.</li>
      <li>Munhu, anamakuhwa, haangasimbiswi pasi; Zvakaipa zvichavhima munhu anomanikidza kuti zvimuparadze.</li>
      <li>Ndinoziva kuti Jehovha achagadzira mhosva yavanotambudzika, Nokururamisira vashaiwi.</li>
      <li>Zvirokwazvo, vakarurama vachavonga zita renyu; Vanemoyo yakarurama vachagara pamberi penyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Jehovha, ndakadana kwamuri; kurumidzai kuuya kwandiri; Teererai inzwi rangu kana ndichidana kwamuri.</li>
      <li>Munyengetero wangu ngauve pamberi penyu sezvinonhuwira; Nokusimudzwa kwamaoko angu sechipiriso chamadekwana.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, isai murindi pamberi pomuromo wangu; Chengetai mukova wemiromo yangu.</li>
      <li>Regai kurerekesa moyo wangu kuchinhu chakaipa, Kuti ndiite zvakaipa Pamwechete navanhu vanoita zvisina kururama.</li>
      <li>Akarurama ngaandirove netsitsi; Ngaandituke, ave mafuta pamusoro wangu; Musoro wangu haungaarambi; Nokuti ndicharamba ndichinyengetera pamusoro pokuipa kwavo.</li>
      <li>Vatongi vavo vakawisirwa kumawere edombo; Vachanzwa kuti mashoko angu akanaka.</li>
      <li>Sezvakaita pasi kana parimwa nokuparurwa, Saizvozvo mapfupa edu akaparadzirwa pamuromo weSheori.</li>
      <li>Nokuti meso angu anotarira kwamuri, Jehovha Ishe; Ndinovimba nemi; regai kudurura upenyu hwangu.</li>
      <li>Ndichengetei pamusungo wavakanditeyera, Naparugombe rwavanoita zvisina kururama.</li>
      <li>Vakaipa ngavabatwe nemimbure yavo vamene, Asi ini ndidarike hangu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndinodanidzira nenzwi rangu kuna Jehovha; Nenzwi rangu ndinonyengetera kuna Jehovha.</li>
      <li>Ndinodurura kuchema kwangu pamberi pake; Ndinomuzivisa kutambudzika kwangu.</li>
      <li>Panguva yokumanikidzwa kwomweya wangu mukati mangu, makaziva nzira yangu. Panzira yandinofamba nayo vakandivanzira musungo.</li>
      <li>Tarirai kurudyi rwangu, muone; nokuti hakuna munhu anondiziva; Ndashaiwa utiziro; hakuna munhu ane hanya nomweya wangu.</li>
      <li>Ndakadanidzira kwamuri, Jehovha; Ndakati, Ndimi utiziro hwangu, Nomugove wangu panyika yavapenyu.</li>
      <li>Teererai kudanidzira kwangu; nokuti ndinoshaiwa simba kwazvo; Ndirwirei panavanonditambudza; nokuti vanondikurira nesimba.</li>
      <li>Budisai mweya wangu patorongo, kuti ndivonge zita renyu; Vakarurama vachandipoteredza; Nokuti muchandiitira zvakanaka kwazvo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Inzwai munyengetero wangu, Jehovha; teererai kukumbira kwangu; Ndipindurei nokutendeka kwenyu nokururama kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Regai kutonga muranda wenyu; Nokuti hapana munhu mumwe mupenyu angaruramiswa pamberi penyu.</li>
      <li>Nokuti muvengi akatambudza mweya wangu; Akatsikirira upenyu hwangu pasi; Akandigarisa panzvimbo dzine rima, savanhu vakanguva vafa.</li>
      <li>Saka mweya wangu wavhunduswa mukati mangu. moyo wangu wavhunduswa mukati mangu.</li>
      <li>Ndinorangarira mazuva akare; Ndinofungisisa zvose zvamakaita; Ndinofunga basa ramaoko enyu.</li>
      <li>Ndinotambanudzira maoko angu kwamuri; Mweya wangu unokushuvai senyika yakaomerwa.</li>
      <li>Kurumidzai kupindura, Jehovha; mweya wangu waziya; Regai kundivanzira chiso chenyu; Ndigosava savanoburukira kugomba.</li>
      <li>Ndinzwisei unyoro hwenyu mangwanani; Nokuti ndinovimba nemi; Ndizivisei nzira yandinofanira kufamba nayo; Nokuti ndinosimudzira mweya wangu kwamuri.</li>
      <li>Ndirwirei Jehovha, panavavengi vangu; Ndinovanda nemi.</li>
      <li>Ndidzidzisei kuita kuda kwenyu; nokuti ndimi Mwari wangu; Mweya wenyu, wakanaka ngaundifambise munyika yakati chechetere,</li>
      <li>Ndiponesei Jehovha, nokuda kwezita renyu; Budisai mweya wangu pakumanikidzwa nokururama kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Pedzai vavengi vangu nounyoro hwenyu, Muparadze vose vanomanikidza mweya wangu; Nokuti ndiri muranda wenyu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ngaarumbidzwe Jehovha, dombo rangu, Anodzidzisa maoko angu kurwa, Neminwe yangu kufura;</li>
