      <li>Unyoro hwangu, nenhare yangu, Shongwe yangu yakakwirira, nomurwiri wangu; nhovo yangu, uye iye wandinovimba naye; Anoisa vanhu vangu pasi pangu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha, munhu chinyiko, zvamune hanya naye? Kana Mwanakomana womunhu, zvamunomurangarira?</li>
      <li>Munhu akafanana nomweya; Mazuva ake anenge mumvuri unopfuura.</li>
      <li>Kotamisa kudenga-denga kwenyu Jehovha, muburuke; Gunzvai makomo, apfungaire hutsi.</li>
      <li>Penyesai mheni, muvaparadze; Furai miseve yenyu, muvavhunduse.</li>
      <li>Tambanudzai ruoko rwenyu muri kumusoro; Ndisunungurei, mundirwire pamvura zhinji, Naparuoko rwavatorwa;</li>
      <li>Avo vanotaura zvisina maturo nomuromo wavo, Uye ruoko rwavo rworudyi ndirwo ruoko rworudyi rwenhema.</li>
      <li>Mwari ndichakuimbirai rwiyo rutsva; Ndichakuimbirai nziyo dzokurumbidza nomutengeranwa une ungiso dzine gumi.</li>
      <li>Ndimi munopa madzimambo kuponeswa, Munorwira Dhavhidhi muranda wenyu pamunondo unokuvadza.</li>
      <li>Ndisunungurei, mundirwire paruoko rwavatorwa, Vanotaura zvisina maturo nomuromo wavo, Uye ruoko rwavo rworudyi ndirwo ruoko rworudyi rwenhema.</li>
      <li>Vanakomana vedu vachava semiti yakakura kwazvo pautsva hwayo; Uye vanasikana vedu samabwe ekona akavezwa sezvinovezerwa imba yamambo;</li>
      <li>Matura edu achazara nezviyo zvamarudzi ose; Namakwai edu achabereka zviuru negumi rezviuru kumafuro edu.</li>
      <li>Nzombe dzedu dzichatakudzwa zvizhinji; Hatingaputsirwi madziro, kana kubuda kundorwa, Hakungavi nemhere inoridzwa panzira dzomumusha medu;</li>
      <li>Vanomufaro vanhu avo, vanoitirwa saizvozvo; Vanomufaro vanhu avo, Mwari wavo ari Jehovha.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndichakukudzai kwazvo, Mwari wangu, imi Mambo; Ndicharumbidza zita renyu nokusingaperi-peri.</li>
      <li>Ndichakurumbidzai zuva rimwe nerimwe; Ndichakudza zita renyu nokusingaperi-peri.</li>
      <li>Jehovha mukuru, anofanira kurumbidzwa kwazvo; Ukuru hwake haunganzverwi.</li>
      <li>Rudzi rumwe rucharumbidza mabasa enyu kuno rumwe, Vachadudzira zvamakaita zvine simba.</li>
      <li>Ndichafungisisa kubwinya kwoumambo hwenyu hunokudzwa, Namabasa enyu anoshamisa.</li>
      <li>Vanhu vachataura vachireva simba ramabasa enyu anotyisa; Neni ndichadudzira ukuru hwenyu.</li>
      <li>Vachareva vachiyeudzira kunaka kwenyu kukuru, Nokuimbira kururama kwenyu.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anenyasha, azere netsitsi, Haachimbidziki kutsamwa, anengoni zhinji.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anomoyo wakanaka kuna vose; Ngoni dzake dziri pamabasa ake ose.</li>
      <li>Mabasa enyu ose achakuvongai Jehovha; Navatsvene venyu vachakurumbidzai.</li>
      <li>Vachataura vachireva kubwinya kwoushe hwenyu, Nokuparidza simba renyu;</li>
      <li>Kuti vazivise vanakomana vavanhu mabasa ake anesimba, Nokubwinya kwoumambo hwoushe hwake.</li>
      <li>Ushe hwenyu ndihwo ushe husingaperi, Noumambo hwenyu huchagara nokusingaperi.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anotsigira vose vanowa, Anosimudza vose vakakotamiswa pasi.</li>
      <li>Meso avose anotarira kwamuri; Munovapa zvokudya zvavo panguva yakafanira.</li>
      <li>Munotadzanura ruoko rwenyu, Ndokugutisa zvipenyu zvose.</li>
      <li>Jehovha akarurama panzira dzake dzose, Anenyasha pazvose zvaanoita.</li>
      <li>Jehovha ari pedo navose vanodana kwaari, Vose vanodana kwaari nezvokwadi.</li>
      <li>Achaitira vanomutya sezvavanoda; Achanzwawo kudanidzira kwavo; ndokuvaponesa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anochengeta vose vanomuda Asi vakaipa achavaparadza vose.</li>
      <li>Muromo wangu uchataura kurumbidzwa kwaJehovha, Vanhu vose ngavarumbidze zita rake dzvene nokusingaperi-peri.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Rumbidzai Jehovha, iwe mweya wangu!</li>
      <li>Ndicharumbidza Jehovha ndichiri mupenyu; Ndichaimbira Mwari wangu nziyo dzokurumbidza, ini ndichiripo.</li>
      <li>Regai kuvimba namachinda, Kana noMwanakomana womunhu, asingagoni kubatsira.</li>
      <li>Mweya wake unobuda, iye ndokudzokera pasi pake; Nezuva iro mano ake anopera.</li>
      <li>Anomufaro munhu uyo kana Mwari waJakobho ari mubatsiri wake, Anotarira kuna Jehovha Mwari wake.</li>
      <li>Iye, akaita kudenga napasi, Negungwa, nezvose zviri mukati mazvo; Iye, anoramba akatendeka nokusingaperi;</li>
      <li>Anoruramisira vanomanikidzwa; Anopa vane nzara zvokudya; Jehovha anosunungura vasungwa;</li>
      <li>Jehovha anosvinudza meso amapofu; Jehovha anosimudza vakakotamiswa pasi; Jehovha anoda vakarurama;</li>
      <li>Jehovha anochengeta vatorwa; Jehovha anotsigira nherera nechirikadzi; Asi nzira yavakaipa anoipesanisa.</li>
      <li>Jehovha achabata ushe nokusingaperi, Mwari wako, iwe Ziyoni, kusvikira kumarudzi namarudzi. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya. Nokuti zvakanaka kuti Mwari wedu aimbirwe nziyo dzokurumbidza; Zvinofadza, uye kurumbidza kwakafanira.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anovaka Jerusaremu; Anounganidza vakadzingwa vaIsiraeri.</li>
      <li>Anoporesa vane moyo yakaputsika, Anosunga mavanga avo.</li>
      <li>Anotara kuwanda kwenyeredzi; Anodzipa dzose mazita adzo.</li>
      <li>Ishe wedu mukuru, anesimba guru; Njere dzake hadziperi.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anobatsira vanyoro;</li>
      <li>Imbirai Jehovha muchimuvonga, Imbirai Mwari wedu nziyo dzokurumbidza nembira;</li>
      <li>Iye anofukidza denga namakore, Anogadzirira pasi mvura, Anomeresa uswa pamakomo.</li>
      <li>Anopa zvipfuwo zvokudya zvazvo, Navana vamakunguvo, anochema.</li>
      <li>Haafadzwi nesimba rebhiza; Haafariri makumbo omurume.</li>
      <li>Jehovha anofara navanomutya, Navanotarira ngoni dzake.</li>
      <li>Rumbidza Jehovha, iwe Jerusaremu; Rumbidza Mwari wako, iwe Ziyoni.</li>
      <li>Nokuti wakasimbisa mazariro amasuo ako; Akaropafadza vana vako mukati mako.</li>
      <li>Anoisa rugare panyika yako; Anokugutisa nezviyo zvakaisvonaka.</li>
      <li>Anotuma mirairo yake panyika; Shoko rake rinomhanya kwazvo.</li>
      <li>Anopa vanhu chando samakushe amakwai, Anoparadzira chando samadota.</li>
      <li>Anokanda chimvuramabwe chake sezvimedu; Ndianiko angamira pachando chake?</li>
      <li>Anotuma shoko rake, ndokuzvinyausa; Anovhuvhutisa mhepo yake mvura ndokuyerera.</li>
      <li>Anozivisa Jakobho shoko rake, Nalsiraeri mitemo yake nezvaakatonga.</li>
      <li>Haana kutongoitira rumwe rudzi saizvozvo; Kana zviri zvaakatonga, havana kuzviziva. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Rumbidzai Jehovha, imi muri kudenga; Murumbidzei panzvimbo dzokumusoro.</li>
      <li>Murumbidzei imi vatumwa vake vose; Murumbidzei imi hondo dzake dzose.</li>
      <li>Murumbidzei imi zuva Murumbidzei imi nyeredzi dzose dzinovhenekera.</li>
      <li>Murumbidzei imi kudenga kwokudenga-denga, Newe mvura zhinji, iri kumusoro kwokudenga-denga.</li>
      <li>Ngazvirumbidze zita raJehovha; Nokuti iye akaraira, zvikasikwa.</li>
      <li>Akazvisimbisawo nokusingaperi-peri; Akatema chirevo chisingafaniri kudarikwa.</li>
      <li>Rumbidzai Jehovha imi vapasi, Imi zvikara zvegungwa, nezviri makadzika;</li>
      <li>Moto nechimvuramabwe, chando noutsi; Dutu guru, rinoita zvaakareva;</li>
      <li>Makomo nezvikomo zvose; Miti inobereka nemisidhari yose;</li>
      <li>Mhuka, nezvipfuwo zvose; Zvinokambaira neshiri dzinobhururuka;</li>
      <li>Madzimambo apasi nendudzi dzose dzavanhu; Machinda navatongi vose vapasi;</li>
      <li>Majaya nemhandara; Vatana navana;</li>
      <li>Ngavarumbidze zita raJehovha; Nokuti zita rake roga rakakurumbira; Umambo hwake huri kumusoro kwapasi nokudenga.</li>
      <li>Akasimudza runyanga rwavanhu vake, Kuti arumbidzwe navatsvene vake vose; Naivo vana vaIsiraeri, ivo vanhu vari pedo naye. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Imbirai Jehovha rwiyo rutsva, Nokurumbidzwa kwake paungano yavatsvene.</li>
      <li>Isiraeri ngaafarire kwazvo musiki wake; Vana veZiyoni ngavave nomufaro naMambo wavo.</li>
      <li>Ngavarumbidze zita rake vachimutambira; Ngavamuimbire nziyo dzokurumbidza nengoma nembira.</li>
      <li>Nokuti Jehovha anofarira vanhu vake; Achashongedza vanyoro noruponeso;</li>
      <li>Vatsvene ngavafare kwazvo nokukudziwa; Ngavaimbe nomufaro panhovo dzavo.</li>
      <li>Kurumbidza kukuru kwaMwari ngakuve pahuro dzavo, Nomunondo unocheka kwose paruoko rwavo;</li>
      <li>Kuti vatsive vahedheni; Varange ndudzi dzavanhu;</li>
      <li>Kuti vasunge madzimambo avo neketani, Navakuru vavo nezvisungo zvamatare.</li>
      <li>Kuti vavaitire zvavakatongerwa zvakanyorwa; Vatsvene vake vose vachakudzwa naizvozvi. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Hareruya! Rumbidzai Jehovha panzvimbo yake tsvene; Murumbidzei mudenga rakaitwa nesimba rake,</li>
      <li>Murumbidzei nokuda kwezvaakaita nesimba rake; Murumbidzei zvakafanira ukuru-kuru hwake.</li>
      <li>Murumbidzei nemitengeranwa nembira.</li>
      <li>Murumbidzei nengoma nokutamba; Murumbidzei nohudimbwa nenyere.</li>
      <li>Murumbidzei namakandira anorira kwazvo; Murumbidzei namakandira anorira zvakanaka.</li>
      <li>Zvinhu zvose zvinofema, ngazvirumbidze Jehovha. Hareruya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
</ol>
